\subsubsection[The Westminster Confession of Faith of 1647]{{The Westminster Confession of
Faith}


\index{Faith:saving ``f10!}\section{Chapter 1 -- Of the Holy Scripture}
\index{Scripture:holy ``f10!}1.1\ \ Although the light of nature and the works of creation\index{God's
attributes:creator:works of ``f10!} and providence\index{Providence:providence ``f10!} do so far manifest
the\index{Providence:manifests goodness of God ``f10!} goodness\index{God's attributes:goodness ``f10!}, wisdom, and
power\index{God's attributes:almighty power ``f10!} of God, as to leave men unexcusable\index{Unbelievers:unexcusable
``f10!};\footnote{\ Romans 2:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}4-15\index{45 Romans:ch.   2, v.  14-15, pg.
``f30!}; Romans 1:19-20\index{45 Romans:ch.   1, v.  19-20, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 19:1-3\index{19 Psalms:ch.  19, v.  
1-3, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 1:32\index{45 Romans:ch.   1, v.  32, pg. ``f30!} with Romans 2:1.} yet are they not
sufficient to\index{Covenant:OT ordinances:sufficient for that time ``f10!} give that knowledge of
God\index{Revelation:natural:not sufficient knowledge of God ``f10!} and of His will, which is necessary unto
salvation\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!}.\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 1:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  
1, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}1\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   1, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 2:13\index{46 1
Corinthians:ch.   2, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}{}-14\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   2, v.  13-14, pg. ``f30!}.} Therefore it
pleased\index{Providence:at God's pleasure ``f10!} the Lord, at sundry times, and in divers
manners\index{Revelation:sundry times and divers manners ``f10!}, to reveal Himself, and to declare
that\index{Revelation:special declaration ``f10!} His will unto His Church\index{Church:Christ's
``f10!};\footnote{\ Hebrews 1:1\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   1, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}.} and afterwards, for the better
preserving\index{Church:to preserve truth ``f10!} and propagating\index{Scripture:for propagating truth ``f10!} of the
truth, and\index{Oaths and Vows:assertion of truth ``f10!} for the more sure establishment\index{Scripture:for
establishment and comfort of Church ``f10!} and comfort of the Church against\index{Church:institution ``f10!} the
corruption of the\index{Sin:original:corrupt nature:flesh ``f10!} flesh, and the\index{flesh, sinful nature ``f10!}
malice of\index{Satan:malice of ``f10!} Satan and of\index{Satan:tempter ``f10!} the world, to commit the same wholly
unto writing:\index{Scripture:written ``f10!}\footnote{\ Proverbs 22:1\index{20 Proverbs:ch.  22, v.   1, pg.
``f30!}9-21\index{20 Proverbs:ch.  22, v.  19-21, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 1:3-4\index{42 Luke:ch.   1, v.   3-4, pg. ``f30!};
Romans 15:4\index{45 Romans:ch.  15, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 4:4\index{40 Matthew:ch.   4, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}, 7,
10\index{40 Matthew:ch.   4, v.   4, 7, 10, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 8:19-20\index{23 Isaiah:ch.   8, v.  19-20, pg.
``f30!}.} which makes the Holy Scripture\index{Scripture:holy ``f10!} to be most necessary;\footnote{\ 2 Timothy
3:15\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   3, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Peter 1:19\index{61 2 Peter:ch.   1, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}.}
those former ways of God's revealing His\index{Revelation:God's will ``f10!} will unto His people being now
ceased\index{Scripture:other forms of revelation have ceased ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Hebrews 1:1\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   1,
v.   1, pg. ``f30!}{}-2\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   1, v.   1-2, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip


1.2\ \ Under the name of Holy Scripture\index{Scripture:holy ``f10!}, or the Word of God\index{Scripture:word of
God:word of God ``f10!} written, are now contained all the books of the Old and New Testament\index{Scripture:New
Testament ``f10!}, which are these\index{Scripture:Old and New Testaments ``f10!}:


\bigskip

{\centering
\textit{Of the Old Testament}\index{Scripture:Old Testament ``f10!}\textit{:}
\par}

\begin{multicols}{3}

{\centering

\par}
\begin{multicols}{3}

\bigskip

All which are given by inspiration of\index{Scripture:inspired by God ``f10!} God, to be the rule of
faith\index{Faith:rule of ``f10!} and life.\footnote{\ Luke 16:29, 31\index{42 Luke:ch.  16, v.  29, 31, pg. ``f30!};
Ephesians 2:2\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}0\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.  20, pg. ``f30!};
Revelation 22:18-19\index{66 Revelation:ch.  22, v.  18-19, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Timothy 3:16\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   3, v. 
16, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

1.3\ \ The books commonly called Apocrypha\index{Apocrypha:not God breathed ``f10!}, not being of divine inspiration,
are no part of the canon\index{Scripture:canon ``f10!} of the Scripture; and\index{Scripture:Apocrypha not part of
canon ``f10!} therefore are of no authority in the Church of God\index{Church:God's ``f10!}, nor to be any otherwise
approved, or made use of, than other human writings\index{Apocrypha:human writings ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Luke 24:27,
44\index{42 Luke:ch.  24, v.  27, 44, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 3:2\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Peter
1:2\index{61 2 Peter:ch.   1, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}1\index{61 2 Peter:ch.   1, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

1.4\ \ The authority of the Holy Scripture\index{Scripture:holy ``f10!}, for which it ought to be believed
and\index{Scripture:to be:believed ``f10!} obeyed\index{Scripture:to be:obeyed:because word of God ``f10!}, depends not
upon the testimony\index{Scripture:authority not from testimony of any man ``f10!} of any man, or
Church\index{Church:institution ``f10!}; but wholly upon God (who is truth\index{God's attributes:truth ``f10!} itself)
the author thereof\index{Scripture:authored by God ``f10!}: and therefore it is to be received because it is the Word
of God\index{Scripture:word of God:word of God ``f10!}.\footnote{\ 2 Peter 1:19\index{61 2 Peter:ch.   1, v.  19, pg.
``f30!}, 21\index{61 2 Peter:ch.   1, v.  19, 21, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Timothy 3:16\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   3, v.  16, pg.
``f30!}; 1 John 5:9\index{62 1 John:ch.   5, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Thessalonians 2:13\index{52 1 Thessalonians:ch.  
2, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}.}

1.5\ \ We may be moved and induced by the testimony\index{Scripture:testimony of the Church ``f10!} of the Church
to\index{Church:institution ``f10!} a high and reverent\index{Scripture:to be:treated with reverent esteem ``f10!}
esteem of the\index{Scripture:to be:esteemed ``f10!} Holy Scripture\index{Scripture:holy ``f10!}.\footnote{\ 1 Timothy
3:1\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   3, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}5\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   3, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}.} And the
heavenliness\index{Scripture:heavenly matter ``f10!} of the matter, the efficacy\index{Scripture:efficacy of doctrine
``f10!} of the doctrine, the\index{Doctrine:of Scripture ``f10!} majesty of the\index{Scripture:majesty of the style
``f10!} style, the consent of all\index{Scripture:consent of all parts ``f10!} the parts, the scope of the whole (which
is, to give all glory\index{Scripture:gives glory to God ``f10!} to God), the full discovery\index{Scripture:makes full
discovery of the only way of salvation ``f10!} it makes of the only way of man's salvation\index{Salvation:belief in
Jesus by faith ``f10!}, the many other incomparable excellencies\index{Scripture:excellency ``f10!}, and the entire
perfection thereof\index{Scripture:perfection of ``f10!}, are arguments whereby it does abundantly evidence itself to
be the Word of God\index{Scripture:word of God:word of God ``f10!}: yet notwithstanding, our full
persuasion\index{Scripture:Holy Spirit persuades us that it is word of God ``f10!} and assurance of
the\index{Assurance:that God's word is true ``f10!} infallible truth\index{Scripture:infallible truth ``f10!} and
divine authority\index{Scripture:divine authority ``f10!} thereof, is from the inward\index{Scripture:witnessed
inwardly by Holy Spirit ``f10!} work of the Holy Spirit\index{Holy Spirit:Holy Spirit ``f10!} bearing witness
by\index{Scripture:witness to heart of man ``f10!} and with the Word in our hearts\index{Heart:new:through ministry of
Word ``f10!}.\footnote{\ 1 John 2:2\index{62 1 John:ch.   2, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}0, 27\index{62 1 John:ch.   2, v.  20,
27, pg. ``f30!}; John 16:13-14\index{43 John:ch.  16, v.  13-14, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 2:10, 11-12\index{46 1
Corinthians:ch.   2, v.  10, 11-12, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 59:2\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  59, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}1\index{23
Isaiah:ch.  59, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}.} 


\bigskip

1.6\ \ The whole counsel of God\index{Causation:God's own will ``f10!} concerning all things necessary for His own
glory\index{God's attributes:glory:his own ``f10!}, man's salvation\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!},
faith, and life, is either expressly set\index{Scripture:interpretation:some things expressly set down ``f10!} down in
Scripture, or by good and necessary consequence\index{Scripture:interpretation:deduced by good and necessary
consequence ``f10!} may be deduced from Scripture: unto which nothing at any time is to be added, whether by new
revelations\index{Revelation:new, not added to Scripture ``f10!} of the Spirit, or\index{Revelation:Word and Spirit
``f10!} traditions\index{Scripture:supersedes traditions of men ``f10!} of men.\footnote{\ 2 Timothy 3:15\index{55 2
Timothy:ch.   3, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}{}-17\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   3, v.  15-17, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 1:8-9\index{48
Galatians:ch.   1, v.   8-9, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Thessalonians 2:2\index{53 2 Thessalonians:ch.   2, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}.}
Nevertheless we acknowledge the inward illumination\index{Conversion:Holy Spirit:provides inner illumination ``f10!} of
the Spirit of God\index{Holy Spirit:God's Spirit ``f10!} to be necessary for the saving
understanding\index{Salvation:by working of Holy Spirit ``f10!} of such things as are revealed in the
Word:\index{Scripture:word of God:standard for:life ``f10!}\footnote{\ John 6:45\index{43 John:ch.   6, v.  45, pg.
``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 2:9-12\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   2, v.   9-12, pg. ``f30!}.} and that there are some
circumstances\index{Worship:circumstances ``f10!} concerning the worship of God, and\index{Worship:correct:instituted
by God ``f10!} government of\index{Church government:government ``f10!} the Church, common\index{Church:institution
``f10!} to human actions and societies\index{Scripture:interpretation:circumstances of societies ``f10!}, which are to
be ordered\index{Scripture:interpretation:by light of nature according rules of Word ``f10!} by the light of nature and
Christian prudence, according\index{Scripture:interpretation:by prudence according rules of Word ``f10!} to the general
rules of the Word, which are always to be observed\index{Scripture:interpretation:general rules to be observed
``f10!}.\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 11:13-14\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  13-14, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians
14:26\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  14, v.  26, pg. ``f30!}, 40\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  14, v.  26, 40, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

1.7\ \ All things in Scripture are not alike plain in\index{Scripture:not all parts plain in themselves ``f10!}
themselves, nor alike clear unto all:\footnote{\ 2 Peter 3:16\index{61 2 Peter:ch.   3, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}.} yet those
things which are necessary to be known, believed, and\index{Scripture:to be:believed ``f10!} observed for
salvation\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!}, are so clearly propounded\index{Scripture:what necessary to
know, clearly propounded ``f10!} and opened in some place of Scripture or\index{Scripture:interpretation:scripture with
scripture ``f10!} other, that not only the learned\index{Scripture:useful for learned and unlearned ``f10!}, but the
unlearned, in a due use of the ordinary means, may\index{Scripture:understandable:through ordinary means ``f10!} attain
unto a sufficient\index{Scripture:understandable:by unlearned ``f10!} understanding of them.\footnote{\ Psalm
119:105\index{19 Psalms:ch. 119, v. 105, pg. ``f30!}, 130\index{19 Psalms:ch. 119, v. 105, 130, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

1.8\ \ The Old Testament\index{Scripture:Old Testament ``f10!} in Hebrew\index{Scripture:Old Testament Hebrew ``f10!}
(which was the native language of the people of God of old), and the New Testament\index{Scripture:New Testament
``f10!} in Greek\index{Scripture:New Testament Greek ``f10!} (which, at the time of the writing
of\index{Scripture:written ``f10!} it was most generally known to the nations\index{Scripture:written in languages
known to nations ``f10!}), being immediately inspired\index{Scripture:inspired by God ``f10!} by God, and, by His
singular care and providence\index{Providence:providence ``f10!} kept pure in\index{Scripture:kept pure in all ages
``f10!} all ages, are therefore authentical\index{Scripture:original language:versions authentic
``f10!};\footnote{\ Matthew 5:18\index{40 Matthew:ch.   5, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}.} so as, in all
controversies\index{Scripture:determine all controversies ``f10!} of religion, the Church is\index{Church:institution
``f10!} finally to appeal unto them.\footnote{\ Isaiah 8:20\index{23 Isaiah:ch.   8, v.  20, pg. ``f30!} ,Acts
15:15\index{44 Acts:ch.  15, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}; John 5:39\index{43 John:ch.   5, v.  39, pg. ``f30!}, 46\index{43
John:ch.   5, v.  39, 46, pg. ``f30!}.} But, because these original tongues\index{Scripture:original language:not known
to all ``f10!} are not known to all the people of God, who have right unto, and interest in the\index{Scripture:all
people have interest (share) in ``f10!} Scriptures, and are commanded, in the\index{Scripture:to be:read and heard
``f10!} fear of\index{Fear:of God:reverence ``f10!} God, to read and search the\index{Heart:God alone able to search
``f10!}m\index{Scripture:to be:searched ``f10!},\footnote{\ John 5:39\index{43 John:ch.   5, v.  39, pg. ``f30!}.}
therefore they are to be translated\index{Scripture:to be:translated into common (vulgar) languages ``f10!} into the
vulgar language of every nation unto which they come,\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 14:6, 9, 11-12, 24, 27-28\index{46 1
Corinthians:ch.  14, v.   6, 9, 11-12, 24, 27-28, pg. ``f30!}.} that the Word of God\index{Scripture:word of God:word
of God ``f10!} dwelling plentifully in all, they may worship Him\index{Worship:acceptable manner ``f10!} in an
acceptable manner;\footnote{\ Colossians 3:16\index{51 Colossians:ch.   3, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}.} and, through patience
and comfort of the Scriptures\index{Scripture:comforts and builds up believers ``f10!}, may have
hope\index{Scripture:provides hope ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Romans 15:4\index{45 Romans:ch.  15, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

1.9\ \ The infallible\index{Scripture:interpretation:scripture with scripture ``f10!} rule of interpretation of
Scripture is the Scripture itself: and therefore, when there is a question about the true and full sense of any
Scripture (which is not manifold, but\index{Scripture:interpretation:not manifold, but on sense ``f10!} one), it must
be searched\index{Scripture:to be:searched ``f10!} and known by other places that speak more clearly.\footnote{\ 2
Peter 1:2\index{61 2 Peter:ch.   1, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}0-21\index{61 2 Peter:ch.   1, v.  20-21, pg. ``f30!}; Acts
15:15\index{44 Acts:ch.  15, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}{}-16\index{44 Acts:ch.  15, v.  15-16, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

1.10\ \ The supreme judge by\index{Scripture:supreme judge of controversies ``f10!} which all
controversies\index{Scripture:determine all controversies ``f10!} of religion are to be determined, and all
decrees\index{Church councils:decrees ``f10!} of councils\index{Church government:councils ``f10!}, opinions
of\index{Scripture:final authority, not opinions of ancient writers ``f10!} ancient writers,
doctrines\index{Doctrine:false:of men ``f10!} of men, and private spirits, are to be examined\index{Scripture:to
be:used to examine all doctrines ``f10!}; and in whose sentence we are to rest; can be no other but the Holy
Spirit\index{Holy Spirit:Holy Spirit ``f10!} speaking in the Scripture\index{Scripture:word of God:Holy Spirit speaking
``f10!}.\footnote{\ Matthew 22:29, 31\index{40 Matthew:ch.  22, v.  29, 31, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 2:2\index{49
Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}0\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.  20, pg. ``f30!} with Acts 28:25\index{44
Acts:ch.  28, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}.}

\section{Chapter 2 -- Of God, and of the Holy Trinity}
\index{God's attributes:trinity:one substance ``f10!}2.1\ \ There is but one only,\footnote{\ Deuteronomy 6:4\index{05
Deuteronomy:ch.   6, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 8:4, 6\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   8, v.   4, 6, pg. ``f30!}.}
living, and true God:\footnote{\ 1 Thessalonians 1:9\index{52 1 Thessalonians:ch.   1, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}; Jeremiah
10:10\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  10, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}.} who is infinite\index{God's attributes:infinite:knowledge
``f10!} in being and perfection\index{God's attributes:perfect blessedness ``f10!},\footnote{\ Job 11:7-9\index{18
Job:ch.  11, v.   7-9, pg. ``f30!}; Job 26:14\index{18 Job:ch.  26, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}.} a most pure\index{God's
attributes:a spirit, most pure ``f10!} spirit,\footnote{\ John 4:24\index{43 John:ch.   4, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}.}
invisible,\footnote{\ 1 Timothy 1:17\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   1, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}.} without body,
parts,\footnote{\ Deuteronomy 4:15-16\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.   4, v.  15-16, pg. ``f30!}; John 4:24\index{43 John:ch.
  4, v.  24, pg. ``f30!} with Luke 24:39\index{42 Luke:ch.  24, v.  39, pg. ``f30!}.} or passions\index{God's
attributes:no passions ``f10!},\footnote{\ Acts 14:11, 15\index{44 Acts:ch.  14, v.  11, 15, pg. ``f30!}.}
immutable\index{God's attributes:immutable ``f10!},\footnote{\ James 1:17\index{59 James:ch.   1, v.  17, pg. ``f30!};
Malachi 3:6\index{39 Malachi:ch.   3, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}.} immense\index{God's attributes:immense
``f10!},\footnote{\ 1 Kings 8:27\index{11 1 Kings:ch.   8, v.  27, pg. ``f30!}; Jeremiah 23:23-24\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.
 23, v.  23-24, pg. ``f30!}.} eternal,\index{God's attributes:eternal ``f10!}\footnote{\ Psalm 90:2\index{19 Psalms:ch.
 90, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Timothy 1:17\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   1, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}.} incomprehensible\index{God's
attributes:incomprehensible ``f10!},\footnote{\ Psalm 145:3\index{19 Psalms:ch. 145, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}.}
almighty\index{God's attributes:almighty power ``f10!},\footnote{\ Genesis 17:1\index{01 Genesis:ch.  17, v.   1, pg.
``f30!}; Revelation 4:8\index{66 Revelation:ch.   4, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}.} most wise\index{God's attributes:wisdom
``f10!},\footnote{\index{45 Romans:ch.  16, v.   2, pg.
``f30!} most
holy\index{God's attributes:holy:most ``f10!},\footnote{\index{23 Isaiah:ch.   6,
v.   3, pg. ``f30!}\index{66 Revelation:ch.   4, v.   8, pg.
``f30!}\index{19 Psalms:ch.
115, v.   3, pg. ``f30!} most absolute\index{God's attributes:absolute
``f10!},\footnote{\index{02 Exodus:ch.   3, v.  14, pg.
``f30!} things
according to the counsel of His\index{Causation:God's own will ``f10!} own immutable and most righteous
will\index{God's attributes:righteousness ``f10!},\footnote{\ Ephesians 1:1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   1, pg.
``f30!}1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}.} for His own glory\index{God's attributes:glory:his own
``f10!};\footnote{\ Proverbs 16:4\index{20 Proverbs:ch.  16, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 11:36\index{45 Romans:ch.  11,
v.  36, pg. ``f30!}.} most loving\index{God's attributes:love ``f10!},\footnote{\ 1 John 4:8, 16\index{62 1 John:ch.  
4, v.   8, 16, pg. ``f30!}.} gracious\index{Grace:God's free ``f10!}, merciful\index{God's attributes:merciful ``f10!},
long-suffering\index{God's attributes:long-suffering ``f10!}, abundant in goodness\index{God's attributes:goodness
``f10!} and truth\index{God's attributes:truth ``f10!}, forgiving iniquity\index{God's attributes:forgiving iniquity
``f10!}, transgression, and\index{God's law:commandments:transgressions ``f10!} sin;\footnote{\ Exodus 34:6\index{02
Exodus:ch.  34, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}{}-7\index{02 Exodus:ch.  34, v.   6-7, pg. ``f30!}.} the
rewarder\index{Believers:rewarded by God ``f10!} of them that diligently seek\index{Salvation:for those who diligently
seek God ``f10!} Him;\footnote{\ Hebrews 11:6\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  11, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}.} and withal, most just and
terrible\index{Judgement:just and terrible ``f10!} in His judgments\index{God's attributes:judge
``f10!},\footnote{\ Nehemiah 9:32-33\index{16 Nehemiah:ch.   9, v.  32-33, pg. ``f30!}.} hating\index{God's
attributes:hates sin ``f10!} all sin,\footnote{\ Psalm 5:5-6\index{19 Psalms:ch.   5, v.   5-6, pg. ``f30!}.} and who
will by no means clear the guilty\index{guilt ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Nahum 1:2-3\index{34 Nahum:ch.   1, v.   2-3, pg.
``f30!}; Exodus 34:7\index{02 Exodus:ch.  34, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}.} 


\bigskip

2.2\ \ God has all life\index{God's attributes:glory:his own ``f10!},\footnote{\ John 5:26\index{43 John:ch.   5, v. 
26, pg. ``f30!}.} glory,\footnote{\ Acts 7:2\index{44 Acts:ch.   7, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}.} goodness\index{God's
attributes:goodness ``f10!},\footnote{\ Psalm 119:68\index{19 Psalms:ch. 119, v.  68, pg. ``f30!}.}
blessedness,\index{God's attributes:perfect blessedness ``f10!}\footnote{\ 1 Timothy 6:1\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   6, v.
  1, pg. ``f30!}5\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   6, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 9:5\index{45 Romans:ch.   9, v.   5, pg.
``f30!}.} in and of Himself; and is alone in and unto Himself all-sufficient\index{God's attributes:all-sufficient
``f10!}, not standing in need of any creatures\index{creatures ``f10!} which He has made,\footnote{\ Acts
17:24\index{44 Acts:ch.  17, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}{}-25\index{44 Acts:ch.  17, v.  24-25, pg. ``f30!}.} nor
deriving\index{God's attributes:glory:not derived from creatures ``f10!} any glory from them,\footnote{\ Job
22:2-3\index{18 Job:ch.  22, v.   2-3, pg. ``f30!}.} but only manifesting\index{God's attributes:glory:manifested
``f10!} His own glory in, by, unto, and upon them: He is the alone fountain\index{God's attributes:creator:fountain of
existence ``f10!} of all being, of whom, through whom, and to whom are all things;\footnote{\ Rom 11:36\index{45
Romans:ch.  11, v.  36, pg. ``f30!}.} and has most sovereign\index{God's attributes:sovereign lordship ``f10!} dominion
over the\index{Mankind:dominion over creation ``f10!}m\index{God's attributes:sovereign dominion ``f10!}, to do by
them, for them, or upon them whatsoever Himself pleases\index{Providence:at God's pleasure
``f10!}.\footnote{\ Revelation 4:11\index{66 Revelation:ch.   4, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Timothy 6:1\index{54 1
Timothy:ch.   6, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}5\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   6, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}; Daniel 4:25, 35\index{27
Daniel:ch.   4, v.  25, 35, pg. ``f30!}.} In His sight all things are open and manifest;\footnote{\ Hebrews
4:13\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   4, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}.} His knowledge\index{God's attributes:omniscience ``f10!} is

creature,\footnote{\ Romans 11:33\index{45 Romans:ch.  11, v.  33, pg. ``f30!}{}-34\index{45 Romans:ch.  11, v.  33-34,
pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 147:5\index{19 Psalms:ch. 147, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.} so as nothing is to Him
contingent\index{Causation:no contingency with God ``f10!}, or uncertain.\footnote{\ Acts 15:18\index{44 Acts:ch.  15,
v.  18, pg. ``f30!}; Ezekiel 11:5\index{26 Ezekiel:ch.  11, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.} He is most holy\index{God's
attributes:holy:most ``f10!} in all His counsels\index{God's attributes:holy:counsels ``f10!}, in all His
works\index{Providence:God's works ``f10!}, and in all His commands\index{God's law:commandments:ten
``f10!}.\footnote{\ Psalm 145:17\index{19 Psalms:ch. 145, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 7:12\index{45 Romans:ch.   7, v. 
12, pg. ``f30!}.} To Him is due from angels\index{Angels:angels ``f10!} and men, and every other creature, whatsoever
worship\index{Worship:of God ``f10!}, service, or obedience\index{God's law:commandments:obedience:required ``f10!} He
is pleased to require of them.\footnote{\ Revelation 5:12-14\index{66 Revelation:ch.   5, v.  12-14, pg. ``f30!}.} 


\bigskip

2.3\ \ In the unity\index{God's attributes:unity of persons ``f10!} of the Godhead\index{God's attributes:Godhead
``f10!} there be three persons\index{God's attributes:trinity:three persons ``f10!}, of one substance\index{God's

\section{Chapter 3 -- Of God's Eternal Decree}
\index{Predestination:eternal decrees ``f10!}3.1\ \ God from all eternity\index{God's attributes:eternal ``f10!} did, by
the most wise\index{God's attributes:wisdom ``f10!} and holy counsel of His\index{Causation:God's own will ``f10!} own
will, freely, and unchangeably ordain whatsoever\index{Predestination:all that happens ``f10!} comes to
pass:\footnote{\ Ephesians 1:1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.  11, pg.
``f30!}; Romans 11:33\index{45 Romans:ch.  11, v.  33, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 6:17\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   6, v.  17, pg.
``f30!}; Romans 9:15, 18\index{45 Romans:ch.   9, v.  15, 18, pg. ``f30!}.} yet so, as thereby neither is God the
author\index{Sin:God not author or approver of ``f10!} of sin,\footnote{\ James 1:13, 17\index{59 James:ch.   1, v. 
13, 17, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 1:5\index{62 1 John:ch.   1, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.} nor is violence\index{Causation:will of
creatures:not destroyed by predestination ``f10!} offered to the will of the creatures\index{creatures ``f10!}, nor is
the liberty or\index{Liberty:natural ``f10!} contingency\index{Causation:contingency ``f10!} of second
causes\index{Causation:second causes ``f10!} taken away, but rather established.\footnote{\ Acts 2:23\index{44 Acts:ch.
  2, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 17:12\index{40 Matthew:ch.  17, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 4:27-28\index{44 Acts:ch.  
4, v.  27-28, pg. ``f30!}; John 19:11\index{43 John:ch.  19, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}; Proverbs 16:33\index{20 Proverbs:ch. 
16, v.  33, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

3.2\ \ Although God knows whatsoever\index{God's attributes:omniscience ``f10!} may or can come to pass upon all
supposed conditions\index{Predestination:not conditional ``f10!},\footnote{\ Acts 15:18\index{44 Acts:ch.  15, v.  18,
pg. ``f30!}; 1 Samuel 23:11-12\index{09 1 Samuel:ch.  23, v.  11-12, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 11:21, 23\index{40
Matthew:ch.  11, v.  21, 23, pg. ``f30!}.} yet has He not decreed\index{Predestination:eternal decrees ``f10!} anything

would come to pass upon such conditions.\footnote{\ Romans 9:11\index{45 Romans:ch.   9, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}, 13,

\bigskip

attributes:glory:his own ``f10!}, some men and angels\index{Angels:angels ``f10!}\footnote{\ 1 Timothy 5:21\index{54 1
Timothy:ch.   5, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 25:41\index{40 Matthew:ch.  25, v.  41, pg. ``f30!}.} are

``f10!}.\footnote{\ Romans 9:22, 23\index{45 Romans:ch.   9, v.  22, 23, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 1:5\index{49

Proverbs:ch.  16, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

3.4\ \ These angels\index{Angels:angels ``f10!} and men, thus predestinated\index{Predestination:predestination ``f10!},
and fore-ordained\index{Predestination:fore-ordination ``f10!}, are particularly and unchangeably
designed\index{Angels:unchangeably designed ``f10!}, and their number so certain and definite\index{Angels:definite

\section{Chapter 4 -- Of Creation}
4.1\ \ It pleased\index{Providence:at God's pleasure ``f10!} God the Father\index{Father:God the ``f10!},
Son\index{Jesus:Son of God ``f10!}, and Holy Ghost\index{Holy Spirit:Holy Ghost ``f10!},\footnote{\ Hebrews
1:2\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   1, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; John 1:2-3\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.   2-3, pg. ``f30!}; Genesis
1:2\index{01 Genesis:ch.   1, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; Job 26:13\index{18 Job:ch.  26, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; Job
33:4\index{18 Job:ch.  33, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.} for the manifestation of the glory of His\index{God's
attributes:glory:his own ``f10!} eternal power\index{God's attributes:eternal power ``f10!}, wisdom, and
goodness\index{God's attributes:goodness ``f10!},\footnote{\ Romans 1:20\index{45 Romans:ch.   1, v.  20, pg. ``f30!};
Jeremiah 10:12\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  10, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 104:24\index{19 Psalms:ch. 104, v.  24, pg.
``f30!}; Psalm 33:5-6\index{19 Psalms:ch.  33, v.   5-6, pg. ``f30!}.} in the beginning, to create, or\index{God's
attributes:creator:from nothing ``f10!} make of nothing, the world, and all things therein whether visible
or\index{God's attributes:creator:of visible or invisible ``f10!} invisible, in\index{Creation:visible and invisible
``f10!} the space of six\index{Creation:in six days ``f10!} days; and all very good.\footnote{\ Genesis 1 chap. Hebrews
11:3\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  11, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}; Colossians 1:16\index{51 Colossians:ch.   1, v.  16, pg. ``f30!};
Acts 17:24\index{44 Acts:ch.  17, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}.}\textsuperscript{,} \footnote{\ \textcolor{black}{Refer to the
}\textit{\textcolor{black}{Statement Concerning Subscription
}}\textcolor{black}{(}\textit{\textcolor{black}{Subscription Clarifications}}\textcolor{black}{).}}


\bigskip

4.2\ \ After God\index{Mankind:created:attributes ``f10!} had made all other creatures\index{creatures ``f10!}, He
created man\index{Mankind:created:by God ``f10!}, male\index{Mankind:male and female ``f10!} and
female\index{Mankind:created:male and female ``f10!},\footnote{\ Genesis 1:2\index{01 Genesis:ch.   1, v.   2, pg.
``f30!}7\index{01 Genesis:ch.   1, v.  27, pg. ``f30!}.} with reasonable\index{Mankind:created:reasonable soul ``f10!}
and immortal\index{Mankind:immortal soul ``f10!} souls,\footnote{\ Genesis 2:7\index{01 Genesis:ch.   2, v.   7, pg.
``f30!} with Ecclesiastes 12:7\index{21 Ecclesiastes:ch.  12, v.   7, pg. ``f30!} \& Luke 23:43\index{42 Luke:ch.  23,
v.  43, pg. ``f30!} and Matthew 10:28\index{40 Matthew:ch.  10, v.  28, pg. ``f30!}.} endued with
knowledge\index{Mankind:created:with knowledge, righteousness, and holiness ``f10!}, righteousness, and true
holiness\index{Mankind:created:holy ``f10!}, after His own image\index{Mankind:image of God ``f10!};\footnote{\ Genesis
1:2\index{01 Genesis:ch.   1, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}6\index{01 Genesis:ch.   1, v.  26, pg. ``f30!}; Colossians
3:10\index{51 Colossians:ch.   3, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 4:24\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}.}
having the law of God written in their hearts\index{God's law:written on man's heart ``f10!},\footnote{\ Romans
2:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}4-15\index{45 Romans:ch.   2, v.  14-15, pg. ``f30!}.} and power to
fulfil it\index{Covenant:works:conditional on perfect obedience ``f10!}:\footnote{\ Ecclesiastes 7:2\index{21
Ecclesiastes:ch.   7, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}9\index{21 Ecclesiastes:ch.   7, v.  29, pg. ``f30!}.} and yet under a
possibility of transgressing\index{Mankind:created:with possibility of transgressing ``f10!}, being left to the liberty
of their\index{Liberty:of own will ``f10!} own will, which was subject unto change.\footnote{\ Genesis 3:6\index{01
Genesis:ch.   3, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; Ecclesiastes 7:2\index{21 Ecclesiastes:ch.   7, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}9\index{21
Ecclesiastes:ch.   7, v.  29, pg. ``f30!}.} Beside this law written in their hearts, they received a command,
not\index{God's law:commandments:given to Adam ``f10!} to eat of the tree of the\index{Tree:of the knowledge of good

communion with God\index{Communion:with God ``f10!},\footnote{\ Genesis 2:17\index{01 Genesis:ch.   2, v.  17, pg.
``f30!}; Genesis 3:8\index{01 Genesis:ch.   3, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}{}-11, 23\index{01 Genesis:ch.   3, v.   8-11, 23,
pg. ``f30!}.} and had dominion over the\index{Mankind:dominion over creation ``f10!} creatures.\footnote{\ Genesis
1:2\index{01 Genesis:ch.   1, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}6\index{01 Genesis:ch.   1, v.  26, pg. ``f30!}, 28\index{01
Genesis:ch.   1, v.  26, 28, pg. ``f30!}.}

\section{Chapter 5 -- Of Providence}
\index{Providence:providence ``f10!}5.1\ \ God the great Creator\index{God's attributes:creator:of all things ``f10!} of
all things does uphold\index{Providence:upholds all creatures ``f10!},\footnote{\ Hebrews 1:3\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   1,
v.   3, pg. ``f30!}.} direct, dispose, and\index{Providence:God disposes all things for his glory ``f10!}
govern\index{Providence:governing all ``f10!} all creatures\index{creatures ``f10!}, actions, and
things,\footnote{\ Daniel 4:34-35\index{27 Daniel:ch.   4, v.  34-35, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 135:6\index{19 Psalms:ch. 135,
v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 17:25\index{44 Acts:ch.  17, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}{}-26, 28\index{44 Acts:ch.  17, v.  25-26,
28, pg. ``f30!}; Job 38 to 41 chapters.} from the greatest even to the least,\footnote{\ Matthew 10:29, 30-31\index{40
Matthew:ch.  10, v.  29, 30-31, pg. ``f30!}.} by His most wise\index{God's attributes:wisdom ``f10!} and holy
providence\index{Providence:providence ``f10!},\footnote{\ Proverbs 15:3\index{20 Proverbs:ch.  15, v.   3, pg.
``f30!}; Psalm 104:24\index{19 Psalms:ch. 104, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 145:17\index{19 Psalms:ch. 145, v.  17, pg.
``f30!}.} according to His infallible\index{God's attributes:infallible fore-knowledge ``f10!}
fore-knowledge\index{God's attributes:foreknowledge ``f10!},\footnote{\ Acts 15:18\index{44 Acts:ch.  15, v.  18, pg.
``f30!}; Psalm 94:8, 11\index{19 Psalms:ch.  94, v.   8, 11, pg. ``f30!}.} and the free and immutable\index{God's
attributes:immutable ``f10!} counsel of His\index{Causation:God's own will ``f10!} own will,\footnote{\ Ephesians
1:1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm
33:10-11\index{19 Psalms:ch.  33, v.  10-11, pg. ``f30!}.} to the praise of the\index{Worship:praising God ``f10!}
glory of His\index{God's attributes:glory:his own ``f10!} wisdom, power\index{God's attributes:listed (definition of
God) ``f10!}, justice, goodness\index{God's attributes:goodness ``f10!}, and mercy.\footnote{\ Isaiah 63:14\index{23
Isaiah:ch.  63, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 3:10\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   3, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; Romans
9:17\index{45 Romans:ch.   9, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; Genesis 45:7\index{01 Genesis:ch.  45, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm
145:7\index{19 Psalms:ch. 145, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

5.2\ \ Although, in relation to the\index{Causation:relation to fore-knowledge ``f10!} fore-knowledge\index{God's
attributes:foreknowledge ``f10!} and decree\index{Predestination:eternal decrees ``f10!} of God, the first
Cause\index{Causation:first cause ``f10!}, all things come to pass immutably\index{God's attributes:immutable ``f10!},
and infallibly\index{Providence:infallible ``f10!}:\footnote{\ Acts 2:23\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}.}
yet, by the same providence\index{Providence:providence ``f10!}, He orders them to fall out, according to the nature of
second causes\index{Causation:second causes ``f10!}, either necessarily, freely, or\index{Causation:God's own will
``f10!} contingently\index{Causation:no contingency with God ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Genesis 8:22\index{01 Genesis:ch.   8,
v.  22, pg. ``f30!}; Jeremiah 31:3\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  31, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}5\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  31, v.  35,
pg. ``f30!}; Exodus 21:13\index{02 Exodus:ch.  21, v.  13, pg. ``f30!} with Deuteronomy 19:5\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch. 
19, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Kings 22:28, 34\index{11 1 Kings:ch.  22, v.  28, 34, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 10:6-7\index{23
Isaiah:ch.  10, v.   6-7, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

5.3\ \ God in His ordinary\index{Providence:ordinary means not binding on God ``f10!}
providence\index{Providence:providence ``f10!} makes use of means,\footnote{\ Acts 27:31, 44\index{44 Acts:ch.  27, v. 
31, 44, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 55:1\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  55, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}0-11\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  55, v.  10-11,

without,\footnote{\ Hosea 1:7\index{28 Hosea:ch.   1, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 4:4\index{40 Matthew:ch.   4, v.  
4, pg. ``f30!}; Job 34:20\index{18 Job:ch.  34, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}.} above,\footnote{\ Romans 4:19-21\index{45
Romans:ch.   4, v.  19-21, pg. ``f30!}.} and against them at His pleasure\index{Providence:at God's pleasure
``f10!}.\footnote{\ 2 Kings 6:6\index{12 2 Kings:ch.   6, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; Daniel 3:27\index{27 Daniel:ch.   3, v. 
27, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

5.4\ \ The almighty\index{God's attributes:almighty power ``f10!} power, unsearchable\index{Providence:unsearchable wise
counsel ``f10!} wisdom, and infinite\index{God's attributes:infinite:goodness ``f10!} goodness\index{God's
attributes:goodness ``f10!} of God so far manifest themselves in\index{Providence:manifests goodness of God ``f10!} His
providence\index{Providence:providence ``f10!}, that it extends itself\index{Providence:extends even to first sin
``f10!} even to the first fall\index{Sin:original:first transgression (of Adam) ``f10!}, and all other sins of
angels\index{Angels:angels ``f10!} and men;\footnote{\ Romans 11:32\index{45 Romans:ch.  11, v.  32, pg.
``f30!}{}-34\index{45 Romans:ch.  11, v.  32-34, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Samuel 24:1\index{10 2 Samuel:ch.  24, v.   1, pg.
``f30!} with 1 Chronicles 21:1\index{13 1 Chronicles:ch.  21, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Kings 22:22-23\index{11 1
Kings:ch.  22, v.  22-23, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Chronicles 10:4, 13-14\index{13 1 Chronicles:ch.  10, v.   4, 13-14, pg.
``f30!}; 2 Samuel 16:10\index{10 2 Samuel:ch.  16, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 2:23\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  23, pg.
``f30!}; Acts 4:27-28\index{44 Acts:ch.   4, v.  27-28, pg. ``f30!}.} and that not by a bare permission\index{Sin:God
purposes and permits for his own glory ``f10!},\footnote{\ Acts 14:16\index{44 Acts:ch.  14, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}.} but
such as has joined with it a most wise\index{God's attributes:wisdom ``f10!} and powerful
bounding\index{Providence:governing all ``f10!},\footnote{\ Psalm 76:10\index{19 Psalms:ch.  76, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; 2

things for his glory and believers' good ``f10!} governing of them, in a manifold dispensation\index{Providence:God's
dispensation ``f10!}, to His own holy\index{God's attributes:holy:ends ``f10!} ends;\footnote{\ Genesis 50:20\index{01
Genesis:ch.  50, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 10:6-7\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  10, v.   6-7, pg. ``f30!}, 12\index{23
Isaiah:ch.  10, v.   6-7, 12, pg. ``f30!}.} yet so, as the sinfulness thereof proceeded only\index{Sin:proceeds only
from man, not God ``f10!} from the creature\index{creatures ``f10!}, and not from God, who, being most holy\index{God's
attributes:holy:most ``f10!} and righteous, neither\index{God's attributes:righteousness ``f10!} is, nor can be, the
author or approver\index{Sin:God not author or approver of ``f10!} of sin.\footnote{\ James 1:13-14, 17\index{59
James:ch.   1, v.  13-14, 17, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 2:16\index{62 1 John:ch.   2, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm
50:21\index{19 Psalms:ch.  50, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}.}

5.5\ \ The most wise\index{God's attributes:wisdom ``f10!}, righteous, and gracious\index{Grace:God's free ``f10!} God
does oftentimes leave for a season His\index{Temptation:left by God for a season ``f10!} own children to manifold

``f10!}ir\index{Sin:original:corrupt nature:hearts ``f10!} own hearts\index{Heart:corrupt ``f10!}, to
chastise\index{Believers:chastened by God ``f10!} them for their former sins, or to discover\index{Temptation:exposes

``f10!} of their hearts, that\index{Heart:deceitful ``f10!} they may be humbled\index{Humility:before God

``f30!}; Mark 14:66 to the end, with John 21:15-17\index{43 John:ch.  21, v.  15-17, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

5.6\ \ As for those wicked\index{blindness, spiritual ``f10!} and ungodly\index{Unbelievers:ungodly ``f10!} men whom

``f30!}; Romans 11:7\index{45 Romans:ch.  11, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}{}-8\index{45 Romans:ch.  11, v.   7-8, pg. ``f30!}.}
from them He not only withholds\index{Providence:God withholds mercy, grace, favour as he wills ``f10!} His grace,

Spirit ``f10!} in their hearts;\index{Heart:new:enlightened ``f10!}\footnote{\ Deuteronomy 29:4\index{05
Deuteronomy:ch.  29, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.} but sometimes also withdraws\index{Punishment:God withdraws gifts ``f10!}

Deuteronomy:ch.   2, v.  30, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Kings 8:12-13\index{12 2 Kings:ch.   8, v.  12-13, pg. ``f30!}.} and,
withal, gives them over to their own lusts\index{Sexual immorality:lust ``f10!}, the
temptations\index{Temptation:temptation ``f10!} of the world, and the power of Satan\index{Satan:power of
``f10!}:\footnote{\ Psalm 81:11\index{19 Psalms:ch.  81, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}{}-12\index{19 Psalms:ch.  81, v.  11-12,
pg. ``f30!}; 2 Thessalonians 2:10\index{53 2 Thessalonians:ch.   2, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}{}-12\index{53 2
Thessalonians:ch.   2, v.  10-12, pg. ``f30!}.} whereby it comes to pass that they harden themselves, even under those

others.\footnote{\ Exodus 7:3\index{02 Exodus:ch.   7, v.   3, pg. ``f30!} with Exodus 8:15, 32\index{02 Exodus:ch.

``f30!}.}


\bigskip

creatures\index{creatures ``f10!}, so after a most special manner, it takes care of His Church\index{Church:Christ's
``f10!}, and disposes\index{Providence:God disposes all for good of his Church ``f10!} all things to the good
thereof.\footnote{\ 1 Timothy 4:1\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   4, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}0\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   4, v.  10,

``f30!}.}

\paragraph[Chapter 6 {}-- Of the Fall of Man, of Sin, and of the Punishment thereof]{Chapter 6 -- Of the Fall of Man, of
Sin, and of the Punishment thereof}
\index{Sin:original:first transgression (of Adam) ``f10!}\index{Punishment:of sin ``f10!}6.1\ \ Our first
parents\index{Parents:first, sinned against God ``f10!}, being seduced\index{Temptation:Satan's seduction of our first
parents ``f10!} by the subtilty\index{Satan:tempter ``f10!} and temptation\index{Temptation:temptation ``f10!} of
Satan, sinned, in eating the forbidden\index{Sin:original:first transgression (of Adam) ``f10!}
fruit.\footnote{\ Genesis 3:13\index{01 Genesis:ch.   3, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Corinthians 11:3\index{47 2
Corinthians:ch.  11, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}.} This their sin God was pleased\index{Providence:at God's pleasure ``f10!},
according to His wise\index{God's attributes:wisdom ``f10!} and holy counsel, to\index{Causation:God's own will ``f10!}
permit\index{Sin:God purposes and permits for his own glory ``f10!}, having purposed to order it to His own
glory\index{God's attributes:glory:his own ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Romans 11:32\index{45 Romans:ch.  11, v.  32, pg.
``f30!}.}


\bigskip

6.2\ \ By this sin they fell\index{Sin:original:all mankind descending from Adam ``f10!} from their original
righteousness and\index{Mankind:created:original righteousness ``f10!} communion, with\index{Communion:with God ``f10!}
God,\footnote{\ Genesis 3:6\index{01 Genesis:ch.   3, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}{}-8\index{01 Genesis:ch.   3, v.   6-8, pg.
``f30!}; Ecclesiastes 7:2\index{21 Ecclesiastes:ch.   7, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}9\index{21 Ecclesiastes:ch.   7, v.  29,
pg. ``f30!}; Romans 3:2\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}3\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}.}
and so became dead\index{Death:spiritual, in sin ``f10!} in sin,\footnote{\ Genesis 2:17\index{01 Genesis:ch.   2, v. 
17, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 2:1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}.} and wholly defiled in
all\index{Sin:original:corrupt nature:defiled in all parts and faculties ``f10!} the parts and faculties of
soul\index{Sin:original:corrupt nature:faculties of the soul ``f10!} and body.\footnote{\ Titus 1:15\index{56 Titus:ch.
  1, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}; Genesis 6:5\index{01 Genesis:ch.   6, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}; Jeremiah 17:9\index{24
Jeremiah:ch.  17, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 3:10\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}{}-19\index{45
Romans:ch.   3, v.  10-19, pg. ``f30!}.}

6.3\ \ They being the root\index{Sin:original:first transgression (of Adam) ``f10!} of all mankind,
the\index{Sin:original:all mankind descending from Adam ``f10!} guilt\index{guilt ``f10!} of this sin was
imputed,\index{Imputation:of Adam's sin ``f10!}\footnote{\ Genesis 1:2\index{01 Genesis:ch.   1, v.   2, pg.
``f30!}7\index{01 Genesis:ch.   1, v.  27, pg. ``f30!}{}-28\index{01 Genesis:ch.   1, v.  27-28, pg. ``f30!} and
Genesis 2:16-17\index{01 Genesis:ch.   2, v.  16-17, pg. ``f30!} and Acts 17:26\index{44 Acts:ch.  17, v.  26, pg.
``f30!} with Romans 5:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}2\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.  12, pg. ``f30!},
15-19\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.  12, 15-19, pg. ``f30!} and 1 Corinthians 15:21-22\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  15, v.
 21-22, pg. ``f30!}, 49\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  15, v.  21-22, 49, pg. ``f30!}.} and the same
death\index{Death:spiritual, in sin ``f10!} in sin and corrupted\index{Sin:original:corrupt nature:conveyed from Adam
``f10!} nature conveyed, to all their posterity descending from them by ordinary\index{Sin:original:by ordinary
generation ``f10!} generation.\footnote{\ Psalm 51:5\index{19 Psalms:ch.  51, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}; Genesis 5:3\index{01
Genesis:ch.   5, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}; Job 14:4\index{18 Job:ch.  14, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}; Job 15:14\index{18 Job:ch. 
15, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

6.4\ \ From this original corruption, whereby\index{Sin:original:corrupt nature:whole ``f10!} we are utterly
indisposed\index{Sin:original:utterly indisposed ``f10!}, disabled\index{Sin:original:utterly unable and unwilling to
do will of God ``f10!}, and made opposite to all good,\footnote{\ Romans 5:6\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.   6, pg.

``f30!}; Colossians 1:21\index{51 Colossians:ch.   1, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}.} and wholly
inclined\index{Sin:original:inclined to do evil ``f10!} to all evil,\footnote{\ Genesis 6:5\index{01 Genesis:ch.   6,
v.   5, pg. ``f30!}; Genesis 8:21\index{01 Genesis:ch.   8, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 3:10\index{45 Romans:ch.   3,
v.  10, pg. ``f30!}{}-12\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.  10-12, pg. ``f30!}.} do proceed all\index{Sin:original:proceeds
all transgressions ``f10!} actual transgressions\index{God's law:commandments:transgressions ``f10!}.\footnote{\ James
1:14\index{59 James:ch.   1, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}{}-15\index{59 James:ch.   1, v.  14-15, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians
2:2\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}{}-3\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   2-3, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew
15:19\index{40 Matthew:ch.  15, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

6.5\ \ This corruption\index{Sanctification:remnants of corruption remain ``f10!} of nature, during this life, does
remain in those that are regenerated\index{Regeneration:regeneration ``f10!};\footnote{\ 1 John 1:8, 10\index{62 1
John:ch.   1, v.   8, 10, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 7:14\index{45 Romans:ch.   7, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}, 17-18, 23\index{45
Romans:ch.   7, v.  14, 17-18, 23, pg. ``f30!}; James 3:2\index{59 James:ch.   3, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; Proverbs

``f30!}0\index{21 Ecclesiastes:ch.   7, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}.} and although it be, through Christ, pardoned
and\index{Regeneration:pardoned of sin ``f10!} mortified\index{Sin:mortified ``f10!}, yet both itself and all the
motions thereof are truly\index{Sin:original:corrupt nature:whole ``f10!} and properly sin.\footnote{\ Romans 7:5, 7-8,

``f30!}7\index{48 Galatians:ch.   5, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

6.6\ \ Every sin, both original and actual, being a transgression of\index{God's law:commandments:transgressions ``f10!}
the righteous law\index{God's law:righteous requirements ``f10!} of God, and contrary thereunto,\footnote{\ 1 John
3:4\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.} does, in its own nature, bring guilt\index{guilt ``f10!} upon the
sinner;\footnote{\ Romans 2:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}5\index{45 Romans:ch.   2, v.  15, pg.
``f30!}; Romans 3:9\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}, 19\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.   9, 19, pg. ``f30!}.}
whereby he is bound over to the wrath of God\index{Wrath:of God:for sin ``f10!},\footnote{\ Ephesians 2:3\index{49
Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}.} and curse of the\index{Curse:of the law ``f10!} law,\footnote{\ Galatians
3:10\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}.} and so made subject to death\index{Death:punishment for sin
``f10!},\footnote{\ Romans 6:23\index{45 Romans:ch.   6, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}.} with all
miseries\index{Punishment:misery ``f10!} spiritual,\footnote{\ Ephesians 4:18\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.  18, pg.
``f30!}.} temporal,\index{Judgement:temporal ``f10!}\footnote{\ Romans 8:2\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   2, pg.
``f30!}0\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}; Lamentations 3:39\index{25 Lamentations:ch.   3, v.  39, pg.
``f30!}.} and eternal.\footnote{\ Matthew 25:41\index{40 Matthew:ch.  25, v.  41, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Thessalonians
1:9\index{53 2 Thessalonians:ch.   1, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}.}

\section{Chapter 7 -- Of God's Covenant with Man}
\index{Covenant:of God with man ``f10!}7.1\ \ The distance\index{Mankind:great distance between him and God ``f10!}
between God and the creature\index{creatures ``f10!} is so great, that although
reasonable\index{Mankind:created:reasonable soul ``f10!} creatures do owe obedience\index{God's
law:commandments:obedience:required ``f10!} unto Him as their Creator\index{God's attributes:creator:of all things
``f10!}, yet they could never have any fruition of Him as their blessedness and\index{Believers:blessed in/by God
``f10!} reward\index{Believers:rewarded by God ``f10!}, but by some voluntary condescension\index{God's
attributes:condescension, voluntary ``f10!} on God's part, which He has been pleased\index{Providence:at God's pleasure
``f10!} to express by way of covenant\index{Covenant:administrations ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Isaiah 40:13-17\index{23
Isaiah:ch.  40, v.  13-17, pg. ``f30!}; Job 9:32-33\index{18 Job:ch.   9, v.  32-33, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Samuel
2:25\index{09 1 Samuel:ch.   2, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 113:5-6\index{19 Psalms:ch. 113, v.   5-6, pg. ``f30!};
Psalm 100:2\index{19 Psalms:ch. 100, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}{}-3\index{19 Psalms:ch. 100, v.   2-3, pg. ``f30!}; Job
22:2-3\index{18 Job:ch.  22, v.   2-3, pg. ``f30!}; Job 35:7-8\index{18 Job:ch.  35, v.   7-8, pg. ``f30!}; Luke
17:10\index{42 Luke:ch.  17, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 17:24\index{44 Acts:ch.  17, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}{}-25\index{44
Acts:ch.  17, v.  24-25, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip


7.2\ \ The first covenant made\index{Covenant:first:made with man ``f10!} with man was a covenant of
works\index{Covenant:works:works ``f10!},\footnote{\ Galatians 3:12\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}.}
wherein life was promised to\index{Covenant:first:promised life ``f10!} Adam, and in him to\index{Adam:covenant made
with him ``f10!} his posterity\index{Sin:original:all mankind descending from Adam ``f10!},\footnote{\ Romans
5:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}2\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}{}-20\index{45 Romans:ch.
  5, v.  12-20, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 10:5\index{45 Romans:ch.  10, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.} upon
condition\index{Covenant:works:conditional on perfect obedience ``f10!} of perfect and personal
obedience\index{Covenant:works:perfect obedience required ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Genesis 2:17\index{01 Genesis:ch.   2, v.
 17, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 3:10\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

7.3\ \ Man by his fall\index{Sin:original:first transgression (of Adam) ``f10!} having made himself
incapable\index{Covenant:works:Adam:incapable of life after his sin ``f10!} of life by that covenant,
the\index{Covenant:first:broken ``f10!} Lord was pleased\index{Providence:at God's pleasure ``f10!} to make a
second\index{Covenant:second ``f10!},\footnote{\ Galatians 3:21\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}; Romans
3:2\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}0\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}{}-21\index{45 Romans:ch.
  3, v.  20-21, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 8:3\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}; Genesis 3:15\index{01 Genesis:ch.
  3, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 42:6\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  42, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}.} commonly called the covenant of
grace\index{Covenant:grace:grace ``f10!}; wherein He freely\index{Salvation:freely offered ``f10!} offers unto sinners
life and salvation\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!} by Jesus Christ, requiring\index{Salvation:faith
alone required ``f10!} of them faith\index{Faith:in Jesus Christ ``f10!} in Him, that they may be
saved,\footnote{\ Mark 16:15\index{41 Mark:ch.  16, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}{}-16\index{41 Mark:ch.  16, v.  15-16, pg.
``f30!}; John 3:16\index{43 John:ch.   3, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 10:6, 9\index{45 Romans:ch.  10, v.   6, 9, pg.
``f30!}; Galatians 3:11\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}.} and promising to\index{Holy Spirit:promising
to believers ``f10!} give unto all those that are ordained unto\index{Predestination:unto life ``f10!} life His Holy
Spirit\index{Holy Spirit:Holy Spirit ``f10!}, to make them willing and able to\index{Conversion:renewal of the will
``f10!} believe.\footnote{\ Ezekiel 36:26\index{26 Ezekiel:ch.  36, v.  26, pg. ``f30!}{}-27\index{26 Ezekiel:ch.  36,
v.  26-27, pg. ``f30!}; John 6:44\index{43 John:ch.   6, v.  44, pg. ``f30!}{}-45\index{43 John:ch.   6, v.  44-45, pg.
``f30!}.}


\bigskip

7.4\ \ This covenant of grace\index{Covenant:grace:grace ``f10!} is frequently set forth in Scripture by the name of a
Testament\index{Covenant:testament ``f10!}, in reference to the death\index{Jesus:death:death ``f10!} of Jesus Christ
the Testator\index{Covenant:grace:Jesus testator ``f10!}, and to the everlasting

11, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

7.5\ \ This covenant was\index{Covenant:administrations ``f10!} differently administered in the time of the law, and in
the time of the gospel\index{Gospel:gospel ``f10!}:\footnote{\ 2 Corinthians 3:6\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   3, v.  
6, pg. ``f30!}{}-9\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   3, v.   6-9, pg. ``f30!}.} under the law, it was administered by
promises\index{Covenant:promises ``f10!}, prophecies\index{Covenant:prophecies ``f10!}, sacrifices\index{Ceremonial
law:sacrifices ``f10!}, circumcision\index{circumcision ``f10!}, the paschal\index{paschal lamb ``f10!}
lamb\index{lamb, paschal ``f10!}, and other types\index{types, OT ``f10!} and ordinances delivered\index{Covenant:OT
ordinances:signified Christ ``f10!} to the people of the Jews, all\index{Jews:OT ordinances ``f10!}
fore-signifying\index{Ceremonial law:fore-signifying Christ ``f10!} Christ to come:\footnote{\ Hebrews 8-10\index{58
Hebrews:ch. 8-10, pg. ``f30!} chapters, Romans 4:11\index{45 Romans:ch.   4, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}; Colossians

pg. ``f30!}.} which were, for that time, sufficient and\index{Covenant:OT ordinances:sufficient for that time ``f10!}
efficacious\index{Covenant:OT ordinances:efficacious ``f10!}, through the operation\index{Holy Spirit:operations:saving
``f10!} of the Spirit, to\index{Holy Spirit:instructs the elect ``f10!} instruct and build up the\index{Holy
Spirit:builds up the elect ``f10!} elect\index{Election:elect of God ``f10!} in faith\index{Faith:in Jesus Christ, as
Messiah ``f10!} in the promised\index{Jesus:Messiah promised ``f10!} Messiah,\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 10:1-4\index{46
1 Corinthians:ch.  10, v.   1-4, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 11:13\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  11, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; John
8:56\index{43 John:ch.   8, v.  56, pg. ``f30!}.} by whom they had full remission\index{Redemption:remission of sins
``f10!} of sins, and eternal salvation\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!}; and is called, the Old
Testament\index{Scripture:Old Testament ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Galatians 3:7-9, 14\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.   7-9,
14, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

7.6\ \ Under the gospel\index{Gospel:gospel ``f10!}, when Christ, the substance,\footnote{\ Colossians 2:17\index{51
Colossians:ch.   2, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}.} was exhibited, the\index{Covenant:grace:exhibited ``f10!} ordinances
in\index{Church:furnished with:ordinances of God ``f10!} which this covenant is dispensed are\index{Covenant:new:ways
dispensed ``f10!} the preaching of the Word\index{Preaching:ministry of the Word ``f10!}, and the
administration\index{Church:true:sacraments administered ``f10!} of the sacraments\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances
``f10!} of Baptism and\index{Baptism:sacrament ``f10!} the Lord's Supper\index{Lord's Supper:sacrament
``f10!}:\footnote{\ Matthew 28:19\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}{}-20\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v. 
19-20, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 11:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}3\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch. 
11, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}{}-25\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  23-25, pg. ``f30!}.} which, though fewer in number,
and administered with\index{Sacraments:to be:administered with simplicity ``f10!} more simplicity, and less
outward\index{Sacraments:NT less outward glory than OT ``f10!} glory; yet, in them, it is held forth in more
fulness\index{Covenant:new:more fulness ``f10!}, evidence, and spiritual efficacy,\footnote{\ Hebrews 12:2\index{58
Hebrews:ch.  12, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}2\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  12, v.  22, pg. ``f30!} to 28; Jeremiah 31:3\index{24
Jeremiah:ch.  31, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}3\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  31, v.  33, pg. ``f30!}{}-34\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  31,
v.  33-34, pg. ``f30!}.} to all nations\index{Gospel:to all nations ``f10!}, both Jews and\index{Jews:called ``f10!}
Gentiles\index{Gentiles:called ``f10!};\footnote{\ Matthew 28:19\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  19, pg. ``f30!};
Ephesians 2:1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}5-19\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.  15-19, pg. ``f30!}.}
and is called the New Testament\index{Scripture:New Testament ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Luke 22:20\index{42 Luke:ch.  22, v. 
20, pg. ``f30!}.} There are not therefore two covenants of\index{Covenant:grace:one only ``f10!} grace, differing in
substance\index{Covenant:grace:one, but differ in substance ``f10!}, but one and the same, under various
dispensations\index{Covenant:dispensations ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Galatians 3:14, 16\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.  14,
16, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 3:2\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}1-23, 30\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.  21-23,
30, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 32:1\index{19 Psalms:ch.  32, v.   1, pg. ``f30!} with Romans 4:3, 6, 16-17, 23-24\index{45
Romans:ch.   4, v.   3, 6, 16-17, 23-24, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 13:8\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  13, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}; Acts
15:11\index{44 Acts:ch.  15, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}.}

\section{Chapter 8 -- Of Christ the Mediator}
\index{Jesus:mediator:of covenant ``f10!}8.1\ \ It pleased\index{Providence:at God's pleasure ``f10!} God, in His
eternal purpose\index{Predestination:eternal purpose ``f10!}, to choose and ordain the\index{Predestination:Jesus as
mediator ``f10!} Lord Jesus, His only begotten\index{Jesus:begotten by the Father ``f10!} Son\index{Jesus:Son of God
``f10!}, to be the Mediator\index{Jesus:mediator:of covenant ``f10!} between God and man;\footnote{\ Isaiah
42:1\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  42, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Peter 1:19-20\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   1, v.  19-20, pg. ``f30!};
John 3:16\index{43 John:ch.   3, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Timothy 2:5\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   2, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.}
the Prophet\index{Jesus:prophet:office ``f10!},\footnote{\ Acts 3:22\index{44 Acts:ch.   3, v.  22, pg. ``f30!}.}
Priest\index{Jesus:priest ``f10!},\footnote{\ Hebrews 5:5-6\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   5, v.   5-6, pg. ``f30!}.} and
King\index{Jesus:King ``f10!},\footnote{\ Psalm 2:6\index{19 Psalms:ch.   2, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 1:33\index{42
Luke:ch.   1, v.  33, pg. ``f30!}.} the Head\index{Church:Christ as head ``f10!} and Saviour\index{Jesus:saviour of the
Church ``f10!} of His Church\index{Church:Christ's ``f10!},\footnote{\ Ephesians 5:2\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   5, v.  
2, pg. ``f30!}3\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   5, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}.} the Heir\index{Jesus:heir of all things ``f10!} of
all things,\footnote{\ Hebrews 1:2\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   1, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}.} and Judge of\index{Jesus:judge:of
world ``f10!} the world:\footnote{\ Acts 17:31\index{44 Acts:ch.  17, v.  31, pg. ``f30!}.} unto whom He did from all
eternity\index{God's attributes:eternal ``f10!} give a people, to be His seed\index{Election:God's seed
``f10!},\footnote{\ John 17:6\index{43 John:ch.  17, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 22:30\index{19 Psalms:ch.  22, v.  30,
pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 53:10\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  53, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}.} and to be by Him in time
redeemed\index{Redemption:purchased by Christ ``f10!}, called, justified\index{Justification:justified ``f10!},
sanctified\index{Sanctification:sanctification ``f10!}, and glorified\index{Resurrection:believers:into
glory:glorification ``f10!}.\footnote{\ 1 Timothy 2:6\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   2, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah
55:4-5\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  55, v.   4-5, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 1:30\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   1, v.  30, pg.
``f30!}.}


\bigskip

8.2\ \ The Son\index{Jesus:Son of God ``f10!} of God, the second person in\index{Jesus:second person in Trinity ``f10!}
the Trinity\index{God's attributes:trinity:one substance ``f10!}, being very and eternal God\index{God's
attributes:eternal ``f10!}, of one substance and equal with the\index{God's attributes:trinity:persons equal ``f10!}
Father\index{Father:God the ``f10!}, did, when the fulness of time\index{Jesus:incarnation:in fulness of time ``f10!}
was come, take upon Him man's nature,\footnote{\ John 1:1\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}, 14\index{43
John:ch.   1, v.   1, 14, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 5:20\index{62 1 John:ch.   5, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}; Philippians
2:6\index{50 Philippians:ch.   2, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 4:4\index{48 Galatians:ch.   4, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.}
with all the essential properties and\index{Jesus:human nature:essential properties ``f10!} common infirmities
thereof\index{Jesus:humiliation:suffered:infirmities ``f10!}, yet without sin:\footnote{\ Hebrews 2:1\index{58
Hebrews:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}4\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   2, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}, 16-17\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   2, v.
 14, 16-17, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 4:15\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   4, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}.} being conceived
by\index{Jesus:conceived:by the power of the Holy Spirit ``f10!} the power of the Holy Ghost\index{Holy Spirit:Holy
Ghost ``f10!}, in the womb\index{Jesus:conceived:in womb of virgin Mary ``f10!} of the virgin\index{Jesus:born of
virgin Mary ``f10!} Mary\index{Mary, mother of Jesus ``f10!}, of her substance\index{Jesus:conceived:of Mary's
substance ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Luke 1:27, 31, 35\index{42 Luke:ch.   1, v.  27, 31, 35, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians
4:4\index{48 Galatians:ch.   4, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.} So that two whole, perfect, and distinct natures\index{Jesus:two
distinct natures ``f10!}, the Godhead\index{God's attributes:Godhead ``f10!} and the manhood\index{Jesus:human
nature:manhood ``f10!}, were inseparably\index{Jesus:human nature:inseparable from divine, one person ``f10!} joined
together in one person, without conversion, composition\index{God's attributes:being:no composition ``f10!}, or
confusion\index{God's attributes:being:no confusion ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Luke 1:35\index{42 Luke:ch.   1, v.  35, pg.
``f30!}; Colossians 2:9\index{51 Colossians:ch.   2, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 9:5\index{45 Romans:ch.   9, v.   5,
pg. ``f30!}; 1 Peter 3:18\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   3, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Timothy 3:1\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   3, v.  
1, pg. ``f30!}6\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   3, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}.} Which person is very God, and very man, yet one
Christ, the only Mediator\index{Jesus:mediator:of covenant ``f10!} between God and man.\footnote{\ Romans
1:3-4\index{45 Romans:ch.   1, v.   3-4, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Timothy 2:5\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   2, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

8.3\ \ The Lord Jesus, in His human nature thus\index{Jesus:human nature:united with divine ``f10!} united to the
divine, was sanctified\index{Sanctification:sanctification ``f10!} and anointed\index{Jesus:anointed with Holy Spirit
``f10!} with the Holy Spirit\index{Holy Spirit:Holy Spirit ``f10!}, above measure,\footnote{\ Psalm 45:7\index{19
Psalms:ch.  45, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}; John 3:3\index{43 John:ch.   3, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}4\index{43 John:ch.   3, v. 
34, pg. ``f30!}.} having in Him all the treasures of wisdom and\index{Jesus:wisdom, treasures of ``f10!}
knowledge;\index{Jesus:human nature:all knowledge ``f10!}\footnote{\ Colossians 2:3\index{51 Colossians:ch.   2, v.  
3, pg. ``f30!}.} in whom it pleased\index{Providence:at God's pleasure ``f10!} the Father\index{Father:God the ``f10!}
that all fulness should\index{Jesus:fulness of Godhead dwells ``f10!} dwell;\footnote{\ Colossians 1:19\index{51
Colossians:ch.   1, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}.} to the end that, being holy\index{Jesus:holy ``f10!},
harmless\index{Jesus:harmless ``f10!}, undefiled\index{Jesus:undefiled ``f10!}, and full of grace\index{Jesus:full of
grace ``f10!} and truth\index{God's attributes:truth ``f10!},\footnote{\ Hebrews 7:26\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   7, v.  26,
pg. ``f30!}; John 1:1\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}4\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}.} He might
be thoroughly furnished\index{Jesus:mediator:fully furnished to execute office ``f10!} to execute the
office\index{Jesus:offices ``f10!} of a mediator\index{Jesus:mediator:of covenant ``f10!} and surety\index{Jesus:surety
for the elect ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Acts 10:38\index{44 Acts:ch.  10, v.  38, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 12:2\index{58
Hebrews:ch.  12, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}4\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  12, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 7:22\index{58 Hebrews:ch. 
 7, v.  22, pg. ``f30!}.} Which office He took not unto Himself, but was thereunto called by His
Father,\footnote{\ Hebrews 5:4\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   5, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}{}-5\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   5, v.   4-5,
pg. ``f30!}.} who put all power\index{Jesus:almighty power ``f10!} and judgment into\index{Jesus:judge:assigned by
Father ``f10!} His hand, and gave Him commandment\index{Jesus:commanded by the Father ``f10!} to execute the
same\index{Jesus:obedience:to God's law ``f10!}.\footnote{\ John 5:22, 27\index{43 John:ch.   5, v.  22, 27, pg.
``f30!}; Matthew 28:18\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 2:36\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  36, pg.
``f30!}.}

8.4\ \ This office\index{Jesus:offices ``f10!} the Lord Jesus did most willingly\index{Jesus:humiliation:willingly
undertaken ``f10!} undertake;\footnote{\ Psalm 40:7-8\index{19 Psalms:ch.  40, v.   7-8, pg. ``f30!} with Hebrews
10:5-10\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  10, v.   5-10, pg. ``f30!}; John 10:18\index{43 John:ch.  10, v.  18, pg. ``f30!};
Philippians 2:8\index{50 Philippians:ch.   2, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}.} which that He might discharge,
He\index{Jesus:discharged:his duties ``f10!} was made under the law,\footnote{\ Galatians 4:4\index{48 Galatians:ch.  
4, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.} and did perfectly fulfil\index{Jesus:obedience:to God's law ``f10!} it,\footnote{\ Matthew
3:15\index{40 Matthew:ch.   3, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 5:17\index{40 Matthew:ch.   5, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}.}
endured most grievous torments immediately\index{Jesus:humiliation:suffered:torments ``f10!} in His
soul,\footnote{\ Matthew 26:37-38\index{40 Matthew:ch.  26, v.  37-38, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 22:44\index{42 Luke:ch.  22,
v.  44, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 27:4\index{40 Matthew:ch.  27, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}6\index{40 Matthew:ch.  27, v.  46, pg.
``f30!}.} and most painful\index{Jesus:humiliation:suffered pain ``f10!} sufferings in\index{Jesus:death:sufferings and
death ``f10!} His body;\footnote{\ Matthew Chapters 26-27.} was crucified\index{Jesus:crucified ``f10!}, and
died\index{Jesus:died ``f10!};\footnote{\ Philippians 2:8\index{50 Philippians:ch.   2, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}.} was
buried\index{Jesus:buried ``f10!}, and remained under the power of death\index{Jesus:death:under power of ``f10!}; yet
saw no corruption\index{Jesus:death:no corruption ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Acts. 2:23-24, 27; Acts 13:3\index{44 Acts:ch. 
13, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}7\index{44 Acts:ch.  13, v.  37, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 6:9\index{45 Romans:ch.   6, v.   9, pg.
``f30!}.} On the third day\index{Jesus:resurrection:third day ``f10!} He arose\index{Jesus:resurrection:historical fact
``f10!} from the dead\index{Jesus:resurrection:from the dead ``f10!},\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 15:3-4\index{46 1
Corinthians:ch.  15, v.   3-4, pg. ``f30!}.} with the same body in which He suffered\index{Jesus:resurrection:body
same:in which he suffered ``f10!},\footnote{\ John 20:25, 27\index{43 John:ch.  20, v.  25, 27, pg. ``f30!}.} with
which also he ascended\index{Jesus:ascension:into heaven ``f10!} into heaven, and there sits\index{Jesus:in
heaven:sitting at right hand of Fathe ``f10!} at the right hand of His Father\index{Father:God the
``f10!},\footnote{\ Mark 16:19\index{41 Mark:ch.  16, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}.} making intercession\index{Jesus:in
heaven:intercession made for all believers ``f10!},\footnote{\ Romans 8:3\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   3, pg.

\section{Chapter 9 -- Of Free Will}
\index{Causation:will of creatures:free ``f10!}9.1\ \ God has endued the\index{Causation:will of creatures:natural
liberty ``f10!} will of man with that natural liberty, that\index{Liberty:natural ``f10!} is neither forced, nor by any
absolute\index{Mankind:human will, natural liberty ``f10!} necessity of\index{Liberty:not absolute necessity to good or
evil ``f10!} nature determined to good or evil.\footnote{\ Matthew 17:12\index{40 Matthew:ch.  17, v.  12, pg. ``f30!};
James 1:14\index{59 James:ch.   1, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}; Deuteronomy 30:19\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.  30, v.  19, pg.
``f30!}.}


\bigskip

9.2\ \ Man, in his state of innocency, had\index{Mankind:created:state of innocence ``f10!} freedom
and\index{Causation:will of creatures:free ``f10!} power to will and to do that which was good, and well
pleasing\index{Mankind:created:initially able to please God ``f10!} to God;\footnote{\ Ecclesiastes 7:2\index{21
Ecclesiastes:ch.   7, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; Genesis 1:2\index{01 Genesis:ch.   1, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}6\index{01
Genesis:ch.   1, v.  26, pg. ``f30!}.} but yet, mutably\index{Mankind:created:mutable ``f10!}, so that he might
fall\index{Sin:original:first transgression (of Adam) ``f10!} from it.\footnote{\ Genesis 2:16-17\index{01 Genesis:ch. 
 2, v.  16-17, pg. ``f30!}; Genesis 3:6\index{01 Genesis:ch.   3, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

9.3\ \ Man, by his fall\index{Sin:original:first transgression (of Adam) ``f10!} into a state of sin, has wholly lost
all ability of\index{Sin:original:inability to:do anything good ``f10!} will to any spiritual
good\index{Sin:original:lost all spiritual good ``f10!} accompanying salvation\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith
``f10!}:\footnote{\ Romans 5:6\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 8:7\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.  
7, pg. ``f30!}; John 15:5\index{43 John:ch.  15, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.} so as, a natural man, being altogether averse
from that good,\footnote{\ Romans 3:10\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}, 12\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v. 
10, 12, pg. ``f30!}.} and dead in sin\index{Death:spiritual, in sin ``f10!},\footnote{\ Ephesians 2:1\index{49
Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}, 5\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   1, 5, pg. ``f30!}; Colossians 2:13\index{51
Colossians:ch.   2, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}.} is not able, by his own strength, to\index{Conversion:not by own strength
``f10!} convert himself\index{Conversion:not of self ``f10!}, or to prepare himself thereunto.\footnote{\ John
6:44\index{43 John:ch.   6, v.  44, pg. ``f30!}, 65\index{43 John:ch.   6, v.  44, 65, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians
2:2\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}{}-5\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   2-5, pg. ``f30!}; 1
Corinthians 2:14\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   2, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}; Titus 3:3-5\index{56 Titus:ch.   3, v.   3-5, pg.
``f30!}.} 


\bigskip

9.4\ \ When God converts\index{Conversion:conversion ``f10!} a sinner, and translates\index{Conversion:translated into
state of grace ``f10!} him into the state of grace\index{Grace:state:translation into at conversion ``f10!}, He
frees\index{Believers:freed from:guilt of sin ``f10!} him from his natural bondage under\index{Sin:bondage to ``f10!}
sin;\footnote{\ Colossians 1:13\index{51 Colossians:ch.   1, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; John 8:34\index{43 John:ch.   8, v. 
34, pg. ``f30!}, 36\index{43 John:ch.   8, v.  34, 36, pg. ``f30!}.} and, by His grace\index{Grace:God's free ``f10!}
alone, enables\index{Sanctification:enabled by:grace ``f10!} him freely\index{Causation:will of creatures:free ``f10!}
to will and to do that which is spiritually good;\index{Good works:spiritual services ``f10!}\footnote{\ Philippians
2:13\index{50 Philippians:ch.   2, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 6:18, 22\index{45 Romans:ch.   6, v.  18, 22, pg.
``f30!}.} yet so, as that by reason of his remaining corruption, he\index{Sanctification:remnants of corruption remain
``f10!} does not perfectly, nor only, will that which is good, but does also will that which is
evil.\footnote{\ Galatians 5:1\index{48 Galatians:ch.   5, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}7\index{48 Galatians:ch.   5, v.  17, pg.
``f30!}; Romans 7:15, 18\index{45 Romans:ch.   7, v.  15, 18, pg. ``f30!}{}-19, 21, 23\index{45 Romans:ch.   7, v.  15,
18-19, 21, 23, pg. ``f30!}.} 


\bigskip

9.5\ \ The will of man is made perfectly and immutably\index{God's attributes:immutable ``f10!} free to do good alone,
in the state of glory\index{Resurrection:believers:into glory:light ``f10!} only.\footnote{\ Ephesians 4:13\index{49
Ephesians:ch.   4, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 12:2\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  12, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}3\index{58

  9, pg. ``f30!}{}-10\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   1, v.   9-10, pg. ``f30!}.} enlightening\index{Effectual

``f30!}5\index{42 Luke:ch.  18, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}{}-16\index{42 Luke:ch.  18, v.  15-16, pg. ``f30!} and Acts

works\index{Providence:God's works ``f10!} when, and where, and how He pleases\index{Providence:at God's pleasure
``f10!}:\footnote{\ John 3:8\index{43 John:ch.   3, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}.} so also, are all other

\bigskip

10.4\ \ Others, not elected\index{Election:some not chosen ``f10!}, although they may be called by the ministry of the

``f30!}.} and may have some common operations\index{Holy Spirit:operations:common ``f10!} of the
Spirit,\footnote{\ Matthew 7:22\index{40 Matthew:ch.   7, v.  22, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 13:20-21\index{40 Matthew:ch.

``f30!}; John 8:24\index{43 John:ch.   8, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}.} much less can men, not professing
the\index{Profession:absent ``f10!} Christian religion\index{Profession:of false religion ``f10!}, be saved in any
other way whatsoever, be they never so diligent to\index{God's law:diligence in application ``f10!} frame
their\index{Salvation:not by:obedience ``f10!} lives according to the light of nature, and the law of that religion
they do profess.\footnote{\ Acts 4:12\index{44 Acts:ch.   4, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 2:1\index{49 Ephesians:ch. 
 2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}2\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}; John 4:22\index{43 John:ch.   4, v.  22, pg.
``f30!}; John 14:6\index{43 John:ch.  14, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; John 17:3\index{43 John:ch.  17, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}.}
And to assert and maintain that they may, is very pernicious\index{Salvation:outside of Christ, pernicious and
detestable claim ``f10!}, and to be detested.\footnote{\ 2 John 9-11\index{63 2 John:v. 9-11, pg. ``f30!}; 1

``f30!}; Galatians 1:6-8\index{48 Galatians:ch.   1, v.   6-8, pg. ``f30!}.}

\section{Chapter 14 -- Of Saving Faith}
\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!}\index{Faith:saving ``f10!}14.1\ \ The grace of faith\index{Faith:given
