is the work of the Spirit of Christ\index{Holy Spirit:Spirit of Christ ``f10!} in their
hearts;\index{Heart:new:enlightened ``f10!}\footnote{\ 2 Corinthians 4:13\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   4, v.  13, pg.
``f30!}; Ephesians 1:1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}7-19\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.  17-19, pg.
``f30!}; Ephesians 2:8\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}.} and is ordinarily wrought by
the\index{Preaching:convincing and converting sinners ``f10!} ministry of the Word\index{Preaching:ministry of the Word
``f10!}:\footnote{\ Romans 10:1\index{45 Romans:ch.  10, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}4\index{45 Romans:ch.  10, v.  14, pg.
``f30!}, 17\index{45 Romans:ch.  10, v.  14, 17, pg. ``f30!}.} by which also, and by the
administration\index{Sacraments:grace:administered ``f10!} of the sacraments\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!},
and prayer, it\index{Prayer:act of worship ``f10!} is increased and strengthened\index{Sacraments:strengthening
ordinances ``f10!}.\footnote{\ 1 Peter 2:2\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   2, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 20:32\index{44 Acts:ch. 
20, v.  32, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 4:11\index{45 Romans:ch.   4, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 17:5\index{42 Luke:ch.  17, v. 
 5, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 1:16\index{45 Romans:ch.   1, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}{}-17\index{45 Romans:ch.   1, v.  16-17, pg.
``f30!}.}


\bigskip

14.2\ \ By this faith\index{Faith:believes Scripture to be word of God ``f10!}, a Christian believes
to\index{Scripture:to be:believed ``f10!} be true whatsoever is revealed in the Word, for\index{Scripture:word of
God:standard for:life ``f10!} the authority of God Himself speaking therein;\footnote{\ John 4:42\index{43 John:ch.  
4, v.  42, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Thessalonians 2:13\index{52 1 Thessalonians:ch.   2, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John
5:10\index{62 1 John:ch.   5, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 24:14\index{44 Acts:ch.  24, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}.} and acts
differently upon that which each particular passage thereof contains; yielding\index{God's
law:commandments:obedience:required ``f10!} obedience to the commands\index{God's law:commandments:ten
``f10!},\footnote{\ Romans 16:2\index{45 Romans:ch.  16, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}6\index{45 Romans:ch.  16, v.  26, pg.
``f30!}.} trembling at the threatenings\index{God's law:threatenings for disobedience ``f10!},\footnote{\ Isaiah
66:2\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  66, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}.} and embracing the promises\index{Salvation:promises made ``f10!} of
God for this life, and that which is to come.\footnote{\ Hebrews 11:13\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  11, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; 1
Timothy 4:8\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   4, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}.} But the principal\index{Faith:principal acts of ``f10!}
acts of saving faith\index{Faith:saving ``f10!} are accepting\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!},
receiving, and\index{Faith:instrument:for receiving Christ ``f10!} resting upon\index{Faith:resting on Christ ``f10!}
Christ alone for justification\index{Justification:justification ``f10!},
sanctification\index{Sanctification:sanctification ``f10!}, and eternal life\index{eternal life ``f10!}, by virtue of
the covenant of grace\index{Covenant:grace:grace ``f10!}.\footnote{\ John 1:1\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.   1, pg.
``f30!}2\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 16:31\index{44 Acts:ch.  16, v.  31, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians
2:20\index{48 Galatians:ch.   2, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 15:11\index{44 Acts:ch.  15, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

14.3\ \ This faith is different in degrees\index{Faith:degrees of ``f10!}, weak or strong;\footnote{\ Hebrews
5:13-14\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   5, v.  13-14, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 4:19-20\index{45 Romans:ch.   4, v.  19-20, pg.
``f30!}; Matthew 6:30\index{40 Matthew:ch.   6, v.  30, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 8:10\index{40 Matthew:ch.   8, v.  10, pg.
``f30!}.} may be often and many ways assailed\index{Faith:assailed ``f10!}, and weakened\index{Faith:weak ``f10!}, but
gets the victory\index{Faith:victorious ``f10!};\footnote{\ Luke 22:31-32\index{42 Luke:ch.  22, v.  31-32, pg.
``f30!}; Ephesians 6:16\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   6, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 5:4\index{62 1 John:ch.   5, v.   4,
pg. ``f30!}{}-5\index{62 1 John:ch.   5, v.   4-5, pg. ``f30!}.} growing up in\index{Assurance:growing ``f10!} many to
the attainment of a full assurance through\index{Assurance:of faith ``f10!} Christ,\footnote{\ Hebrews 6:11-12\index{58
Hebrews:ch.   6, v.  11-12, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 10:22\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  10, v.  22, pg. ``f30!}; Colossians
2:2\index{51 Colossians:ch.   2, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}.} who is both the author\index{Jesus:author of a believer's faith
``f10!} and finisher\index{Jesus:finisher of a believer's faith ``f10!} of our faith.\footnote{\ Hebrews 12:2\index{58
Hebrews:ch.  12, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}.}

\section{Chapter 15 -- Of Repentance unto Life}
\index{Repentance:unto life ``f10!}15.1\ \ Repentance\index{Repentance:unto life ``f10!} unto life is an evangelical
grace\index{Grace:evangelical ``f10!},\footnote{\ Zechariah 12:10\index{38 Zechariah:ch.  12, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; Acts
11:18\index{44 Acts:ch.  11, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}.} the doctrine whereof\index{Doctrine:Gospel ``f10!} is to be preached
by every\index{Preaching:call to repentance ``f10!} minister\index{Church officers:minsters ``f10!} of the
Gospel\index{Gospel:gospel ``f10!}, as well as that of faith\index{Faith:in Jesus Christ ``f10!} in
Christ.\footnote{\ Luke 24:47\index{42 Luke:ch.  24, v.  47, pg. ``f30!}; Mark 1:15\index{41 Mark:ch.   1, v.  15, pg.
``f30!}; Acts 20:21\index{44 Acts:ch.  20, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

15.2\ \ By it, a sinner, out of the sight and sense not only of the danger\index{Repentance:apprehension of danger of
sin ``f10!}, but also of the filthiness\index{Confession:of sin ``f10!} and odiousness\index{Sin:odious before God
``f10!} of his sins, as contrary to the holy\index{God's law:holy ``f10!} nature and righteous law\index{God's
law:righteous requirements ``f10!} of God; and upon the apprehension\index{Repentance:apprehension of God's mercy
``f10!} of his mercy in\index{God's attributes:merciful ``f10!} Christ to such as are
penitent\index{Repentance:penitence ``f10!}, so grieves for\index{Sin:grief and hatred of ``f10!}, and
hates\index{Sin:to be hated ``f10!} his sins, as to turn from them all unto God,\footnote{\ Ezekiel 18:30-31\index{26
Ezekiel:ch.  18, v.  30-31, pg. ``f30!}; Ezekiel 36:31\index{26 Ezekiel:ch.  36, v.  31, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah
30:22\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  30, v.  22, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 51:4\index{19 Psalms:ch.  51, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}; Jeremiah
31:18\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  31, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}{}-19\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  31, v.  18-19, pg. ``f30!}; Joel
2:12\index{29 Joel:ch.   2, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}{}-13\index{29 Joel:ch.   2, v.  12-13, pg. ``f30!}; Amos 5:15\index{30
Amos:ch.   5, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 119:128\index{19 Psalms:ch. 119, v. 128, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Corinthians
7:1\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   7, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}1\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   7, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}.}
purposing\index{Repentance:purposing to walk with God ``f10!} and endeavouring to walk with\index{God's
law:commandments:obedience:endeavoring ``f10!} Him in all the ways of His commandments\index{God's law:commandments:ten
``f10!}.\footnote{\ Psalm 119:6, 59, 106\index{19 Psalms:ch. 119, v.   6, 59, 106, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 1:6\index{42
Luke:ch.   1, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Kings 23:25\index{12 2 Kings:ch.  23, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

15.3\ \ Although repentance be\index{Repentance:required for pardon ``f10!} not to be rested in, as any satisfaction for
sin\index{Jesus:satisfied divine justice ``f10!}, or any cause of the pardon the\index{Forgiveness:God alone pardons
``f10!}reof,\footnote{\ Ezekiel 36:31\index{26 Ezekiel:ch.  36, v.  31, pg. ``f30!}{}-32\index{26 Ezekiel:ch.  36, v. 
31-32, pg. ``f30!}; Ezekiel 16:61-63\index{26 Ezekiel:ch.  16, v.  61-63, pg. ``f30!}.} which is the act of God's free
grace\index{Grace:God's free ``f10!} in Christ;\footnote{\ Hosea 14:2\index{28 Hosea:ch.  14, v.   2, pg. ``f30!},
4\index{28 Hosea:ch.  14, v.   2, 4, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 3:2\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}4\index{45
Romans:ch.   3, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 1:7\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}.} yet is it of such
necessity to\index{Repentance:necessity ``f10!} all sinners, that none may expect pardon without it.\footnote{\ Luke
13:3, 5\index{42 Luke:ch.  13, v.   3, 5, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 17:30-31\index{44 Acts:ch.  17, v.  30-31, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

15.4\ \ As there is no sin so small, but it deserves\index{Sin:deserves damnation ``f10!}
damnation\index{Punishment:everlasting:damnation ``f10!},\footnote{\ Romans 6:23\index{45 Romans:ch.   6, v.  23, pg.
``f30!}; Romans 5:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}2\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew
12:36\index{40 Matthew:ch.  12, v.  36, pg. ``f30!}.} so there is no sin so great, that it can bring damnation upon
those who truly\index{Repentance:for all sins ``f10!} repent.\footnote{\ Isaiah 55:7\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  55, v.   7,
pg. ``f30!}; Romans 8:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 1:16, 18\index{23 Isaiah:ch.   1, v.  16,
18, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

15.5\ \ Men ought not to content themselves with a general repentance, but\index{Repentance:for all sins ``f10!} it is
every man's duty to endeavour\index{Repentance:duty to endeavour ``f10!} to repent of his particular sins,
particularly.\footnote{\ Psalm 19:13\index{19 Psalms:ch.  19, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 19:8\index{42 Luke:ch.  19, v. 
 8, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Timothy 1:13, 15\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   1, v.  13, 15, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

15.6\ \ As every man is bound to make private confession\index{Confession:of sin ``f10!} of his sins to God, praying
for\index{Prayer:for pardon of sin ``f10!} the pardon the\index{Forgiveness:God alone pardons
``f10!}reof;\index{Forgiveness:beg pardon for ``f10!}\footnote{\ Psalm 51:4\index{19 Psalms:ch.  51, v.   4, pg.
``f30!}{}-5, 7, 9, 14\index{19 Psalms:ch.  51, v.   4-5, 7, 9, 14, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 32:5\index{19 Psalms:ch.  32, v. 
 5, pg. ``f30!}{}-6\index{19 Psalms:ch.  32, v.   5-6, pg. ``f30!}.} upon which, and the
forsaking\index{Repentance:forsaking sin ``f10!} of them, he shall find mercy:\index{Mercy:on confession
``f10!}\footnote{\ Proverbs 28:13\index{20 Proverbs:ch.  28, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 1:9\index{62 1 John:ch.   1,
v.   9, pg. ``f30!}.} so, he that scandalizes\index{Scandalous behaviour:to be confessed ``f10!} his brother, or the
Church of Christ\index{Church:Christ's ``f10!}, ought to be willing, by a private or public confession, and
sorrow\index{Confession:sorrow for sin ``f10!} for his sin, to declare his\index{Repentance:public declaration ``f10!}
repentance to\index{Repentance:to those offended ``f10!} those that are offended,\index{Confession:to those offended
``f10!}\footnote{\ James 5:16\index{59 James:ch.   5, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 17:3-4\index{42 Luke:ch.  17, v.   3-4,
pg. ``f30!}; Joshua 7:19\index{06 Joshua:ch.   7, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 51.} who are thereupon to be
reconciled\index{Confession:to be reconciled to God ``f10!} to him, and in love to\index{Love toward God:for God
``f10!} receive him.\footnote{\ 2 Corinthians 2:8\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   2, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}.}

\section{Chapter 16 -- Of Good Works}
\index{Good works:definition ``f10!}16.1\ \ Good works\index{Good works:definition ``f10!} are only such as God has
commanded in His\index{God's law:commandments:ten ``f10!} holy Word\index{Scripture:holy ``f10!},\footnote{\ Micah
6:8\index{33 Micah:ch.   6, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 12:2\index{45 Romans:ch.  12, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews
13:21\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  13, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}.} and not such as, without the warrant\index{Good works:not devised
by men without warrant ``f10!} thereof, are devised\index{Good works:not devised by men ``f10!} by men, out of blind
zeal, or\index{Good works:not out of blind zeal ``f10!} upon any pretence\index{pretence ``f10!} of good
intention\index{Good works:not by good intentions ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Matthew 15:9\index{40 Matthew:ch.  15, v.   9,
pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 29:13\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  29, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Peter 1:18\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   1, v.  18,
pg. ``f30!}; Romans 10:2\index{45 Romans:ch.  10, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; John 16:2\index{43 John:ch.  16, v.   2, pg.
``f30!}; 1 Samuel 15:21\index{09 1 Samuel:ch.  15, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}{}-23\index{09 1 Samuel:ch.  15, v.  21-23, pg.
``f30!}.} 


\bigskip

16.2\ \ These good works\index{Good works:adorn profession of faith ``f10!}, done in obedience\index{God's
law:commandments:obedience:required ``f10!} to God's commandments\index{God's law:commandments:ten ``f10!}, are the
fruits\index{Good works:fruit of salvation ``f10!} and evidences of a true and lively\index{Faith:lively ``f10!}
faith:\footnote{\ James 2:18, 22\index{59 James:ch.   2, v.  18, 22, pg. ``f30!}.} and by them believers
manifest\index{Good works:believers manifest thankfulness ``f10!} their thankfulness\index{Prayer:thanking God
``f10!},\footnote{\ Psalm 116:12-13\index{19 Psalms:ch. 116, v.  12-13, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Peter 2:9\index{60 1 Peter:ch.  
2, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}.} strengthen their assurance\index{Assurance:strengthened ``f10!},\footnote{\ 1 John
2:3\index{62 1 John:ch.   2, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}, 5\index{62 1 John:ch.   2, v.   3, 5, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Peter
1:5-10\index{61 2 Peter:ch.   1, v.   5-10, pg. ``f30!}.} edify\index{Good works:edify other Christians ``f10!} their
brethren\index{Believers:to build up fellow believers ``f10!},\footnote{\ 2 Corinthians 9:2\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch. 
 9, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 5:16\index{40 Matthew:ch.   5, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}.} adorn the
profession\index{Faith:profession of ``f10!} of the Gospel\index{Gospel:gospel ``f10!},\footnote{\ Titus 2:5,
9-12\index{56 Titus:ch.   2, v.   5, 9-12, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Timothy 6:1\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   6, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}.}
stop the mouths\index{Good works:stop mouths of adversaries ``f10!} of the adversaries,\footnote{\ 1 Peter
2:15\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   2, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}.} and glorify\index{Worship:glorifying God ``f10!} God,\footnote{\ 1
Peter 2:12\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   2, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}; Philippians 1:1\index{50 Philippians:ch.   1, v.   1, pg.
``f30!}1\index{50 Philippians:ch.   1, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}; John 15:8\index{43 John:ch.  15, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}.}
whose workmanship\index{Believers:God's workmanship ``f10!} they are, created in Christ\index{Conversion:created in
Christ ``f10!} Jesus thereunto;\footnote{\ Ephesians 2:1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}0\index{49
Ephesians:ch.   2, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}.} that, having their fruit unto holiness\index{Believers:holy:made perfect at
death ``f10!}, they may have the end, eternal life\index{eternal life ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Romans 6:22\index{45
Romans:ch.   6, v.  22, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

16.3\ \ Their ability to do\index{Good works:only in Holy Spirit ``f10!} good works\index{Good works:adorn profession of
faith ``f10!} is not at all of themselves, but wholly from the Spirit of Christ\index{Holy Spirit:Spirit of Christ
``f10!}.\footnote{\ John 15:4-5\index{43 John:ch.  15, v.   4-5, pg. ``f30!}; Ezekiel 36:26\index{26 Ezekiel:ch.  36,
v.  26, pg. ``f30!}{}-27\index{26 Ezekiel:ch.  36, v.  26-27, pg. ``f30!}.} And that they may be enabled
thereunto\index{Good works:enabled by Holy Spirit ``f10!}, besides the graces\index{Grace:in believers:by Holy Spirit
``f10!} they have already received, there is required an actual influence of the same Holy Spirit\index{Holy
Spirit:Holy Spirit ``f10!}, to work in them to will and to do of His good pleasure\index{Providence:at God's pleasure
``f10!}:\footnote{\ Philippians 2:13\index{50 Philippians:ch.   2, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; Philippians 4:13\index{50
Philippians:ch.   4, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Corinthians 3:5\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   3, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.} yet
are they not hereupon to grow negligent, as\index{Good works:not be negligent ``f10!} if they were not bound to perform
any duty, unless\index{God's law:commandments:duties:required by God ``f10!} upon a special motion of the Spirit;
but\index{Holy Spirit:helps believers do good works ``f10!} they ought to be diligent in\index{Grace:diligent use of
means ``f10!} stirring up the grace of\index{Grace:in believers:to be stirred up ``f10!} God that is in
them.\footnote{\ Philippians 2:12\index{50 Philippians:ch.   2, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 6:11-12\index{58
Hebrews:ch.   6, v.  11-12, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Peter 1:3, 5, 10-11\index{61 2 Peter:ch.   1, v.   3, 5, 10-11, pg. ``f30!};
Isaiah 64:7\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  64, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Timothy 1:6\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   1, v.   6, pg.
``f30!}; Acts 26:6-7\index{44 Acts:ch.  26, v.   6-7, pg. ``f30!}; Jude 20-21\index{65 Jude:v. 20-21, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

16.4\ \ They, who in their obedience\index{Salvation:not by:obedience ``f10!} attain to the greatest height which is
possible in this life, are so far from being able to supererogate\index{Good works:believers cannot supererogate (do
more than required) ``f10!}, and to do more than God requires, as\index{God's law:commandments:duties:required by God
``f10!} that they fall short\index{Sanctification:imperfection in believers ``f10!} of much which in duty they are
bound to do.\footnote{\ Luke 17:10\index{42 Luke:ch.  17, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; Nehemiah 13:22\index{16 Nehemiah:ch. 
13, v.  22, pg. ``f30!}; Job 9:2-3\index{18 Job:ch.   9, v.   2-3, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 5:1\index{48 Galatians:ch.  
5, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}7\index{48 Galatians:ch.   5, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

16.5\ \ We cannot, by our best works, merit\index{Salvation:not by:works ``f10!} pardon of sin, or\index{Good works:not
merit pardon of sin ``f10!} eternal life\index{eternal life ``f10!} at the hand of God, by reason of the great
disproportion\index{Good works:great disproportion compared with glory ``f10!} that is between them and the glory
to\index{Resurrection:believers:into glory:state of ``f10!} come; and the infinite\index{God's
attributes:infinite:separation from creatures ``f10!} distance\index{Mankind:great distance between him and God ``f10!}
that is between us and God, whom, by them, we can neither profit, nor satisfy for\index{Jesus:satisfied divine justice
``f10!} the debt\index{Forgiveness:of debtors ``f10!} of our former sins,\footnote{\ Romans 3:2\index{45 Romans:ch.  
3, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}0\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 4:2, 4, 6\index{45 Romans:ch.   4, v.   2,
4, 6, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 2:8\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}{}-9\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.  
8-9, pg. ``f30!}; Titus 3:5\index{56 Titus:ch.   3, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}{}-7\index{56 Titus:ch.   3, v.   5-7, pg.
``f30!}; Romans 8:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}8\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm
16:2\index{19 Psalms:ch.  16, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; Job 22:2-3\index{18 Job:ch.  22, v.   2-3, pg. ``f30!}; Job
35:7-8\index{18 Job:ch.  35, v.   7-8, pg. ``f30!}.} but when we have done all we can, we have done but our duty, and
are\index{God's law:commandments:duties:required by God ``f10!} unprofitable servants\index{Good works:duty of
unprofitable servants ``f10!};\footnote{\ Luke 17:10\index{42 Luke:ch.  17, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}.} and because, as they
are good, they proceed from His\index{Good works:only in Holy Spirit ``f10!} Spirit;\footnote{\ Galatians 5:2\index{48
Galatians:ch.   5, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}2-23\index{48 Galatians:ch.   5, v.  22-23, pg. ``f30!}.} and as they are wrought
by us, they are defiled, and\index{Good works:defiled ``f10!} mixed\index{Good works:mixed with weakness and
imperfection ``f10!} with so much weakness and\index{Sanctification:weaknesses and imperfections remain ``f10!}
imperfection, that they cannot endure the severity\index{Good works:cannot endure severity of God's judgement ``f10!}
of God's judgment\index{Judgement:severe ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Isaiah 64:6\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  64, v.   6, pg. ``f30!};
Galatians 5:1\index{48 Galatians:ch.   5, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}7\index{48 Galatians:ch.   5, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; Romans
7:15, 18\index{45 Romans:ch.   7, v.  15, 18, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 143:2\index{19 Psalms:ch. 143, v.   2, pg. ``f30!};
Psalm 130:3\index{19 Psalms:ch. 130, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}.} 


\bigskip

16.6\ \ Yet notwithstanding, the persons of believers being accepted through\index{Believers:accepted in Christ ``f10!}
Christ, their good works\index{Good works:adorn profession of faith ``f10!} also are accepted in Him\index{Good
works:accepted in Christ ``f10!},\footnote{\ Ephesians 1:6\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Peter
2:5\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   2, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}; Exodus 28:38\index{02 Exodus:ch.  28, v.  38, pg. ``f30!}; Genesis
4:4\index{01 Genesis:ch.   4, v.   4, pg. ``f30!} with Hebrews 11:4\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  11, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.} not
as though they were in this life wholly unblameable and unreproveable\index{Good works:not unreproveable ``f10!} in
God's sight;\footnote{\ Job 9:20\index{18 Job:ch.   9, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 143:2\index{19 Psalms:ch. 143, v.  
2, pg. ``f30!}.} but that He, looking upon them in His Son\index{Jesus:Son of God ``f10!}, is
pleased\index{Providence:at God's pleasure ``f10!} to accept and reward\index{Believers:rewarded by God ``f10!} that
which is sincere\index{Good works:sincere accepted by God ``f10!}, although accompanied with many
weaknesses\index{Sanctification:weaknesses and imperfections remain ``f10!} and
imperfections\index{Sanctification:imperfection in believers ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Hebrews 13:20-21\index{58 Hebrews:ch. 
13, v.  20-21, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Corinthians 8:1\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   8, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}2\index{47 2
Corinthians:ch.   8, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 6:10\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   6, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew
25:21\index{40 Matthew:ch.  25, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}, 23\index{40 Matthew:ch.  25, v.  21, 23, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

16.7\ \ Works done\index{Good works:not merit pardon of sin ``f10!} by unregenerate\index{Unbelievers:unregenerate
``f10!} men, although, for the matter of them, they may be things which God commands, and of\index{God's
law:commandments:obedience:not salvific ``f10!} good use both to themselves and others:\footnote{\ 2 Kings
10:30-31\index{12 2 Kings:ch.  10, v.  30-31, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Kings 21:27, 29\index{11 1 Kings:ch.  21, v.  27, 29, pg.
``f30!}; Philippians 1:1\index{50 Philippians:ch.   1, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}5-16, 18\index{50 Philippians:ch.   1, v. 
15-16, 18, pg. ``f30!}.} yet, because they proceed not\index{Good works:not from unregenerate ``f10!} from a
heart\index{Heart:new:purified ``f10!} purified by faith\index{Faith:false ``f10!};\footnote{\ Genesis 4:5\index{01
Genesis:ch.   4, v.   5, pg. ``f30!} with Hebrews 11:4\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  11, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}, 6\index{58
Hebrews:ch.  11, v.   4, 6, pg. ``f30!}.} nor are done in a right manner according to the Word;\index{Scripture:word of
God:standard for:life ``f10!}\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 13:3\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  13, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah
1:12\index{23 Isaiah:ch.   1, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}.} nor to a right end, the glory of God;\index{Good works:to be done
for the glory of God ``f10!}\footnote{\ Matthew 6:2, 5, 16\index{40 Matthew:ch.   6, v.   2, 5, 16, pg. ``f30!}.} they
are therefore sinful, and cannot please God\index{Good works:cannot please God ``f10!}, or make a man meet to receive
grace\index{Grace:received from God ``f10!} from God.\footnote{\ Haggai 2:14\index{37 Haggai:ch.   2, v.  14, pg.
``f30!}; Titus 1:15\index{56 Titus:ch.   1, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}; Amos 5:22-23\index{30 Amos:ch.   5, v.  22-23, pg.
``f30!}; Hosea 1:4\index{28 Hosea:ch.   1, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 9:16\index{45 Romans:ch.   9, v.  16, pg.
``f30!}; Titus 3:5\index{56 Titus:ch.   3, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.} And yet, their neglect of them\index{Good works:not be
negligent ``f10!} is more sinful, and displeasing unto God.\footnote{\ Psalm 14:4\index{19 Psalms:ch.  14, v.   4, pg.
``f30!}; Psalm 36:3\index{19 Psalms:ch.  36, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}; Job 21:14\index{18 Job:ch.  21, v.  14, pg.
``f30!}{}-15\index{18 Job:ch.  21, v.  14-15, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 25:41\index{40 Matthew:ch.  25, v.  41, pg.
``f30!}{}-43\index{40 Matthew:ch.  25, v.  41-43, pg. ``f30!}, 45\index{40 Matthew:ch.  25, v.  41-43, 45, pg. ``f30!};
Matthew 23:23\index{40 Matthew:ch.  23, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}.}

\section{Chapter 17 -- Of the Perseverance of the Saints}
\index{Perseverance:of the saints ``f10!}\index{Believers:saints ``f10!}17.1\ \ They, whom God has accepted in
His\index{Believers:accepted in Christ ``f10!} Beloved\index{Jesus:beloved of the Father ``f10!}, effectually
called\index{Effectual call:calling ``f10!}, and sanctified\index{Sanctification:sanctification ``f10!} by His Spirit,
can\index{Holy Spirit:applies:sanctification ``f10!} neither totally\index{Assurance:never fall from being saved
``f10!}, nor finally, fall away from the state of grace\index{Grace:state:fall from ``f10!}: but shall certainly
persevere\index{Perseverance:of the saints ``f10!} therein to the end, and be eternally\index{Salvation:eternal for
those effectually called ``f10!} saved.\footnote{\ Philippians 1:6\index{50 Philippians:ch.   1, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; 2
Peter 1:10\index{61 2 Peter:ch.   1, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; John 10:28\index{43 John:ch.  10, v.  28, pg.
``f30!}{}-29\index{43 John:ch.  10, v.  28-29, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 3:9\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}; 1
Peter 1:5\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   1, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}, 9\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   1, v.   5, 9, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

17.2\ \ This perseverance\index{Perseverance:of the saints ``f10!} of the saints\index{Believers:saints ``f10!} depends
not upon their\index{Perseverance:depends not on person's will ``f10!} own free will, but upon the
immutability\index{God's attributes:immutable ``f10!} of the decree\index{Predestination:eternal decrees ``f10!} of
election\index{Election:decree of ``f10!}, flowing from the free and unchangeable\index{God's attributes:unchangeable
``f10!} love of God\index{Love toward God:for God ``f10!} the Father\index{Father:God the ``f10!};\footnote{\ 2 Timothy
2:18-19\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   2, v.  18-19, pg. ``f30!}; Jeremiah 31:3\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  31, v.   3, pg.
``f30!}.} upon the efficacy\index{Perseverance:enabled by Holy Spirit ``f10!} of the merit
and\index{Jesus:obedience:merit of ``f10!} intercession\index{Jesus:in heaven:intercession made for all believers
``f10!} of Jesus Christ;\footnote{\ Hebrews 10:1\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  10, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}0\index{58 Hebrews:ch. 
10, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}, 14\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  10, v.  10, 14, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 13:20-21\index{58 Hebrews:ch. 
13, v.  20-21, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 9:12\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   9, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}{}-15\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   9,
v.  12-15, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 8:3\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}3\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.  33, pg.
``f30!} to the end, John 17:11, 24\index{43 John:ch.  17, v.  11, 24, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 22:32\index{42 Luke:ch.  22, v.
 32, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 7:25\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   7, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}.} the abiding of\index{Holy Spirit:abiding
in believers ``f10!} the Spirit, and of the seed of God\index{Believers:seed of God planted within ``f10!} within
them;\footnote{\ John 14:16-17\index{43 John:ch.  14, v.  16-17, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 2:2\index{62 1 John:ch.   2, v.  
2, pg. ``f30!}7\index{62 1 John:ch.   2, v.  27, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 3:9\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}.}
and the nature of the covenant of grace\index{Covenant:grace:grace ``f10!}:\footnote{\ Jeremiah 32:40\index{24
Jeremiah:ch.  32, v.  40, pg. ``f30!}.} from all which arises also the certainty and
infallibility\index{Covenant:grace:infallible ``f10!} thereof.\footnote{\ John 10:28\index{43 John:ch.  10, v.  28, pg.
``f30!}; 2 Thessalonians 3:3\index{53 2 Thessalonians:ch.   3, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 2:19\index{62 1 John:ch.  
2, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

17.3\ \ Nevertheless, they may, through the temptations\index{Temptation:temptation ``f10!} of Satan and
of\index{Satan:tempter ``f10!} the world, the prevalence of corruption remaining\index{Sanctification:remnants of
corruption remain ``f10!} in them, and the neglect of the means\index{Love for others:neighbour as self ``f10!} of
their preservation\index{Perseverance:means neglected ``f10!}, fall into grievous sins\index{Temptation:fall into
grievous sins ``f10!};\footnote{\ Matthew 26:70, 72, 74\index{40 Matthew:ch.  26, v.  70, 72, 74, pg. ``f30!}.} and,
for a time, continue therein:\footnote{\ Psalm 51 title and 14.} whereby they incur\index{Believers:may experience
God's displeasure for sin ``f10!} God's displeasure,\footnote{\ Isaiah 64:5, 7, 9\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  64, v.   5, 7,
9, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Samuel 11:27\index{10 2 Samuel:ch.  11, v.  27, pg. ``f30!}.} and grieve\index{Sin:grieves the Holy
Spirit ``f10!} His Holy Spirit\index{Holy Spirit:Holy Spirit ``f10!},\footnote{\ Ephesians 4:3\index{49 Ephesians:ch.  
4, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}0\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.  30, pg. ``f30!}.} come to be deprived of some measure of their
graces and\index{Grace:withheld ``f10!} comforts\index{Temptation:comforts removed ``f10!},\footnote{\ Psalm
51:8\index{19 Psalms:ch.  51, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}, 10, 12\index{19 Psalms:ch.  51, v.   8, 10, 12, pg. ``f30!};
Revelation 2:4\index{66 Revelation:ch.   2, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}; Song of Solomon 5:2-4, 6\index{22 Song of Solomon:ch. 
 5, v.   2-4, 6, pg. ``f30!}.} have their hearts hardened\index{Heart:hardened ``f10!},\footnote{\ Isaiah
63:17\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  63, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; Mark 6:52\index{41 Mark:ch.   6, v.  52, pg. ``f30!}; Mark
16:14\index{41 Mark:ch.  16, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}.} and their consciences\index{Conscience:wounded ``f10!}
wounded,\footnote{\ Psalm 32:3-4\index{19 Psalms:ch.  32, v.   3-4, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 51:8\index{19 Psalms:ch.  51, v.
  8, pg. ``f30!}.} hurt and scandalize\index{Scandalous behaviour:scandalize others ``f10!} others,\footnote{\ 2 Samuel
12:14\index{10 2 Samuel:ch.  12, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}.} and bring temporal judgments upon\index{Judgement:temporal
``f10!} themselves.\footnote{\ Psalm 89:31-32\index{19 Psalms:ch.  89, v.  31-32, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians
11:32\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  32, pg. ``f30!}.}

\paragraph[Chapter 18 {}-- Of the Assurance of Grace and Salvation]{Chapter 18 -- Of the Assurance of Grace and
Salvation}
\index{Assurance:of state of grace ``f10!}\index{Salvation:assurance of ``f10!}18.1\ \ Although
hypocrites\index{hypocrisy ``f10!} and other unregenerate\index{Unbelievers:unregenerate ``f10!} men may vainly
deceive\index{Deceitfulness:of self ``f10!} themselves with false hopes\index{Hope:false ``f10!}, and carnal
presumptions\index{presumption ``f10!} of being in the favour\index{Unbelievers:presumptuous about favour with God
``f10!} of God, and estate of salvation\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!};\footnote{\ Job
8:13-14\index{18 Job:ch.   8, v.  13-14, pg. ``f30!}; Micah 3:11\index{33 Micah:ch.   3, v.  11, pg. ``f30!};
Deuteronomy 29:19\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.  29, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}; John 8:41\index{43 John:ch.   8, v.  41, pg.
``f30!}.} which hope of theirs shall perish:\footnote{\ Matthew 7:22\index{40 Matthew:ch.   7, v.  22, pg.
``f30!}{}-23\index{40 Matthew:ch.   7, v.  22-23, pg. ``f30!}.} yet such as truly believe in the Lord Jesus, and love
Him\index{Love toward God:for God ``f10!} in sincerity\index{Love:of Christ ``f10!}, endeavouring to walk in
all\index{Believers:strive to walk in good conscience ``f10!} good conscience\index{Conscience:good, endeavour for
``f10!} before Him, may, in this life, be certainly assured that\index{Assurance:of state of grace ``f10!} they are in
the state of grace\index{Grace:state:believers in ``f10!},\footnote{\ 1 John 2:3\index{62 1 John:ch.   2, v.   3, pg.
``f30!}; 1 John 3:1\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}4\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}, 18-19,
21, 24\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.  14, 18-19, 21, 24, pg. ``f30!}; John 5:13\index{43 John:ch.   5, v.  13, pg.
``f30!}.} and may rejoice in the hope of\index{Hope:of glory of God, rejoice in ``f10!} the glory of God,
which\index{Resurrection:believers:into glory:everlasting ``f10!} hope shall\index{Hope:certain ``f10!} never make them
ashamed\index{Believers:never made ashamed by God ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Romans 5:2\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.   2, pg.
``f30!}, 5\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.   2, 5, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

18.2\ \ This certainty is not a bare conjectural\index{Assurance:not bare conjecture ``f10!} and probable
persuasion\index{Assurance:not probable persuasion ``f10!}, grounded upon a fallible hope;\index{Hope:fallible
``f10!}\footnote{\ Hebrews 6:11, 19\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   6, v.  11, 19, pg. ``f30!}.} but an
infallible\index{Assurance:infallible ``f10!} assurance of faith\index{Assurance:of faith ``f10!},
founded\index{Assurance:founded on God's promises ``f10!} upon the divine\index{Salvation:founded on divine truth
``f10!} truth of the promises\index{Salvation:promises made ``f10!} of salvation\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by
faith ``f10!},\footnote{\ Hebrews 6:17\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   6, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}{}-18\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   6, v. 
17-18, pg. ``f30!}.} the inward evidence\index{Assurance:inward evidence ``f10!} of those graces\index{Grace:in
believers:by Holy Spirit ``f10!} unto which these promises\index{Assurance:promises of God ``f10!} are
made,\footnote{\ 2 Peter 1:4-5, 10-11\index{61 2 Peter:ch.   1, v.   4-5, 10-11, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 2:3\index{62 1
John:ch.   2, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 3:1\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}4\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.
 14, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Corinthians 1:1\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   1, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}2\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.  
1, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}.} the testimony of the Spirit\index{Assurance:Holy Spirit witnesses with our spirits ``f10!} of
adoption\index{Adoption:in salvation ``f10!} witnessing with our spirits\index{Conversion:Holy Spirit:bears witness to
our spirits ``f10!} that we are the children of God:\footnote{\ Romans 8:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   1, pg.
``f30!}5\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}{}-16\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.  15-16, pg. ``f30!}.} which
Spirit\index{Holy Spirit:earnest of believers' inheritance ``f10!} is the earnest
of\index{Believers:inheritance:earnest of ``f10!} our inheritance\index{Believers:inheritance:everlasting ``f10!},
whereby we are sealed to the\index{Salvation:sealed to the day of redemption ``f10!} day of
redemption\index{Redemption:day of ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Ephesians 1:1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   1, pg.
``f30!}3\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}{}-14\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.  13-14, pg. ``f30!};
Ephesians 4:3\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}0\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.  30, pg. ``f30!}; 2
Corinthians 1:21-22\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   1, v.  21-22, pg. ``f30!}.}

18.3\ \ This infallible\index{Assurance:infallible ``f10!} assurance does\index{Assurance:believer may await ``f10!} not
so belong to the essence of faith\index{Faith:essence of ``f10!}, but that a true believer may wait long, and conflict
with many difficulties\index{Assurance:believer may experience difficulties ``f10!} before he be partaker of
it:\footnote{\ 1 John 5:13\index{62 1 John:ch.   5, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 50:10\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  50, v.  10,
pg. ``f30!}; Mark 9:24\index{41 Mark:ch.   9, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 88:1-18\index{19 Psalms:ch.  88, v.   1-18,
pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 77:1-12\index{19 Psalms:ch.  77, v.   1-12, pg. ``f30!}.} yet, being enabled
by\index{Assurance:enabled by Holy Spirit ``f10!} the Spirit to\index{Revelation:Word and Spirit ``f10!} know the
things which are freely\index{Salvation:freely offered ``f10!} given him of God, he may without extraordinary
revelation\index{Revelation:extraordinary ``f10!}, in the right use of ordinary means, attain thereunto.\footnote{\ 1
Corinthians 2:12\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   2, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 4:1\index{62 1 John:ch.   4, v.   1, pg.
``f30!}3\index{62 1 John:ch.   4, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 6:11-12\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   6, v.  11-12, pg.
``f30!}; Ephesians 3:17\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   3, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}{}-19\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   3, v.  17-19, pg.
``f30!}.} And therefore it is the duty of everyone\index{Election:duty to make calling sure ``f10!} to give all
diligence to\index{Election:diligence to make calling sure ``f10!} make his calling and\index{Effectual call:elect
``f10!} election sure;\footnote{\ 2 Peter 1:10\index{61 2 Peter:ch.   1, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}.} that thereby his heart
may be enlarged\index{Heart:enlarged in peace and joy ``f10!} in peace\index{Assurance:peace and joy ``f10!} and joy
in\index{Joy:in Holy Spirit ``f10!} the Holy Ghost\index{Holy Spirit:Holy Ghost ``f10!}, in love and\index{Love toward
God:for God ``f10!} thankfulness\index{Prayer:thanking God ``f10!} to God, and in strength\index{Sanctification:supply
of strength from Holy Spirit ``f10!} and cheerfulness\index{cheerfulness ``f10!} in the duties of obedience,
the\index{God's law:commandments:obedience:required ``f10!} proper fruits\index{Good works:fruit of salvation ``f10!}
of this assurance:\index{Assurance:not to be used to justify sin ``f10!}\footnote{\ Romans 5:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   5,
v.   1, pg. ``f30!}{}-2\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.   1-2, pg. ``f30!}, 5\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.   1-2, 5, pg.
``f30!}; Romans 14:17\index{45 Romans:ch.  14, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 15:13\index{45 Romans:ch.  15, v.  13, pg.
``f30!}; Ephesians 1:3-4\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   3-4, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 4:6-7\index{19 Psalms:ch.   4, v.  
6-7, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 119:32\index{19 Psalms:ch. 119, v.  32, pg. ``f30!}.} so far is it from inclining men to
looseness.\footnote{\ 1 John 2:1-2\index{62 1 John:ch.   2, v.   1-2, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 6:1-2\index{45 Romans:ch.  
6, v.   1-2, pg. ``f30!}; Titus 2:11-12, 14\index{56 Titus:ch.   2, v.  11-12, 14, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Corinthians
7:1\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   7, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 8:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   1, pg. ``f30!},
12\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   1, 12, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 3:2\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.   2, pg.
``f30!}{}-3\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.   2-3, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 130:4\index{19 Psalms:ch. 130, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}; 1
John 1:6-7\index{62 1 John:ch.   1, v.   6-7, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

18.4\ \ True believers may\index{Assurance:believer may not have at all times ``f10!} have the assurance of their
salvation\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!} divers ways shaken\index{Assurance:shaken at times ``f10!},
diminished, and intermitted; as, by negligence\index{Assurance:negligence in preserving ``f10!} in
preserving\index{Perseverance:means neglected ``f10!} of it, by falling\index{God's law:broken daily by believers
``f10!} into some special sin, which wounds the conscience\index{Conscience:wounded ``f10!} and grieves
the\index{Sin:grieves the Holy Spirit ``f10!} Spirit; by some sudden\index{Temptation:sudden ``f10!} or
vehement\index{Temptation:vehement ``f10!} temptation\index{Temptation:temptation ``f10!}, by God's withdrawing the
light of His countenance\index{Believers:chastened by God ``f10!}, and suffering even such as fear Him\index{Fear:of
God:reverence ``f10!} to walk in darkness\index{darkness, spiritual ``f10!} and to have no light:\footnote{\ Song of
Solomon 5:2-3, 6\index{22 Song of Solomon:ch.   5, v.   2-3, 6, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 51:8\index{19 Psalms:ch.  51, v.  
8, pg. ``f30!}, 12\index{19 Psalms:ch.  51, v.   8, 12, pg. ``f30!}, 14\index{19 Psalms:ch.  51, v.   8, 12, 14, pg.
``f30!}; Ephesians 4:3\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}0\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.  30, pg.
``f30!}{}-31\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.  30-31, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 77:1-10\index{19 Psalms:ch.  77, v.   1-10, pg.

\section{Chapter 19 -- Of the Law of God}
19.1\ \ God gave to Adam a law\index{Adam:given a law ``f10!}, as a covenant of works\index{Covenant:works:works
``f10!}, by which He bound him and all his posterity\index{Sin:original:all mankind descending from Adam ``f10!} to
personal, entire, exact, and perpetual obedience\index{Covenant:works:perpetual obedience required ``f10!}; promised
life\index{Covenant:first:promised life ``f10!} upon the fulfilling, and\index{Covenant:works:conditional on perfect
obedience ``f10!} threatened death\index{Death:punishment for sin ``f10!} upon the breach of it\index{God's
law:breach:death threatened ``f10!}: and endued him\index{Mankind:created:attributes ``f10!} with power and ability to
keep\index{Covenant:works:Adam:original ability and power to keep ``f10!} it.\footnote{\ Genesis 1:2\index{01
Genesis:ch.   1, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}6\index{01 Genesis:ch.   1, v.  26, pg. ``f30!}{}-27\index{01 Genesis:ch.   1, v. 
26-27, pg. ``f30!} with Genesis 2:17\index{01 Genesis:ch.   2, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 2:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   2,
v.   1, pg. ``f30!}4-15\index{45 Romans:ch.   2, v.  14-15, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 10:5\index{45 Romans:ch.  10, v.   5,
pg. ``f30!}; Romans 5:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}2\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.  12, pg. ``f30!},
19\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.  12, 19, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 3:10\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.  10, pg. ``f30!},
12\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.  10, 12, pg. ``f30!}; Ecclesiastes 7:2\index{21 Ecclesiastes:ch.   7, v.   2, pg.
``f30!}9\index{21 Ecclesiastes:ch.   7, v.  29, pg. ``f30!}; Job 28:28\index{18 Job:ch.  28, v.  28, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

19.2\ \ This law, after his fall\index{Sin:original:first transgression (of Adam) ``f10!}, continued to be a perfect
rule of righteousness, and, as\index{God's law:righteous requirements ``f10!} such, was delivered by\index{God's
law:commandments:delivered on Sinai ``f10!} God upon Mount Sinai\index{Sinai, mount ``f10!}, in ten\index{God's
law:commandments:ten ``f10!} commandments, and written in two tables\index{God's law:commandments:two tables
``f10!}:\footnote{\index{59 James:ch.   1, v.  25, pg.
``f30!}{,
10-12}\index{59 James:ch.   2, v.   8, 10-12, pg. ``f30!}\index{45 Romans:ch. 
13, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}\index{45 Romans:ch.  13, v.   8-9, pg.
``f30!}\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.   5, v.  32, pg.
``f30!}\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.  10, v.   4, pg.
``f30!}
the four first commandment\index{God's law:commandments:first ``f10!}s\index{God's law:commandments:first four, duty to
God ``f10!} containing our duty towards\index{God's law:commandments:duties:required by God ``f10!} God; and the other
six\index{Sabbath:six days:for own affairs ``f10!} our duty to man\index{God's law:commandments:duties:to others
``f10!}.\footnote{\ Matthew 22:37-40\index{40 Matthew:ch.  22, v.  37-40, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

19.3\ \ Beside this law, commonly called moral\index{God's law:commandments:moral ``f10!}, God was
pleased\index{Providence:at God's pleasure ``f10!} to give to the people of Israel\index{Israel ``f10!}, as a
church\index{Church:OT ``f10!} under age, ceremonial\index{Ceremonial law:fore-signifying Christ ``f10!} laws,
containing several typical\index{types, OT ``f10!} ordinances, partly\index{Covenant:OT ordinances:signified Christ
``f10!} of worship\index{Worship:of God ``f10!}, prefiguring\index{Jesus:prefigured in ceremonial ordinances ``f10!}
Christ, His graces\index{Jesus:full of grace ``f10!}, actions, sufferings, and\index{Jesus:death:sufferings and death
``f10!} benefits;\footnote{\ Hebrews chap. 9; Hebrews 10:1\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  10, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians
4:1-3\index{48 Galatians:ch.   4, v.   1-3, pg. ``f30!}; Colossians 2:17\index{51 Colossians:ch.   2, v.  17, pg.
``f30!}.} and partly holding\index{God's law:benefits ``f10!} forth divers instructions of moral duties.\index{God's
law:commandments:duties:required by God ``f10!}\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 5:7\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   5, v.   7,
pg. ``f30!}; 2 Corinthians 6:17\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   6, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; Jude 23\index{65 Jude:v.  23, pg.
``f30!}.} All which ceremonial laws are now abrogated\index{Ceremonial law:abrogated ``f10!}, under the new
testament\index{Scripture:New Testament ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Colossians 2:14, 16-17\index{51 Colossians:ch.   2, v.  14,
16-17, pg. ``f30!}; Daniel 9:27\index{27 Daniel:ch.   9, v.  27, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 2:1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2,
v.   1, pg. ``f30!}5-16\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.  15-16, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

19.4\ \ To them also, as a body politic, He gave sundry judicial laws, which expired\index{God's law:judicial:expired
``f10!} together with the State of that people; not obliging any other now, further than the general equity
thereof\index{God's law:judicial:apply equity today ``f10!} may require.\footnote{\ Exodus chap. 21; Exodus
22:1-29\index{02 Exodus:ch.  22, v.   1-29, pg. ``f30!}; Genesis 49:10\index{01 Genesis:ch.  49, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}
with 1 Peter 2:13\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   2, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}{}-14\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   2, v.  13-14, pg. ``f30!};
Matthew 5:17\index{40 Matthew:ch.   5, v.  17, pg. ``f30!} with Matthew 5:38-39\index{40 Matthew:ch.   5, v.  38-39,
pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 9:8-10\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   9, v.   8-10, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

19.5\ \ The moral\index{God's law:commandments:moral ``f10!} law does for ever bind all\index{God's law:binding on all
men ``f10!}, as well justified\index{Justification:justified ``f10!} persons as others, to the obedience
thereof\index{God's law:commandments:obedience:required ``f10!};\footnote{\ Romans 13:8\index{45 Romans:ch.  13, v.  
8, pg. ``f30!}{}-10\index{45 Romans:ch.  13, v.   8-10, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 6:2\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   6, v.   2,

pg. ``f30!}.} and that, not only in regard of the matter contained in it, but also in respect of the authority of God
the Creator\index{God's attributes:creator:of all things ``f10!}, who gave it:\footnote{\ James 2:10\index{59 James:ch.
  2, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}{}-11\index{59 James:ch.   2, v.  10-11, pg. ``f30!}.} neither does Christ, in the
Gospel\index{Gospel:gospel ``f10!}, any way dissolve, but much strengthen this obligation\index{God's law:obligation to
obey:strengthened by Gospel ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Matthew 5:17\index{40 Matthew:ch.   5, v.  17, pg.
``f30!}{}-19\index{40 Matthew:ch.   5, v.  17-19, pg. ``f30!}; James 2:8\index{59 James:ch.   2, v.   8, pg. ``f30!};
Romans 3:31\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.  31, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

19.6\ \ Although true believers\index{Covenant:works:believers not under ``f10!} be not under the law, as a covenant of
works\index{Covenant:works:works ``f10!}, to be thereby justified\index{Justification:justified ``f10!}, or
condemned\index{Covenant:works:believers delivered from ``f10!};\footnote{\ Romans 6:14\index{45 Romans:ch.   6, v. 
14, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 2:16\index{48 Galatians:ch.   2, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 3:13\index{48 Galatians:ch. 
 3, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 4:4\index{48 Galatians:ch.   4, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}{}-5\index{48 Galatians:ch.   4,
v.   4-5, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 13:3\index{44 Acts:ch.  13, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}9\index{44 Acts:ch.  13, v.  39, pg.
``f30!}; Romans 8:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}.} yet is it of great use to them, as well as to
others; in that, as a rule of life\index{God's law:moral:rule for life ``f10!} informing them of the will of God, and
their duty, it\index{God's law:commandments:duties:required by God ``f10!} directs, and binds them\index{God's
law:binding on all men ``f10!} to walk accordingly;\footnote{\ Romans 7:12\index{45 Romans:ch.   7, v.  12, pg.
``f30!}, 22, 25\index{45 Romans:ch.   7, v.  12, 22, 25, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 119:4-6\index{19 Psalms:ch. 119, v.   4-6,
pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 7:19\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   7, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 5:1\index{48
Galatians:ch.   5, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}4, 16, 18-23\index{48 Galatians:ch.   5, v.  14, 16, 18-23, pg. ``f30!}.}
discovering also the sinful pollutions\index{Sin:original:corrupt nature:polluted ``f10!} of their nature, hearts, and
lives\index{Heart:polluted ``f10!};\footnote{\ Romans 7:7\index{45 Romans:ch.   7, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}; Romans
3:2\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}0\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}.} so as,
examining\index{God's law:examine self against ``f10!} themselves thereby, they may come to further
conviction\index{God's law:conviction of sin furthered ``f10!} of, humiliation for\index{Humility:before God ``f10!},
and hatred against\index{Sin:to be hated ``f10!} sin;\footnote{\ James 1:23-25\index{59 James:ch.   1, v.  23-25, pg.
``f30!}; Romans 7:9, 14, 24\index{45 Romans:ch.   7, v.   9, 14, 24, pg. ``f30!}.} together with a clearer sight of the
need they have of Christ, and the perfection of His obedience\index{Jesus:obedience:to God's law
``f10!}.\footnote{\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.  24, pg.
``f30!}\index{45 Romans:ch.   7, v.  24-25, pg.
``f30!}\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   3, pg.
``f30!} It is
likewise of use to the regenerate\index{Regeneration:regeneration ``f10!}, to restrain their corruptions,
in\index{God's law:restrains corruptions ``f10!} that it forbids\index{God's law:forbids sin ``f10!}
sin:\footnote{\index{59 James:ch.   2, v.  11, pg.
``f30!}\index{19 Psalms:ch. 119, v. 101, 104, 128, pg.
``f30!} of it
serve to show what even their sins deserve\index{Sin:deserves damnation ``f10!}; and what afflictions, in\index{God's
law:breach:define afflictions imposed on sin ``f10!} this life, they may expect for them, although
freed\index{Believers:freed from:curse of the law ``f10!} from the curse thereof\index{Curse:of the law ``f10!}
threatened in\index{God's law:commandments:threatenings for disobedience ``f10!} the law.\footnote{\ Ezra
9:13-14\index{15 Ezra:ch.   9, v.  13-14, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 89:30-34\index{19 Psalms:ch.  89, v.  30-34, pg. ``f30!}.}
The promises\index{God's law:promises ``f10!} of it, in like manner, show them God's approbation\index{God's
law:approbation for obedience ``f10!} of obedience, and\index{Believers:obedience:rewarded ``f10!} what blessings
they\index{Believers:blessed in/by God ``f10!} may expect upon the performance thereof;\footnote{\ Leviticus
26:1-14\index{03 Leviticus:ch.  26, v.   1-14, pg. ``f30!} with 2 Corinthians 6:16\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   6, v. 
16, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 6:2\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   6, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}{}-3\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   6, v.  
2-3, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 37:11\index{19 Psalms:ch.  37, v.  11, pg. ``f30!} with Matthew 5:5\index{40 Matthew:ch.   5,
v.   5, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 19:11\index{19 Psalms:ch.  19, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}.} although not as due to them by the law,
as a covenant of works.\footnote{\ Galatians 2:16\index{48 Galatians:ch.   2, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 17:10\index{42
Luke:ch.  17, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}.} So as, a man's doing good, and refraining from evil\index{God's
law:commandments:obedience:refraining from evil ``f10!}, because the law encourages to the one and
deterrers\index{God's law:deterrence from sin ``f10!} from the other, is no evidence of his being under the law; and
not under grace\index{Grace:in believers:by Holy Spirit ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Romans 6:12, 14\index{45 Romans:ch.   6, v.
 12, 14, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Peter 3:8-12\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   3, v.   8-12, pg. ``f30!} with Psalm 34:1\index{19
Psalms:ch.  34, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}2-16\index{19 Psalms:ch.  34, v.  12-16, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 12:2\index{58
Hebrews:ch.  12, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}8\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  12, v.  28, pg. ``f30!}{}-29\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  12, v. 
28-29, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

19.7\ \ Neither are the forementioned uses of the law contrary to the grace of\index{Grace:of Gospel ``f10!} the
Gospel\index{Gospel:gospel ``f10!}, but do sweetly comply\index{God's law:compliance with help of Holy Spirit ``f10!}
with it;\footnote{\ Galatians 3:21\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}.} the Spirit of Christ\index{Holy
Spirit:Spirit of Christ ``f10!} subduing and\index{Holy Spirit:subdues will of man ``f10!} enabling the\index{God's
law:commandments:obedience:enabled by Holy Spirit ``f10!} will of man to do that, freely\index{Causation:will of
creatures:free ``f10!} and cheerfully\index{cheerfulness ``f10!}, which the will of God, revealed in the
law\index{Revelation:God's will ``f10!}, requires to be\index{God's law:commandments:duties:required by God ``f10!}
done.\footnote{\ Ezekiel 36:27\index{26 Ezekiel:ch.  36, v.  27, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 8:10\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   8, v.
 10, pg. ``f30!} with Jeremiah 31:3\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  31, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}3\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  31, v.  33,
pg. ``f30!}.}

\paragraph[Chapter 20 {}-- Of Christian Liberty, and Liberty of Conscience]{Chapter 20 -- Of Christian Liberty, and
Liberty of Conscience}
\index{Christian liberty:defined ``f10!}\index{Conscience:liberty of:defined ``f10!}20.1\ \ The liberty
which\index{Christian liberty:purchased by Christ ``f10!} Christ has purchased\index{Redemption:purchased by Christ
``f10!} for believers under\index{Christian liberty:believers under the Gospel ``f10!} the Gospel\index{Gospel:gospel
``f10!} consists in their freedom\index{Believers:freed from:guilt of sin ``f10!} from the guilt\index{guilt ``f10!} of
sin, and condemning\index{Punishment:condemnation ``f10!} wrath of God\index{Wrath:of God:for sin ``f10!}, the curse of
the\index{Curse:of the law ``f10!} moral\index{God's law:commandments:moral ``f10!} law;\footnote{\ Titus 2:14\index{56
Titus:ch.   2, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Thessalonians 1:10\index{52 1 Thessalonians:ch.   1, v.  10, pg. ``f30!};
Galatians 3:13\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}.} and, in their being delivered from
this\index{Believers:delivered from:this evil world ``f10!} present evil\index{Christian liberty:deliverance from evil
world ``f10!} world, bondage to Satan\index{Satan:bondage to ``f10!}, and dominion of sin\index{Christian
liberty:dominion of sin destroyed ``f10!};\footnote{\ Galatians 1:4\index{48 Galatians:ch.   1, v.   4, pg. ``f30!};
Colossians 1:13\index{51 Colossians:ch.   1, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 26:18\index{44 Acts:ch.  26, v.  18, pg.
``f30!}; Romans 6:14\index{45 Romans:ch.   6, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}.} from the evil of afflictions,
the\index{Salvation:release from evil afflictions ``f10!} sting of death\index{Death:believers:delivered from sting of
``f10!}, the victory of\index{Death:defeated by Christ ``f10!} the grave, and
everlasting\index{Punishment:everlasting:damnation ``f10!} damnation;\footnote{\ Romans 8:2\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.
  2, pg. ``f30!}8\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.  28, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 119:71\index{19 Psalms:ch. 119, v.  71, pg.
``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 15:54-57\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  15, v.  54-57, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 8:1\index{45 Romans:ch. 
 8, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}.} as also, in their free access to God\index{Believers:access to God only through Christ
``f10!},\footnote{\ Romans 5:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}{}-2\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.   1-2, pg.
``f30!}.} and their yielding\index{God's law:commandments:obedience:required ``f10!} obedience unto Him, not out of
slavish\index{God's law:commandments:obedience:not of slavish fear ``f10!} fear, but\index{Fear:slavish ``f10!} a
child-like\index{Love toward God:childlike ``f10!} love and willing mind.\index{God's
law:commandments:obedience:willing mind ``f10!}\footnote{\ Romans 8:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   1, pg.
``f30!}4-15\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.  14-15, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 4:1\index{62 1 John:ch.   4, v.   1, pg.
``f30!}8\index{62 1 John:ch.   4, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}.} All which were common also to believers under\index{Christian
liberty:believers under the law ``f10!} the law.\footnote{\ Galatians 3:9, 14\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.   9, 14,
pg. ``f30!}.} But, under the new testament\index{Scripture:New Testament ``f10!}, the liberty of
Christians\index{Christian liberty:enlarged under NT economy ``f10!} is further enlarged, in
their\index{Believers:freed from:yoke of the law ``f10!} freedom from the yoke\index{Ceremonial law:yoke ``f10!} of the
ceremonial\index{Ceremonial law:fore-signifying Christ ``f10!} law, to which the Jewish\index{Church:Jewish ``f10!}
Church was subjected\index{Ceremonial law:subjected Jewish Church ``f10!};\footnote{\ Galatians 4:1-3\index{48
Galatians:ch.   4, v.   1-3, pg. ``f30!}, 6-7\index{48 Galatians:ch.   4, v.   1-3, 6-7, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians
5:1\index{48 Galatians:ch.   5, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 15:10-11\index{44 Acts:ch.  15, v.  10-11, pg. ``f30!}.} and
in greater boldness\index{Prayer:with boldness ``f10!} of access to the\index{Believers:bold access to God's throne
``f10!} throne of grace\index{Grace:throne of ``f10!},\footnote{\ Hebrews 4:14, 16\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   4, v.  14,
16, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 10:1\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  10, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}9-22\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  10, v.  19-22,
pg. ``f30!}.} and in fuller communications of the free Spirit\index{Holy Spirit:instructs the elect ``f10!} of God,
than believers under the law did ordinarily partake\index{Believers:benefits:in this life ``f10!} of.\footnote{\ John
7:38-39\index{43 John:ch.   7, v.  38-39, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Corinthians 3:13, 17-18\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   3, v. 
13, 17-18, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

20.2\ \ God alone is Lord of the conscience\index{Conscience:God alone lord of ``f10!},\footnote{\ James 4:12\index{59
James:ch.   4, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 14:4\index{45 Romans:ch.  14, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.} and has left it free
from the doctrines\index{Doctrine:false:of men ``f10!} and commandments\index{Commandments of men:false ``f10!} of men,
which are in any thing contrary to His Word; or beside it, in matters of faith\index{Faith:contrary opinions to the
``f10!} or worship\index{Worship:of God ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Acts 4:19\index{44 Acts:ch.   4, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}; Acts
5:2\index{44 Acts:ch.   5, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}9\index{44 Acts:ch.   5, v.  29, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 7:23\index{46
1 Corinthians:ch.   7, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 23:8-10\index{40 Matthew:ch.  23, v.   8-10, pg. ``f30!}; 2
Corinthians 1:24\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   1, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 15:9\index{40 Matthew:ch.  15, v.   9,
pg. ``f30!}.} So that, to believe such doctrines, or to obey such commands, out of
conscience\index{Conscience:influenced falsely by others ``f10!},\footnote{\ Colossians 2:2\index{51 Colossians:ch.  
2, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}0, 22-23\index{51 Colossians:ch.   2, v.  20, 22-23, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 1:10\index{48
Galatians:ch.   1, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 2:4-5\index{48 Galatians:ch.   2, v.   4-5, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians
5:1\index{48 Galatians:ch.   5, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}.} is to betray true liberty of conscience\index{Conscience:liberty
of:defined ``f10!}: and the requiring\index{Salvation:faith alone required ``f10!} of an implicit\index{Faith:implicit
``f10!} faith, and an absolute\index{Conscience:liberty of:not absolute obedience when contrary to God's Word ``f10!}
and blind obedience is to destroy\index{Conscience:liberty of:destroyed ``f10!} liberty of conscience, and reason
also.\footnote{\ Romans 10:1\index{45 Romans:ch.  10, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}7\index{45 Romans:ch.  10, v.  17, pg.
``f30!}; Romans 14:23\index{45 Romans:ch.  14, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 8:20\index{23 Isaiah:ch.   8, v.  20, pg.
``f30!}; Acts 17:11\index{44 Acts:ch.  17, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}; John 4:22\index{43 John:ch.   4, v.  22, pg. ``f30!};
Hosea 5:11\index{28 Hosea:ch.   5, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}; Revelation 13:12, 16-17\index{66 Revelation:ch.  13, v.  12,
16-17, pg. ``f30!}; Jeremiah 8:9\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.   8, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

20.3\ \ They who, upon pretence\index{pretence ``f10!} of Christian liberty\index{Christian liberty:defined ``f10!}, do
practice any sin, or cherish any lust\index{Sexual immorality:lust ``f10!}, do thereby destroy
the\index{Conscience:liberty of:destroyed ``f10!} end of Christian liberty, which is, that being delivered
out\index{Believers:delivered from:hands of enemies ``f10!} of the hands of our enemies\index{Enemies:believers
delivered from ``f10!}, we might serve the\index{Love toward God:in service ``f10!} Lord, without fear\index{Fear:none
``f10!}, in holiness and\index{Believers:holy:being perfected ``f10!} righteousness before\index{Believers:to serve God
in righteousness ``f10!} Him, all the days of our life.\footnote{\ Galatians 5:1\index{48 Galatians:ch.   5, v.   1,
pg. ``f30!}3\index{48 Galatians:ch.   5, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Peter 2:16\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   2, v.  16, pg.
``f30!}; 2 Peter 2:19\index{61 2 Peter:ch.   2, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}; John 8:34\index{43 John:ch.   8, v.  34, pg.
``f30!}; Luke 1:74-75\index{42 Luke:ch.   1, v.  74-75, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

20.4\ \ And because the powers which God has ordained, and\index{Civil magistrate:ordained by God ``f10!} the liberty
which\index{Christian liberty:purchased by Christ ``f10!} Christ has purchased\index{Redemption:purchased by Christ
``f10!}, are not intended by God to destroy\index{Conscience:liberty of:destroyed ``f10!}, but mutually to uphold
and\index{Christian liberty:upholds just laws of men ``f10!} preserve one\index{Human life:preservation ``f10!}
another; they who, upon pretence\index{pretence ``f10!} of Christian liberty\index{Christian liberty:defined ``f10!},
shall oppose\index{Liberty:not oppose lawful governance ``f10!} any lawful power, or the lawful exercise of it, whether
it be civil or ecclesiastical\index{Church government:ecclesiastical powers not to be resisted ``f10!}, resist the
ordinance of\index{Worship:ordinances:to be:esteemed ``f10!} God.\footnote{\ Matthew 12:25\index{40 Matthew:ch.  12, v.
 25, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Peter 2:13\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   2, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}{}-14\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   2, v.  13-14,
pg. ``f30!}, 16\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   2, v.  13-14, 16, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 13:1\index{45 Romans:ch.  13, v.   1, pg.
``f30!}{}-8\index{45 Romans:ch.  13, v.   1-8, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 13:17\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  13, v.  17, pg.
``f30!}.} And, for their publishing\index{Church discipline:for opinions contrary to truth ``f10!} of such opinions, or
maintaining of such practices, as are contrary to the light of nature, or to the known principles of
Christianity\index{Christianity ``f10!}, whether concerning faith\index{Faith:contrary opinions to the ``f10!},
worship, or\index{Worship:of God ``f10!} conversation\index{Believers:to walk faithfully in obedience (conversation)
``f10!}; or, to the power of godliness\index{God's attributes:power of godliness ``f10!}; or, such
erroneous\index{Falsehood:false opinions ``f10!} opinions or practices, as either in their own nature, or in the manner
of publishing or maintaining them, are destructive\index{Heresy:heresies ``f10!} to the
external\index{Heresy:destructive or external peace of Church ``f10!} peace and order\index{Church:to maintain peace
and order ``f10!} which Christ has established\index{Church:order established by Christ ``f10!} in the Church,
they\index{Church:institution ``f10!} may lawfully be\index{Church discipline:heresies lawfully censured ``f10!} called
to account, and proceeded against by the censures of\index{Church discipline:censures ``f10!} the
Church,\footnote{\ Romans 1:32\index{45 Romans:ch.   1, v.  32, pg. ``f30!} with 1 Corinthians 5:1\index{46 1
Corinthians:ch.   5, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}, 5, 11, 13\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   5, v.   1, 5, 11, 13, pg. ``f30!}; 2
John 10-11\index{63 2 John:v. 10-11, pg. ``f30!} and 2 Thessalonians 3:1\index{53 2 Thessalonians:ch.   3, v.   1, pg.
``f30!}4\index{53 2 Thessalonians:ch.   3, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Timothy 6:3\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   6, v.   3, pg.
``f30!}{}-5\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   6, v.   3-5, pg. ``f30!}; Titus 1:10-11, 13\index{56 Titus:ch.   1, v.  10-11, 13,
pg. ``f30!}; Titus 3:1\index{56 Titus:ch.   3, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}0\index{56 Titus:ch.   3, v.  10, pg. ``f30!} with
Matthew 18:15\index{40 Matthew:ch.  18, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}{}-17\index{40 Matthew:ch.  18, v.  15-17, pg. ``f30!}; 1
Timothy 1:19-20\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   1, v.  19-20, pg. ``f30!}; Revelation 2:2, 14-15, 20\index{66 Revelation:ch.  
2, v.   2, 14-15, 20, pg. ``f30!}; Revelation 3:9\index{66 Revelation:ch.   3, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}.} and by the power
of the civil magistrate\index{Civil magistrate:to punish evil doers ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Deuteronomy 13:6-12\index{05
Deuteronomy:ch.  13, v.   6-12, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 13:3\index{45 Romans:ch.  13, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}{}-4\index{45
Romans:ch.  13, v.   3-4, pg. ``f30!} with 2 John 10-11\index{63 2 John:v. 10-11, pg. ``f30!}; Ezra 7:23,
25-28\index{15 Ezra:ch.   7, v.  23, 25-28, pg. ``f30!}; Revelation 17:12, 16-17\index{66 Revelation:ch.  17, v.  12,
16-17, pg. ``f30!}; Nehemiah 13:15, 17\index{16 Nehemiah:ch.  13, v.  15, 17, pg. ``f30!}, 21-22, 25, 30\index{16

9, 20-21, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Chronicles 34:33\index{14 2 Chronicles:ch.  34, v.  33, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Chronicles

\paragraph[Chapter 21 {}-- Of Religious Worship and the Sabbath Day]{Chapter 21 -- Of Religious Worship and the Sabbath
Day}
\index{Worship:glorifying God ``f10!}\index{Worship:on the Sabbath ``f10!}\index{Sabbath:for worship ``f10!}21.1\ \ The
light of nature shows\index{Revelation:natural:declares there is a God ``f10!} that there is a God, who has
lordship\index{God's attributes:sovereign lordship ``f10!} and sovereignty over all, is good, and does good unto all,
and is therefore to be feared\index{Fear:of God:reverence ``f10!}, loved\index{Love toward God:for God ``f10!},
praised\index{Worship:praising God ``f10!}, called upon, trusted\index{trust in God ``f10!} in, and served\index{Love
toward God:in service ``f10!}, with all the heart, and with all the soul\index{Love toward God:with all our:soul
``f10!}, and with all the might.\footnote{\ Romans 1:20\index{45 Romans:ch.   1, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}; Acts
17:24\index{44 Acts:ch.  17, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 119:68\index{19 Psalms:ch. 119, v.  68, pg. ``f30!}; Jeremiah
10:7\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  10, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 31:23\index{19 Psalms:ch.  31, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm
18:3\index{19 Psalms:ch.  18, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 10:1\index{45 Romans:ch.  10, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}2\index{45
Romans:ch.  10, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 62:8\index{19 Psalms:ch.  62, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}; Joshua 24:14\index{06
Joshua:ch.  24, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}; Mark 12:33\index{41 Mark:ch.  12, v.  33, pg. ``f30!}.} But the acceptable way of
worship\index{Worship:of God ``f10!}ping the true God is instituted by Himself\index{Worship:correct:instituted by God
``f10!}, and so limited\index{Worship:only acts approved by God ``f10!} by His own revealed will\index{Revelation:God's
will ``f10!}, that He may not be worshipped according to the imaginations and\index{Worship:false:imaginations and
devices of men ``f10!} devices of men, or the suggestions of Satan\index{Satan:tempter ``f10!}, under any
visible\index{Idolatry:worship of likeness of any created thing ``f10!} representation\index{Idolatry:any visible
representation of God or gods ``f10!}, or any other way not prescribed in the holy\index{Scripture:holy ``f10!}
Scripture.\footnote{\ Deuteronomy 12:32\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.  12, v.  32, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 15:9\index{40
Matthew:ch.  15, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 17:25\index{44 Acts:ch.  17, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 4:9-10\index{40
Matthew:ch.   4, v.   9-10, pg. ``f30!}; Deuteronomy 4:15-20\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.   4, v.  15-20, pg. ``f30!};
Exodus 20:4-6\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.   4-6, pg. ``f30!}; Colossians 2:2\index{51 Colossians:ch.   2, v.   2, pg.
``f30!}3\index{51 Colossians:ch.   2, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

21.2\ \ Religious\index{Worship:glorifying God ``f10!} worship is to\index{Worship:of Trinity ``f10!} be given to God,
the Father\index{Father:God the ``f10!}, Son\index{Jesus:Son of God ``f10!}, and Holy Ghost\index{Holy Spirit:Holy
Ghost ``f10!}; and to Him alone;\footnote{\ Matthew 4:10\index{40 Matthew:ch.   4, v.  10, pg. ``f30!} with John
5:23\index{43 John:ch.   5, v.  23, pg. ``f30!} and 2 Corinthians 13:1\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.  13, v.   1, pg.
``f30!}4\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.  13, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}.} not to angels\index{Angels:angels ``f10!},
saints\index{Believers:saints ``f10!}, or any other creature\index{creatures ``f10!}:\footnote{\ Colossians
2:18\index{51 Colossians:ch.   2, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}; Revelation 19:10\index{66 Revelation:ch.  19, v.  10, pg.
``f30!}; Romans 1:25\index{45 Romans:ch.   1, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}.} and since the fall\index{Sin:original:first
transgression (of Adam) ``f10!}, not without a Mediator\index{Jesus:mediator:of covenant ``f10!}; nor in the mediation
of any other but of Christ alone.\footnote{\ John 14:6\index{43 John:ch.  14, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Timothy
2:5\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   2, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 2:1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   1, pg.
``f30!}8\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}; Colossians 3:17\index{51 Colossians:ch.   3, v.  17, pg.
``f30!}.}


\bigskip

21.3\ \ Prayer, with\index{Prayer:with thanksgiving ``f10!} thanksgiving\index{Prayer:thanking God ``f10!}, being one
special part of religious worship,\index{Worship:elements ``f10!}\footnote{\ Philippians 4:6\index{50 Philippians:ch.  
4, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}.} is by God required of all men:\footnote{\ Psalm 65:2\index{19 Psalms:ch.  65, v.   2, pg.
``f30!}.} and that it may be accepted, it is to be made in\index{Prayer:accepted in Christ ``f10!} the name of the
Son\index{Jesus:Son of God ``f10!},\footnote{\ John 14:13-14\index{43 John:ch.  14, v.  13-14, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Peter
2:5\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   2, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.} by the help of His\index{Prayer:helped by Holy Spirit ``f10!}
Spirit,\footnote{\ Romans 8:2\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}6\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.  26, pg.
``f30!}.} according to His will,\footnote{\ 1 John 5:14\index{62 1 John:ch.   5, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}.} with
understanding, reverence, humility\index{Humility:before God ``f10!}, fervency\index{Prayer:with fervency ``f10!},
faith, love\index{Scripture:to be:loved in faith ``f10!}, and perseverance;\index{Prayer:with perseverance
``f10!}\footnote{\ Psalm 47:7\index{19 Psalms:ch.  47, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}; Ecclesiastes 5:1\index{21 Ecclesiastes:ch. 
 5, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}{}-2\index{21 Ecclesiastes:ch.   5, v.   1-2, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 12:2\index{58 Hebrews:ch. 
12, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}8\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  12, v.  28, pg. ``f30!}; Genesis 18:27\index{01 Genesis:ch.  18, v.  27,
pg. ``f30!}; James 5:16\index{59 James:ch.   5, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; James 1:6\index{59 James:ch.   1, v.   6, pg.
``f30!}{}-7\index{59 James:ch.   1, v.   6-7, pg. ``f30!}; Mark 11:24\index{41 Mark:ch.  11, v.  24, pg. ``f30!};
Matthew 6:1\index{40 Matthew:ch.   6, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}2\index{40 Matthew:ch.   6, v.  12, pg. ``f30!},
14-15\index{40 Matthew:ch.   6, v.  12, 14-15, pg. ``f30!}; Colossians 4:2\index{51 Colossians:ch.   4, v.   2, pg.
``f30!}; Ephesians 6:18\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   6, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}.} and, if vocal\index{Prayer:vocal in a known
language ``f10!}, in a known tongue.\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 14:14\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  14, v.  14, pg.
``f30!}.}


\bigskip

21.4\ \ Prayer is to be made for things lawful\index{Prayer:for lawful things ``f10!};\footnote{\ 1 John 5:14\index{62 1
John:ch.   5, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}.} and for all sorts of men living, or that shall live hereafter:\footnote{\ 1 Timothy
2:1\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}{}-2\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   2, v.   1-2, pg. ``f30!}; John

\bigskip

21.5\ \ The reading\index{Scripture:to be:read and heard ``f10!} of the Scriptures with godly fear,\footnote{\ Acts
15:2\index{44 Acts:ch.  15, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}1\index{44 Acts:ch.  15, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}; Revelation 1:3\index{66

``f10!}\footnote{\ Colossians 3:16\index{51 Colossians:ch.   3, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 5:19\index{49

are all parts of the ordinary\index{Sacraments:part of ordinary worship ``f10!} religious worship of
God\index{Worship:of God ``f10!}:\footnote{\ Matthew 28:19\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians
11:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}3\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  23, pg.
``f30!}{}-29\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  23-29, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 2:42\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  42, pg.
``f30!}.} beside religious\index{Oaths and Vows:religious worship ``f10!} oaths\index{Oaths and Vows:oaths
``f10!},\footnote{\ Deuteronomy 6:13\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.   6, v.  13, pg. ``f30!} with Nehemiah 10:29\index{16
Nehemiah:ch.  10, v.  29, pg. ``f30!}.} vows,\footnote{\ Isaiah 19:21\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  19, v.  21, pg. ``f30!} with
Ecclesiastes 5:4-5\index{21 Ecclesiastes:ch.   5, v.   4-5, pg. ``f30!}.} solemn fastings\index{fasting
``f10!},\footnote{\ Joel 2:12\index{29 Joel:ch.   2, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}; Esther 4:16\index{17 Esther:ch.   4, v.  16,
pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 9:15\index{40 Matthew:ch.   9, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 7:5\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  
7, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.} and thanksgivings\index{Prayer:thanking God ``f10!}, upon special occasions,\footnote{\ Psalm
107; Esther 9:22\index{17 Esther:ch.   9, v.  22, pg. ``f30!}.} which are, in their several times and
seasons\index{Worship:elements in times and seasons ``f10!}, to be used in a holy\index{Scripture:holy ``f10!} and
religious manner\index{Worship:acceptable manner ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Hebrews 12:2\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  12, v.   2, pg.
``f30!}8\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  12, v.  28, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

21.6\ \ Neither prayer\index{Prayer:act of worship ``f10!}, nor any other part of religious
worship,\index{Worship:elements ``f10!} is now under the Gospel\index{Gospel:gospel ``f10!} either tied unto, or made
more acceptable by any place in which it is performed, or towards which it is directed:\footnote{\ John 4:21\index{43
John:ch.   4, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}.} but God is to be worshipped everywhere\index{Worship:in spirit and truth
``f10!},\footnote{\ Malachi 1:11\index{39 Malachi:ch.   1, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Timothy 2:8\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.  
2, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}.} in spirit and truth\index{God's attributes:truth ``f10!};\footnote{\ John 4:23-24\index{43
John:ch.   4, v.  23-24, pg. ``f30!}.} as in private families\index{family, natural ``f10!}\footnote{\ Jeremiah
10:25\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  10, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}; Deuteronomy 6:6\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.   6, v.   6, pg.
``f30!}{}-7\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.   6, v.   6-7, pg. ``f30!}; Job 1:5\index{18 Job:ch.   1, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}; 2
Samuel 6:18, 20\index{10 2 Samuel:ch.   6, v.  18, 20, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Peter 3:7\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   3, v.   7, pg.
``f30!}; Acts 10:2\index{44 Acts:ch.  10, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}.} daily,\index{Prayer:daily in private families,
``f10!}\footnote{\ Matthew 6:1\index{40 Matthew:ch.   6, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}.} and in secret each\index{Prayer:secret
``f10!} one by himself;\footnote{\ Matthew 6:6\index{40 Matthew:ch.   6, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 6:18\index{49
Ephesians:ch.   6, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}.} so, more solemnly, in\index{Prayer:solemn ``f10!} the public assemblies,
which\index{Worship:assemblies not to be neglected ``f10!} are not carelessly or wilfully to be neglected, or forsaken,
when\index{Worship:not to be:forsaken ``f10!} God, by His Word or providence\index{Providence:providence ``f10!}, calls
thereunto\index{Worship:assembly called together ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Isaiah 56:6-7\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  56, v.   6-7,
pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 10:25\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  10, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}; Proverbs 1:20-21, 24\index{20 Proverbs:ch.  
1, v.  20-21, 24, pg. ``f30!}; Proverbs 8:34\index{20 Proverbs:ch.   8, v.  34, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 13:42\index{44
Acts:ch.  13, v.  42, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 4:16\index{42 Luke:ch.   4, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 2:42\index{44 Acts:ch.  
2, v.  42, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

21.7\ \ As it is the law of nature, that, in general, a due proportion\index{Sabbath:proportion of time set apart for
worship ``f10!} of time be set apart for the worship of God; so\index{Worship:times of ``f10!}, in His Word, by a
positive\index{Sabbath:positive, moral, perpetual command ``f10!}, moral\index{God's law:commandments:moral ``f10!},
and perpetual commandment\index{Sabbath:perpetual commandment ``f10!}, binding all\index{Sabbath:binding on all men
``f10!} men, in all ages, He has particularly appointed one day in seven\index{Sabbath:one whole day in seven ``f10!},
for a Sabbath, to\index{Sabbath:seventh day ``f10!} be kept holy\index{Sabbath:to be:kept holy ``f10!} unto
Him:\footnote{\ Exodus 20:8\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}, 10\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.   8, 10, pg.
``f30!}{}-11\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.   8, 10-11, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 56:2, 4, 6-7\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  56, v.   2,
4, 6-7, pg. ``f30!}.} which, from the beginning of the world to the resurrection of
Christ\index{Jesus:resurrection:from the dead ``f10!}, was the last day of\index{Sabbath:last day of week ``f10!} the
week; and, from the resurrection of Christ, was changed into the first day\index{Sabbath:first day of week ``f10!} of
the week,\footnote{\ Genesis 2:2-3\index{01 Genesis:ch.   2, v.   2-3, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 16:1-2\index{46 1
Corinthians:ch.  16, v.   1-2, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 20:7\index{44 Acts:ch.  20, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}.} which, in Scripture,
is\index{Sabbath:Lord's Day ``f10!} called the Lord's Day,\footnote{\ Revelation 1:10\index{66 Revelation:ch.   1, v. 
10, pg. ``f30!}.} and is to be continued to the end of the world, as the Christian Sabbath\index{Sabbath:Christian
``f10!}.\footnote{\ Exodus 20:8\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}, 10\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.   8, 10,
pg. ``f30!} with Matthew 5:17\index{40 Matthew:ch.   5, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}{}-18\index{40 Matthew:ch.   5, v.  17-18,
pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

21.8\ \ This Sabbath is\index{Sabbath:to be:kept holy ``f10!} then kept holy unto the Lord, when men, after a due
preparing\index{Heart:prepared for Sabbath ``f10!} of their hearts, and ordering of the\index{Church
councils:directions for ordering public worship ``f10!}ir common affairs beforehand\index{Sabbath:order common affairs
before ``f10!}, do not only observe an holy rest, all the day, from their own works\index{Sabbath:cease:own works
``f10!}, words, and thoughts about\index{Sabbath:avoid unnecessary, worldly thoughts ``f10!} their worldly employments
and recreations\index{Sabbath:cease:worldly employments and recreations ``f10!},\footnote{\ Exodus 20:8\index{02
Exodus:ch.  20, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}; Exodus 16:23\index{02 Exodus:ch.  16, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}, 25-26, 29-30\index{02
Exodus:ch.  16, v.  23, 25-26, 29-30, pg. ``f30!}; Exodus 31:15\index{02 Exodus:ch.  31, v.  15, pg.
``f30!}{}-17\index{02 Exodus:ch.  31, v.  15-17, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 58:13\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  58, v.  13, pg.
``f30!}; Nehemiah 13:15-19, 21-22\index{16 Nehemiah:ch.  13, v.  15-19, 21-22, pg. ``f30!}.} but also are taken up the
whole time in the public and private exercises\index{Worship:private exercises ``f10!} of His worship, and
in\index{Worship:of God ``f10!} the duties of necessity and\index{Sabbath:works of necessity and mercy ``f10!}
mercy.\footnote{\ Isaiah 58:13\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  58, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 12:1-13\index{40 Matthew:ch.  12,
v.   1-13, pg. ``f30!}.}
