creatures\index{creatures ``f10!}, or anything contained under the name of God, to charms\index{Superstitions:charms
``f10!},\footnote{\ Deuteronomy 18:10-14\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.  18, v.  10-14, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 19:1\index{44
Acts:ch.  19, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}3\index{44 Acts:ch.  19, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}.} or sinful lusts\index{Sexual
immorality:lust ``f10!} and practices;\footnote{\ 2 Timothy 4:3\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   4, v.   3, pg.
``f30!}{}-4\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   4, v.   3-4, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 13:1\index{45 Romans:ch.  13, v.   1, pg.
``f30!}3\index{45 Romans:ch.  13, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}{}-14\index{45 Romans:ch.  13, v.  13-14, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Kings
21:9-10\index{11 1 Kings:ch.  21, v.   9-10, pg. ``f30!}; Jude 1:4\index{65 Jude:v.   1, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.} the
maligning\index{God's name:not to be:maligned ``f10!},\footnote{\ Acts 13:45\index{44 Acts:ch.  13, v.  45, pg.
``f30!}; 1 John 3:1\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}2\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}.}
scorning\index{God's name:not to be:scorned ``f10!},\footnote{\ Psalm 1:1\index{19 Psalms:ch.   1, v.   1, pg. ``f30!};
2 Peter 3:3\index{61 2 Peter:ch.   3, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}.} reviling\index{reviling God or man ``f10!},\footnote{\ 1
Peter 4:4\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   4, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.} or any wise opposing of\index{Falsehood:opposing truth
``f10!} God's truth, grace, and ways\index{Grace:opposed ``f10!};\footnote{\ Acts 4:18\index{44 Acts:ch.   4, v.  18,
pg. ``f30!}; Acts 13:45\index{44 Acts:ch.  13, v.  45, pg. ``f30!}{}-46, 50\index{44 Acts:ch.  13, v.  45-46, 50, pg.
``f30!}; Acts 19:9\index{44 Acts:ch.  19, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Thessalonians 2:16\index{52 1 Thessalonians:ch.   2,
v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 10:29\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  10, v.  29, pg. ``f30!}.} making
profession\index{Profession:false:hypocrisy ``f10!} of religion in\index{Profession:of false religion ``f10!}
hypocrisy\index{hypocrisy ``f10!}, or for sinister\index{Profession:false:sinister ends ``f10!} ends;\footnote{\ 2
Timothy 3:5\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   3, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 6:1\index{40 Matthew:ch.   6, v.   1, pg.
``f30!}{}-2, 5, 16\index{40 Matthew:ch.   6, v.   1-2, 5, 16, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 23:14\index{40 Matthew:ch.  23, v. 
14, pg. ``f30!}.} being ashamed\index{Sin:ashamed of God's truth ``f10!} of it,\footnote{\ Mark 8:38\index{41 Mark:ch. 
 8, v.  38, pg. ``f30!}.} or a shame to\index{God's name:not to be:shamed ``f10!} it, by
unconformable,\footnote{\ Psalm 73:14-15\index{19 Psalms:ch.  73, v.  14-15, pg. ``f30!}.} unwise,\footnote{\ 1
Corinthians 6:5-6\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   6, v.   5-6, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 5:15-17\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   5,
v.  15-17, pg. ``f30!}.} unfruitful,\footnote{\ Isaiah 5:4\index{23 Isaiah:ch.   5, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Peter
1:8-9\index{61 2 Peter:ch.   1, v.   8-9, pg. ``f30!}.} and offensive walking,\footnote{\ Romans 2:23-24\index{45
Romans:ch.   2, v.  23-24, pg. ``f30!}.} or backsliding\index{backsliding ``f10!} from it.\footnote{\ Galatians 3:1,
3\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.   1, 3, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 6:6\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   6, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 114 \textit{What reasons are annexed to the third commandment}\index{God's law:commandments:third ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The reasons annexed to the third commandment\index{God's law:commandments:third ``f10!}, in these words, The Lord thy
God, and, For the Lord will not hold him guiltless\index{God's name:not guiltless if take in vain ``f10!} that takes
his name in vain\index{God's name:not to be:taken in vain ``f10!},\footnote{\ Exodus 20:7\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.  
7, pg. ``f30!}.} are, because he is the Lord and our God, therefore his name is not to be profaned, or\index{God's
name:not to be:profaned ``f10!} any way abused\index{God's name:not to be:abused ``f10!} by us;\footnote{\ Leviticus
19:12\index{03 Leviticus:ch.  19, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}.} especially because he will be so far from
acquitting\index{Judgement day:blasphemers:not acquitted ``f10!} and sparing\index{Judgement day:blasphemers:not spared
``f10!} the transgressors\index{God's law:commandments:transgressions ``f10!} of this commandment, as\index{God's
law:commandments:second ``f10!} that he will not suffer them to escape\index{Punishment:no escape ``f10!} his righteous
judgment\index{Judgement:righteous ``f10!},\footnote{\ Ezekiel 36:21-23\index{26 Ezekiel:ch.  36, v.  21-23, pg.
``f30!}; Deuteronomy 28:58\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.  28, v.  58, pg. ``f30!}{}-59\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.  28, v. 
58-59, pg. ``f30!}; Zechariah 5:2-4\index{38 Zechariah:ch.   5, v.   2-4, pg. ``f30!}.} albeit many such escape the
censures and\index{Punishment:escape from man's ``f10!} punishments of men.\footnote{\ 1 Samuel 2:1\index{09 1
Samuel:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}2, 17, 22, 24\index{09 1 Samuel:ch.   2, v.  12, 17, 22, 24, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Samuel
3:18\index{09 1 Samuel:ch.   3, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 115 \textit{Which is the fourth commandment}\index{God's law:commandments:fourth ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The fourth commandment\index{God's law:commandments:fourth ``f10!} is, Remember\index{Sabbath:to be:remembered
``f10!} the sabbath day, to keep it holy\index{Sabbath:to be:kept holy ``f10!}. Six\index{Sabbath:six days:for labour
``f10!} days shalt you labor, and do\index{Sabbath:labour six days, rest on Sabbath ``f10!} all thy work: but the
seven\index{Sabbath:one whole day in seven ``f10!}th day is the sabbath of\index{Sabbath:instituted by God ``f10!} the
Lord thy God: in it you shalt not do any work, thou, nor thy son, nor thy daughter, thy manservant, nor thy
maidservant\index{Sabbath:servants not to be made to work ``f10!}, nor thy cattle, nor thy stranger that is within thy
gates: For in six\index{Creation:in six days ``f10!} days the Lord made heaven\index{God's attributes:creator:of heaven
and earth ``f10!} and earth, the sea\index{God's attributes:creator:of sea ``f10!}, and all that in them is, and rested
the\index{Sabbath:God rested the seventh day ``f10!} seventh day\index{Sabbath:seventh day ``f10!}: wherefore the Lord
blessed the\index{Sabbath:blessed ``f10!} sabbath day, and hallowed\index{God's name:hallowed ``f10!}
it.\footnote{\ Exodus 20:8\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}{}-11\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.   8-11, pg.
``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 116 \textit{What is required in the fourth commandment}\index{God's law:commandments:fourth ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The fourth commandment\index{God's law:commandments:fourth ``f10!} requires of all\index{Sabbath:to be:kept holy
``f10!} men the sanctifying or\index{Sabbath:sanctified ``f10!} keeping holy to God such set times as he has appointed
in his word, expressly one\index{Sabbath:one whole day in seven ``f10!} whole day in seven; which was the seventh
from\index{Sabbath:seventh day ``f10!} the beginning of the world to the resurrection of
Christ\index{Jesus:resurrection:from the dead ``f10!}, and the first day\index{Sabbath:first day of week ``f10!} of the
week ever since, and so to continue to the end of the world; which is the Christian sabbath,\footnote{\ Deuteronomy
5:12, 14, 18\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.   5, v.  12, 14, 18, pg. ``f30!}; Genesis 2:2-3\index{01 Genesis:ch.   2, v.  
2-3, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 16:1-2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  16, v.   1-2, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 20:7\index{44
Acts:ch.  20, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 5:17\index{40 Matthew:ch.   5, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}{}-18\index{40 Matthew:ch.
  5, v.  17-18, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 56:2, 4, 6-7\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  56, v.   2, 4, 6-7, pg. ``f30!}.} and in the New
Testament\index{Scripture:New Testament ``f10!} called The Lord's day\index{Sabbath:Lord's Day
``f10!}.\footnote{\ Revelation 1:10\index{66 Revelation:ch.   1, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 117 \textit{How is the sabbath or}\index{Sabbath:Lord's Day ``f10!}\textit{ the Lord's day to be
sanctified}\index{Sanctification:sanctification ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The sabbath or\index{Sabbath:Lord's Day ``f10!} Lord's day is to be sanctified\index{Sanctification:sanctification
``f10!} by an holy resting\index{Sabbath:to be:kept holy ``f10!} all the day,\footnote{\ Exodus 20:8\index{02
Exodus:ch.  20, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}, 10\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.   8, 10, pg. ``f30!}.} not only from such works as
are at all times sinful, but even from such worldly employments and recreations\index{Sabbath:cease:worldly employments
and recreations ``f10!} as are on other days lawful\index{Sabbath:cease:activities lawful on other days
``f10!};\footnote{\ Exodus 16:25-28\index{02 Exodus:ch.  16, v.  25-28, pg. ``f30!}; Nehemiah 13:15-22\index{16
Nehemiah:ch.  13, v.  15-22, pg. ``f30!}; Jeremiah 17:21-22\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  17, v.  21-22, pg. ``f30!}.} and
making it our delight\index{Worship:Sabbath delight ``f10!} to spend\index{Sabbath:spend bulk of time in public and
private worship ``f10!} the whole time (except so much of it as is to be taken up in works of necessity
and\index{Sabbath:works of necessity and mercy ``f10!} mercy)\footnote{\ Matthew 12:1-13\index{40 Matthew:ch.  12, v.  
1-13, pg. ``f30!}.} in the public and private exercises\index{Worship:private exercises ``f10!} of God's
worship\index{Worship:of God ``f10!}:\footnote{\ Isaiah 58:13\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  58, v.  13, pg.
``f30!}{}-14\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  58, v.  13-14, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 66:2\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  66, v.   2, pg.
``f30!}3\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  66, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 4:16\index{42 Luke:ch.   4, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; Acts
20:7\index{44 Acts:ch.  20, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 16:1-2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  16, v.   1-2, pg.
``f30!}; Psalm 92; Leviticus 23:3\index{03 Leviticus:ch.  23, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}.} and, to that end, we are to prepare
our hearts\index{Worship:prepare hearts ``f10!}, and with such foresight\index{Lord's Supper:preparation:foresight
``f10!}, diligence, and moderation\index{Material things:moderation:in use ``f10!}, to dispose
and\index{Sabbath:seasonably dispatch and dispose worldly business ``f10!} seasonably dispatch our worldly
business\index{Sabbath:order common affairs before ``f10!}, that we may be the more free and fit for the
duties\index{Sabbath:duties ``f10!} of that day.\footnote{\ Exodus 16:22, 25-26, 29\index{02 Exodus:ch.  16, v.  22,
25-26, 29, pg. ``f30!}; Exodus 20:8\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 23:54, 56\index{42 Luke:ch.  23,
v.  54, 56, pg. ``f30!}; Nehemiah 13:19\index{16 Nehemiah:ch.  13, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 118 \textit{Why is the charge of}\index{Sabbath:charge of keeping directed to:governors ``f10!}\textit{ keeping the
sabbath more specially directed to governors of families}\index{family, natural ``f10!}\textit{, and other
superiors}\index{Sabbath:charge of keeping directed to:other superiors ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The charge of\index{Sabbath:charge of keeping directed to:governors ``f10!} keeping the sabbath is more specially
directed to governors of families\index{family, natural ``f10!}, and other superiors\index{Sabbath:charge of keeping
directed to:other superiors ``f10!}, because they are bound not only to keep it themselves, but to see that it be
observed by\index{Sabbath:superiors to ensure inferiors keep ``f10!} all those that are under their charge; and because
they are prone\index{Sabbath:minds distracted by worldly business ``f10!} ofttimes to hinder them by
employments\index{Sabbath:cease:worldly employments and recreations ``f10!} of their own.\footnote{\ Exodus
20:10\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; Exodus 23:1\index{02 Exodus:ch.  23, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}2\index{02
Exodus:ch.  23, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}; Joshua 24:15\index{06 Joshua:ch.  24, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}; Nehemiah 13:15,
17\index{16 Nehemiah:ch.  13, v.  15, 17, pg. ``f30!}; Jeremiah 17:20-22\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  17, v.  20-22, pg.
``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 119 \textit{What are the sins forbidden}\index{God's law:commandments:sins forbidden ``f10!}\textit{ in the fourth
commandment}\index{God's law:commandments:fourth ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The sins forbidden\index{God's law:commandments:sins forbidden ``f10!} in the fourth commandment\index{God's
law:commandments:fourth ``f10!} are, all omissions\index{Sin:omission of duties ``f10!} of the duties
required\index{God's law:commandments:duties:required by God ``f10!},\footnote{\ Ezekiel 22:26\index{26 Ezekiel:ch. 
22, v.  26, pg. ``f30!}.} all careless, negligent, and\index{Sabbath:negligent of duties ``f10!} unprofitable
performing of them, and being weary of them;\footnote{\ Acts 15:7, 9\index{44 Acts:ch.  15, v.   7, 9, pg. ``f30!};
Ezekiel 33:30-32\index{26 Ezekiel:ch.  33, v.  30-32, pg. ``f30!}; Amos 8:5\index{30 Amos:ch.   8, v.   5, pg. ``f30!};
Malachi 1:13\index{39 Malachi:ch.   1, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}.} all profaning the\index{Sabbath:not to be profaned ``f10!}
day by idleness\index{idleness ``f10!}, and doing that which is in itself sinful;\footnote{\ Ezekiel 23:38\index{26
Ezekiel:ch.  23, v.  38, pg. ``f30!}.} and by all needless\index{Sabbath:cease:activities lawful on other days ``f10!}
works, words, and thoughts, about\index{Sabbath:avoid unnecessary, worldly thoughts ``f10!} our worldly employments and
recreations\index{Sabbath:cease:worldly employments and recreations ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Jeremiah 17:24, 27\index{24
Jeremiah:ch.  17, v.  24, 27, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 58:13\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  58, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 120 \textit{What are the reasons annexed to the fourth commandment}\index{God's law:commandments:fourth
``f10!}\textit{, the more to enforce it}\index{God's law:commandments:words of enforcement ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The reasons annexed to the fourth commandment\index{God's law:commandments:fourth ``f10!}, the more to enforce
it\index{God's law:commandments:words of enforcement ``f10!}, are taken from the equity of it, God allowing us
six\index{Sabbath:six days:for own affairs ``f10!} days of seven for our own affairs, and reserving
but\index{Sabbath:one whole day in seven ``f10!} one for himself, in these words, Six\index{Sabbath:six days:for labour
``f10!} days shalt you labor, and do\index{Sabbath:labour six days, rest on Sabbath ``f10!} all thy
work:\footnote{\ Exodus 20:9\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}.} from God's challenging a special propriety
in that\index{Sabbath:God's propriety over ``f10!} day, The seventh day\index{Sabbath:seventh day ``f10!} is the
sabbath of\index{Sabbath:instituted by God ``f10!} the Lord thy God:\footnote{\ Exodus 20:10\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20,
v.  10, pg. ``f30!}.} from the example of God, who in six\index{Creation:in six days ``f10!} days made
heaven\index{God's attributes:creator:of heaven and earth ``f10!} and earth, the sea\index{God's attributes:creator:of
sea ``f10!}, and all that in them is, and rested the\index{Sabbath:God rested the seventh day ``f10!} seventh day: and
from that blessing which God put upon that day, not only in sanctifying it\index{Sabbath:sanctified ``f10!} to be a day
for his service\index{Sabbath:day for service of God ``f10!}, but in ordaining it\index{Sabbath:ordained as means of
blessing ``f10!} to be a means of blessing to us in our sanctifying it; Wherefore the Lord blessed
the\index{Sabbath:blessed ``f10!} sabbath day, and hallowed\index{God's name:hallowed ``f10!} it.\footnote{\ Exodus
20:11\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 121 \textit{Why is the word Remember}\index{Sabbath:to be:remembered ``f10!}\textit{ set in the beginning of the
fourth commandment}\index{God's law:commandments:fourth ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The word Remember\index{Sabbath:to be:remembered ``f10!} is set in the beginning of the fourth
commandment\index{God's law:commandments:fourth ``f10!},\footnote{\ Exodus 20:8\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.   8, pg.
``f30!}.} partly, because of the great benefit of\index{Sabbath:benefit of ``f10!} remembering it, we being thereby
helped in our preparation to keep\index{Sabbath:preparation for ``f10!} it,\footnote{\ Exodus 16:23\index{02 Exodus:ch.
 16, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 23:54, 56\index{42 Luke:ch.  23, v.  54, 56, pg. ``f30!}; Mark 15:42\index{41 Mark:ch. 
15, v.  42, pg. ``f30!}; Nehemiah 13:19\index{16 Nehemiah:ch.  13, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}.} and, in keeping it, better to
keep all the rest of the commandment\index{God's law:commandments:given to Adam ``f10!}s\index{God's
law:commandments:ten ``f10!},\footnote{\ Psalm 92:13-14\index{19 Psalms:ch.  92, v.  13-14, pg. ``f30!}; Ezekiel 20:12,
19-20\index{26 Ezekiel:ch.  20, v.  12, 19-20, pg. ``f30!}.} and to continue a thankful\index{Prayer:thanking God
``f10!} remembrance of the two\index{Sabbath:thankful remembrance of benefits ``f10!} great benefits of
creation\index{Believers:benefits:of creation ``f10!} and redemption, which\index{Redemption:purchased by Christ
``f10!} contain a short abridgment of religion;\footnote{\ Genesis 2:2-3\index{01 Genesis:ch.   2, v.   2-3, pg.
``f30!}; Psalm 118:22, 24\index{19 Psalms:ch. 118, v.  22, 24, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 4:10, 11\index{44 Acts:ch.   4, v. 
10, 11, pg. ``f30!}; Revelation 1:10\index{66 Revelation:ch.   1, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}.} and partly, because we are very
ready to forget\index{Sabbath:mankind prone to forget ``f10!} it,\footnote{\ Ezekiel 22:26\index{26 Ezekiel:ch.  22, v.
 26, pg. ``f30!}.} for that there is less light of nature for it,\footnote{\ Nehemiah 9:1\index{16 Nehemiah:ch.   9, v.
  1, pg. ``f30!}4\index{16 Nehemiah:ch.   9, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}.} and yet it restrains\index{Sabbath:cease:activities
lawful on other days ``f10!} our natural liberty in things\index{Liberty:natural ``f10!} at other times
lawful;\footnote{\ Exodus 34:21\index{02 Exodus:ch.  34, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}.} that it comes but once in
seven\index{Sabbath:one whole day in seven ``f10!} days, and many worldly business\index{Sabbath:order common affairs
before ``f10!}es\index{Sabbath:cease:worldly employments and recreations ``f10!} come between, and too often take off
our minds from\index{Sabbath:minds distracted by worldly business ``f10!} thinking of\index{Sabbath:avoid unnecessary,
worldly thoughts ``f10!} it, either to prepare for it, or to sanctify\index{Sabbath:sanctified ``f10!}
it;\footnote{\ Deuteronomy 5:14-15\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.   5, v.  14-15, pg. ``f30!}; Amos 8:5\index{30 Amos:ch.  
8, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.} and that Satan with\index{Satan:enemy of God ``f10!} his
instruments\index{Unbelievers:instruments of Satan ``f10!} much labor to blot\index{Sabbath:Satan labours to blot out
``f10!} out the glory, and even the memory of it, to bring in all irreligion\index{Satan:labours to bring irreligion
and impiety ``f10!} and impiety.\footnote{\ Lamentations 1:7\index{25 Lamentations:ch.   1, v.   7, pg. ``f30!};
Jeremiah 17:21-23\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  17, v.  21-23, pg. ``f30!}; Nehemiah 13:15-23\index{16 Nehemiah:ch.  13, v. 
15-23, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 122 \textit{What is the sum of the six commandments}\index{God's law:commandments:last six, duty to man
``f10!}\textit{ which contain our duty to man}\index{God's law:commandments:duties:to others ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The sum of the six commandments\index{God's law:commandments:last six, duty to man ``f10!} which contain our duty to
man\index{God's law:commandments:duties:to others ``f10!} is, to love our neighbor\index{Love for others:neighbour as
self ``f10!} as ourselves,\footnote{\ Matthew 22:39\index{40 Matthew:ch.  22, v.  39, pg. ``f30!}.} and to do to others
what we would have them to do to us.\footnote{\ Matthew 7:1\index{40 Matthew:ch.   7, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}2\index{40
Matthew:ch.   7, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 123 \textit{Which is the fifth commandment}\index{God's law:commandments:fifth ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The fifth commandment\index{God's law:commandments:fifth ``f10!} is, Honor\index{Parents:to be honoured ``f10!} thy
father and thy mother\index{Superiors:styled as fathers and mothers ``f10!}; that thy days may be long upon the land
which the Lord thy God gives you.\footnote{\ Exodus 20:12\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}.} 


\bigskip

Q. 124 \textit{Who are meant by father and}\index{Parents:to be honoured ``f10!}\textit{ mother}\index{Superiors:styled
as fathers and mothers ``f10!}\textit{ in the fifth commandment}\index{God's law:commandments:fifth ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. By father and\index{Parents:to be honoured ``f10!} mother\index{Superiors:styled as fathers and mothers ``f10!}, in
the fifth commandment\index{God's law:commandments:fifth ``f10!}, are meant, not only natural
parents\index{Parents:natural ``f10!},\footnote{\ Proverbs 23:22\index{20 Proverbs:ch.  23, v.  22, pg.
``f30!}{}-25\index{20 Proverbs:ch.  23, v.  22-25, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 6:1-2\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   6, v.   1-2,
pg. ``f30!}.} but all superiors in age\footnote{\ 1 Timothy 5:1\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   5, v.   1, pg.
``f30!}{}-2\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   5, v.   1-2, pg. ``f30!}.} and gifts;\index{Church:furnished with:gifts and graces
``f10!}\footnote{\ Genesis 4:20-22\index{01 Genesis:ch.   4, v.  20-22, pg. ``f30!}; Genesis 45:8\index{01 Genesis:ch. 
45, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}.} and especially such as, by God's ordinance, are\index{Superiors:authority by God's ordinance
``f10!} over us in place of authority, whether in family\index{family, natural ``f10!},\footnote{\ 2 Kings
5:13\index{12 2 Kings:ch.   5, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}.} church,\footnote{\ 2 Kings 2:12\index{12 2 Kings:ch.   2, v.  12,
pg. ``f30!}; 2 Kings 13:14\index{12 2 Kings:ch.  13, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 4:19\index{48 Galatians:ch.   4, v.
 19, pg. ``f30!}.} or commonwealth\index{commonwealth ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Isaiah 49:23\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  49, v.  23,
pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 125 \textit{Why are superiors styled Father}\index{Father:God the ``f10!}\textit{ and Mother}\index{Superiors:styled
as fathers and mothers ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. Superiors are styled Father\index{Father:God the ``f10!} and Mother\index{Superiors:styled as fathers and mothers
``f10!}, both to teach them in all duties toward\index{Superiors:duties toward inferiors ``f10!} their inferiors, like
natural parents\index{Parents:natural ``f10!}, to express love\index{Love for others:parents ``f10!} and
tenderness\index{Superiors:to:express love and tenderness ``f10!} to them, according to their several
relations;\footnote{\ Ephesians 6:4\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   6, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Corinthians 12:14\index{47 2
Corinthians:ch.  12, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Thessalonians 2:7-8, 11\index{52 1 Thessalonians:ch.   2, v.   7-8, 11, pg.
``f30!}; Numbers 11:11-12\index{04 Numbers:ch.  11, v.  11-12, pg. ``f30!}.} and to work inferiors to
a\index{Superiors:to:encourage inferiors ``f10!} greater willingness\index{Inferiors:to:willingly perform duties
``f10!} and cheerfulness\index{cheerfulness ``f10!} in performing their duties\index{Inferiors:to:perform duties
cheerfully ``f10!} to their superiors, as to their parents\index{Parents:superiors, equivalent ``f10!}.\footnote{\ 1
Corinthians 4:1\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   4, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}4-16\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   4, v.  14-16, pg.
``f30!}; 2 Kings 5:13\index{12 2 Kings:ch.   5, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 126 \textit{What is the general scope of the fifth commandment}\index{God's law:commandments:fifth ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The general scope of the fifth commandment\index{God's law:commandments:fifth ``f10!} is, the performance of those
duties\index{God's law:commandments:duties:to others ``f10!} which we mutually owe in\index{Love for
others:mutual:duties ``f10!} our several relations, as inferiors, superiors, or equals\index{Equals:duties of
``f10!}.\footnote{\ Ephesians 5:2\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   5, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   5, v.  21,
pg. ``f30!}; 1 Peter 2:17\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   2, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 12:10\index{45 Romans:ch.  12, v.  10,
pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 127 \textit{What is the honor that}\index{Inferiors:to:honour superiors ``f10!}\textit{ inferiors owe to their
superiors?}

A. The honor which\index{Inferiors:to:honour superiors ``f10!} inferiors owe to their superiors is, all due
reverence\index{Inferiors:due reverence to superiors ``f10!} in heart\index{Love for others:from heart
``f10!},\footnote{\ Malachi 1:6\index{39 Malachi:ch.   1, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; Leviticus 19:3\index{03 Leviticus:ch. 
19, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}.} word,\footnote{\ Proverbs 31:28\index{20 Proverbs:ch.  31, v.  28, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Peter
3:6\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   3, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}.} and behavior\index{Good works:behavior
``f10!};\footnote{\ Leviticus 19:3\index{03 Leviticus:ch.  19, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}2\index{03 Leviticus:ch.  19, v.  32,
pg. ``f30!}; 1 Kings 2:19\index{11 1 Kings:ch.   2, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}.} prayer and thanksgiving\index{Prayer:thanking
God ``f10!} for them;\footnote{\ 1 Timothy 2:1\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}{}-2\index{54 1
Timothy:ch.   2, v.   1-2, pg. ``f30!}.} imitation of their virtues\index{Inferiors:to:imitate superiors' virtues
``f10!} and graces;\footnote{\ Hebrews 13:7\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  13, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}; Philippians 3:17\index{50
Philippians:ch.   3, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}.} willing obedience\index{Commandments of men:lawful to be obeyed ``f10!} to
their lawful commands and counsels;\footnote{\ Ephesians 6:1-2\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   6, v.   1-2, pg. ``f30!},
5-7\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   6, v.   1-2, 5-7, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Peter 2:13\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   2, v.  13, pg.
``f30!}{}-14\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   2, v.  13-14, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 13:1\index{45 Romans:ch.  13, v.   1, pg.
``f30!}{}-5\index{45 Romans:ch.  13, v.   1-5, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 13:17\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  13, v.  17, pg.
``f30!}; Proverbs 4:3-4\index{20 Proverbs:ch.   4, v.   3-4, pg. ``f30!}; Proverbs 23:22\index{20 Proverbs:ch.  23, v. 
22, pg. ``f30!}; Exodus 18:19, 24\index{02 Exodus:ch.  18, v.  19, 24, pg. ``f30!}.} due
submission\index{Inferiors:submission to superiors ``f10!} to their corrections\index{Inferiors:to:accept correction
``f10!};\footnote{\ Hebrews 12:9\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  12, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Peter 2:18-20\index{60 1 Peter:ch.  
2, v.  18-20, pg. ``f30!}.} fidelity\index{Inferiors:fidelity to superiors ``f10!} to,\footnote{\ Titus 2:9-10\index{56
Titus:ch.   2, v.   9-10, pg. ``f30!}.} defense\footnote{\ 1 Samuel 26:15-16\index{09 1 Samuel:ch.  26, v.  15-16, pg.
``f30!}; 2 Samuel 18:3\index{10 2 Samuel:ch.  18, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}; Esther 6:2\index{17 Esther:ch.   6, v.   2, pg.
``f30!}.} and maintenance of their persons and authority, according to their several ranks\index{station in life, ranks
``f10!}, and the nature of their places;\footnote{\ Matthew 22:21\index{40 Matthew:ch.  22, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}; Romans
13:6-7\index{45 Romans:ch.  13, v.   6-7, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Timothy 5:1\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   5, v.   1, pg.
``f30!}7\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   5, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}{}-18\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   5, v.  17-18, pg. ``f30!};
Galatians 6:6\index{48 Galatians:ch.   6, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; Genesis 45:11\index{01 Genesis:ch.  45, v.  11, pg.
``f30!}; Genesis 47:12\index{01 Genesis:ch.  47, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}.} bearing with their infirmities,
and\index{Inferiors:to:bear with infirmities of superiors ``f10!} covering them in love, that\index{Inferiors:to:love
superiors ``f10!} so they may be an honor to them and to their government\index{Inferiors:to:honour superiors'
government ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Psalm 127:3-5\index{19 Psalms:ch. 127, v.   3-5, pg. ``f30!}; Proverbs 31:23\index{20
Proverbs:ch.  31, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip


\bigskip

Q. 128 \textit{What are the sins of inferiors}\index{Inferiors:sins against superiors ``f10!}\textit{ against their
superiors}\index{Superiors:sins against by inferiors ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The sins of inferiors\index{Inferiors:sins against superiors ``f10!} against their superiors\index{Superiors:sins
against by inferiors ``f10!} are, all neglect of the duties required\index{God's law:commandments:duties:required by
God ``f10!} toward them;\footnote{\ Matthew 15:4-6\index{40 Matthew:ch.  15, v.   4-6, pg. ``f30!}.}
envying\index{Envy:envy ``f10!} at,\footnote{\ Numbers 11:28-29\index{04 Numbers:ch.  11, v.  28-29, pg. ``f30!}.}
contempt of,\index{Contempt:for superiors ``f10!}\footnote{\ 1 Samuel 8:7\index{09 1 Samuel:ch.   8, v.   7, pg.
``f30!}; Isaiah 3:5\index{23 Isaiah:ch.   3, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.} and rebellion\index{Inferiors:not to:rebel against
superiors ``f10!}\footnote{\ 2 Samuel 15:1-12\index{10 2 Samuel:ch.  15, v.   1-12, pg. ``f30!}.} against, their
persons\footnote{\ Exodus 21:15\index{02 Exodus:ch.  21, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}.} and places,\index{Commandments of
men:lawful to be obeyed ``f10!}\footnote{\ 1 Samuel 10:27\index{09 1 Samuel:ch.  10, v.  27, pg. ``f30!}.} in their
lawful counsels,\footnote{\ 1 Samuel 2:25\index{09 1 Samuel:ch.   2, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}.} commands, and
corrections\index{Inferiors:to:accept correction ``f10!};\footnote{\ Deuteronomy 21:18-21\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.  21,
v.  18-21, pg. ``f30!}.} cursing\index{cursing ``f10!}, mocking\index{Inferiors:not to:mock superiors
``f10!},\footnote{\ Proverbs 30:11, 17\index{20 Proverbs:ch.  30, v.  11, 17, pg. ``f30!}.} and all such
refractory\index{Inferiors:not to:dishonor superiors ``f10!} and scandalous\index{Scandalous behaviour:behaviour
``f10!} carriage, as proves a shame and dishonor to them and their government\index{Inferiors:to:honour superiors'
government ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Proverbs 19:26\index{20 Proverbs:ch.  19, v.  26, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 129 \textit{What is required of superiors}\index{Superiors:duties toward inferiors ``f10!}\textit{ towards their
inferiors?}

A. It is required of superiors\index{Superiors:duties toward inferiors ``f10!}, according to that
power\index{Superiors:power delegated by Christ ``f10!} they receive from God, and that relation wherein they stand, to
love\index{Superiors:to:love inferiors ``f10!},\footnote{\ Colossians 3:19\index{51 Colossians:ch.   3, v.  19, pg.
``f30!}; Titus 2:4\index{56 Titus:ch.   2, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.} pray for,\index{Prayer:for others ``f10!}\footnote{\ 1
Samuel 12:23\index{09 1 Samuel:ch.  12, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}; Job 1:5\index{18 Job:ch.   1, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.} and
bless the\index{Lord's Supper:elements:Jesus blessed ``f10!}ir\index{Superiors:to:bless inferiors ``f10!}
inferiors;\footnote{\ 1 Kings 8:55-56\index{11 1 Kings:ch.   8, v.  55-56, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 7:7\index{58
Hebrews:ch.   7, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}; Genesis 49:28\index{01 Genesis:ch.  49, v.  28, pg. ``f30!}.} to
instruct,\footnote{\ Deuteronomy 6:6\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.   6, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}{}-7\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.  
6, v.   6-7, pg. ``f30!}.} counsel, and\index{Superiors:to:instruct and counsel inferiors ``f10!}
admonish\index{Superiors:to:admonish inferiors ``f10!} them;\footnote{\ Ephesians 6:4\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   6, v.  
4, pg. ``f30!}.} countenancing,\footnote{\ 1 Peter 3:7\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   3, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}.}
commending\index{Superiors:to:commend inferiors ``f10!},\footnote{\ 1 Peter 2:14\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   2, v.  14, pg.
``f30!}; Romans 13:3\index{45 Romans:ch.  13, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}.} and rewarding such\index{Superiors:to:reward justly
``f10!} as do well;\footnote{\ Esther 6:3\index{17 Esther:ch.   6, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}.} and
discountenancing\index{Superiors:to:use discountenancing wisely ``f10!},\footnote{\ Romans 13:3\index{45 Romans:ch. 
13, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}{}-4\index{45 Romans:ch.  13, v.   3-4, pg. ``f30!}.} reproving\index{Superiors:to:reprove those
who do ill ``f10!}, and chastising\index{Superiors:to:chastise inferiors ``f10!} such as do ill;\footnote{\ Proverbs
29:1\index{20 Proverbs:ch.  29, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}5\index{20 Proverbs:ch.  29, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Peter
2:14\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   2, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}.} protecting,\footnote{\ Job 29:12-17\index{18 Job:ch.  29, v. 
12-17, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 1:10\index{23 Isaiah:ch.   1, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}, 17\index{23 Isaiah:ch.   1, v.  10, 17,
pg. ``f30!}.} and providing\index{Superiors:to:proved for and protect inferiors ``f10!} for them all things necessary
for soul\index{Superiors:to:provide inferiors with things necessary for soul and body ``f10!}\footnote{\ Ephesians
6:4\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   6, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.} and body:\footnote{\ 1 Timothy 5:8\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   5, v.
  8, pg. ``f30!}.} and by grave, wise\index{Superiors:to:display wisdom ``f10!}, holy, and\index{Superiors:to:display
holy lives ``f10!} exemplary\index{Superiors:to:set example ``f10!} carriage, to procure glory\index{Superiors:to:give
glory to God ``f10!} to God,\footnote{\ 1 Timothy 4:1\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   4, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}2\index{54 1
Timothy:ch.   4, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}; Titus 2:3-5\index{56 Titus:ch.   2, v.   3-5, pg. ``f30!}.} honor to
them\index{Inferiors:to:honour superiors ``f10!}selves\index{Superiors:procure honour through exemplary behaviour
``f10!},\footnote{\ 1 Kings 3:28\index{11 1 Kings:ch.   3, v.  28, pg. ``f30!}.} and so to preserve
that\index{Superiors:to:preserve authority ``f10!} authority which God has put upon them.\footnote{\ Titus
2:15\index{56 Titus:ch.   2, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip


\bigskip


Q. 130 \textit{What are the sins of superiors}\index{Superiors:sins of ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The sins of superiors\index{Superiors:sins of ``f10!} are, besides the neglect of the duties required\index{God's
law:commandments:duties:required by God ``f10!} of them,\footnote{\ Ezekiel 34:2-4\index{26 Ezekiel:ch.  34, v.   2-4,
pg. ``f30!}.} an inordinate seeking\index{Superiors:not to:seek selfish ends ``f10!} of
themselves,\footnote{\ Philippians 2:21\index{50 Philippians:ch.   2, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}.} their own glory\index{God's
attributes:glory:his own ``f10!},\footnote{\ John 5:44\index{43 John:ch.   5, v.  44, pg. ``f30!}; John 7:18\index{43
John:ch.   7, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}.} ease, profit, or pleasure;\footnote{\ Isaiah 56:10-11\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  56, v. 
10-11, pg. ``f30!}; Deuteronomy 17:17\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.  17, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}.}
commanding\index{Sin:commanding things unlawful ``f10!} things unlawful,\index{Superiors:not to:command things unlawful
``f10!}\footnote{\ Daniel 3:4-6\index{27 Daniel:ch.   3, v.   4-6, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 4:17-18\index{44 Acts:ch.   4, v. 
17-18, pg. ``f30!}.} or not in the power\index{Superiors:not to:command things not in inferiors' power ``f10!} of
inferiors to perform;\index{Superiors:not to:counsel or encourage evil ``f10!}\footnote{\ Exodus 5:10-18\index{02
Exodus:ch.   5, v.  10-18, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 23:2, 4\index{40 Matthew:ch.  23, v.   2, 4, pg. ``f30!}.}
counseling,\footnote{\ Matthew 14:8\index{40 Matthew:ch.  14, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}; Mark 6:24\index{41 Mark:ch.   6, v. 
24, pg. ``f30!}.} encouraging,\footnote{\ 2 Samuel 13:28\index{10 2 Samuel:ch.  13, v.  28, pg. ``f30!}.} or favoring
them in that which is evil;\footnote{\ 1 Samuel 3:13\index{09 1 Samuel:ch.   3, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}.}
dissuading\index{Superiors:not to:dissuade inferiors from doing good ``f10!}, discouraging, or\index{Superiors:not
to:discourage inferiors ``f10!} discountenancing\index{Superiors:to:use discountenancing wisely ``f10!} them in that
which is good;\footnote{\ John 7:46-49\index{43 John:ch.   7, v.  46-49, pg. ``f30!}; Colossians 3:2\index{51
Colossians:ch.   3, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}1\index{51 Colossians:ch.   3, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}; Exodus 5:17\index{02
Exodus:ch.   5, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}.} correcting them unduly\index{Superiors:not to:correct inferiors unduly
``f10!};\footnote{\ 1 Peter 2:18-20\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   2, v.  18-20, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 12:1\index{58 Hebrews:ch.
 12, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}0\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  12, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; Deuteronomy 25:3\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.  25,
v.   3, pg. ``f30!}.} careless exposing\index{Superiors:not to:expose inferiors to temptation ``f10!}, or
leaving\index{Superiors:not to:leave inferiors in wrong ``f10!} them to wrong, temptation\index{Temptation:temptation
``f10!}, and danger\index{Superiors:not to:leave inferiors in danger ``f10!};\footnote{\ Genesis 38:11, 26\index{01
Genesis:ch.  38, v.  11, 26, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 18:17\index{44 Acts:ch.  18, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}.}
provoking\index{Sin:provoking others to commit ``f10!} them to wrath;\index{Wrath:provoking others to
``f10!}\footnote{\ Ephesians 6:4\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   6, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.} or any way
dishonoring\index{Superiors:not to:dishonor themselves through sin ``f10!} themselves, or lessening\index{Superiors:not
to:lessen authority by bad behaviour ``f10!} their authority, by an unjust\index{unjust behaviour ``f10!}, indiscreet,
rigorous\index{Superiors:not to:be rigorous ``f10!}, or remiss behavior\index{Sin:remiss behavior by superiors
``f10!}.\footnote{\ Genesis 9:21\index{01 Genesis:ch.   9, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Kings 1:6\index{11 1 Kings:ch.   1,
v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Kings 12:13-16\index{11 1 Kings:ch.  12, v.  13-16, pg. ``f30!}; Samuel 2:29-31.}


\bigskip

Q. 131 \textit{What are the duties of equals}\index{Equals:duties of ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The duties of equals\index{Equals:duties of ``f10!} are, to regard the dignity\index{Equals:regard dignity of others
``f10!} and worth of\index{Equals:regard worth of others ``f10!} each other,\footnote{\ 1 Peter 2:17\index{60 1
Peter:ch.   2, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}.} in giving honor to go\index{Love for others:seek neighbours' honour ``f10!} one
before another;\footnote{\ Romans 12:10\index{45 Romans:ch.  12, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}.} and to rejoice in
each\index{Love for others:rejoice in:gifts of others ``f10!} other's gifts and advancement\index{Love for
others:acknowledge gifts and graces of others ``f10!}, as their own.\footnote{\ Romans 12:15\index{45 Romans:ch.  12,
v.  15, pg. ``f30!}{}-16\index{45 Romans:ch.  12, v.  15-16, pg. ``f30!}; Philippians 2:3-4\index{50 Philippians:ch.  
2, v.   3-4, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 132 \textit{What are the sins of equals}\index{Equals:sins of ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The sins of equals\index{Equals:sins of ``f10!} are, besides the neglect of the duties required\index{God's
law:commandments:duties:required by God ``f10!},\footnote{\ Romans 13:8\index{45 Romans:ch.  13, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}.}
the undervaluing\index{Equals:not to undervalue worth of another ``f10!} of the worth,\footnote{\ 2 Timothy
3:3\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   3, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}.} envying\index{Envy:envy ``f10!} the gifts,\footnote{\ Acts
7:9\index{44 Acts:ch.   7, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 5:2\index{48 Galatians:ch.   5, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}6\index{48
Galatians:ch.   5, v.  26, pg. ``f30!}.} grieving at\index{Envy:grieving at success of others ``f10!} the advancement

Q. 133 \textit{What is the reason annexed to the fifth commandment}\index{God's law:commandments:fifth ``f10!}\textit{,
the more to enforce it}\index{God's law:commandments:words of enforcement ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The reason annexed to the fifth commandment\index{God's law:commandments:fifth ``f10!}, in these words, That thy days
may be long upon the land which the Lord thy God gives you,\footnote{\ Exodus 20:12\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.  12,
pg. ``f30!}.} is an express promise of long\index{God's law:commandments:promises included ``f10!} life and prosperity,
as far as it shall serve for God's glory\index{God's law:commandments:obedience:for God's glory ``f10!} and their own
good, to all such as keep this commandment.\footnote{\ Deuteronomy 5:16\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.   5, v.  16, pg.
``f30!}; 1 Kings 8:25\index{11 1 Kings:ch.   8, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 6:2\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   6, v.   2,
pg. ``f30!}{}-3\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   6, v.   2-3, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 134 \textit{Which is the sixth commandment}\index{God's law:commandments:sixth ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The sixth commandment\index{God's law:commandments:sixth ``f10!} is, You shalt not kill\index{murder, unjust killing
``f10!}.\footnote{\ Exodus 20:13\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}.}

15-16, pg. ``f30!}.} and practices, which tend to the unjust\index{murder, unjust killing ``f10!} taking away the life
of any;\footnote{\ 1 Samuel 24:2\index{09 1 Samuel:ch.  24, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Samuel 26:9-11\index{09 1 Samuel:ch.

Q. 136 \textit{What are the sins forbidden}\index{God's law:commandments:sins forbidden ``f10!}\textit{ in the sixth

A. The sins forbidden\index{God's law:commandments:sins forbidden ``f10!} in the sixth commandment\index{God's
law:commandments:sixth ``f10!} are, all taking away the life of ourselves,\footnote{\ Acts 16:28\index{44 Acts:ch.  16,
v.  28, pg. ``f30!}.} or of others,\footnote{\ Genesis 9:6\index{01 Genesis:ch.   9, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}.} except in

``f30!}; Deuteronomy 20:1-20\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.  20, v.   1-20, pg. ``f30!}.} or necessary defense\index{Human
life:defend ``f10!};\footnote{\ Exodus 22:2-3\index{02 Exodus:ch.  22, v.   2-3, pg. ``f30!}.} the neglecting
or\index{Human life:not neglect or withdraw preservation ``f10!} withdrawing the lawful and necessary\index{Human
life:protect with:lawful endeavors ``f10!} means of preservation\index{Human life:preservation ``f10!} of
life;\footnote{\ Matthew 25:42-43\index{40 Matthew:ch.  25, v.  42-43, pg. ``f30!}; James 2:15-16\index{59 James:ch.  
2, v.  15-16, pg. ``f30!}; Ecclesiastes 6:1-2\index{21 Ecclesiastes:ch.   6, v.   1-2, pg. ``f30!}.} sinful
anger\index{anger ``f10!},\footnote{\ Matthew 5:22\index{40 Matthew:ch.   5, v.  22, pg. ``f30!}.} hatred,\footnote{\ 1
John 3:1\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}5\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}; Leviticus
19:17\index{03 Leviticus:ch.  19, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}.} envy\index{Human life:no anger, hatred, envy, revenge
``f10!},\footnote{\ Proverbs 14:30\index{20 Proverbs:ch.  14, v.  30, pg. ``f30!}.} desire of
revenge\index{Revenge:man's desire for ``f10!};\footnote{\ Romans 12:19\index{45 Romans:ch.  12, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}.}
all excessive passions\index{Love for others:passions, subduing ``f10!},\footnote{\ Ephesians 4:3\index{49
Ephesians:ch.   4, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.  31, pg. ``f30!}.} distracting

Romans:ch.  13, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}.} labor,\footnote{\ Ecclesiastes 2:22-23\index{21 Ecclesiastes:ch.   2, v.  22-23,

12, pg. ``f30!}.} and recreations;\index{Human life:protect with:balanced labour and recreation
``f10!}\footnote{\ Isaiah 5:12\index{23 Isaiah:ch.   5, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}.} provoking\index{Sin:provoking others to
commit ``f10!} words,\footnote{\ Proverbs 12:18\index{20 Proverbs:ch.  12, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}; Proverbs 15:1\index{20

Q. 137 \textit{Which is the seven}\index{Sabbath:one whole day in seven ``f10!}\textit{th commandment?}

immorality:adultery ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Exodus 20:14\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}.}

2, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}.} and the preservation of it\index{Sexual purity:preservation ``f10!} in ourselves and
others;\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 7:2, 35-36\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   7, v.   2, 35-36, pg. ``f30!}.}

Q. 140 \textit{Which is the eighth}\index{God's law:commandments:eighth ``f10!}\textit{ commandment?}

``f10!}.\footnote{\ Exodus 20:15\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}.}

Q. 143 \textit{Which is the ninth}\index{God's law:commandments:ninth ``f10!}\textit{ commandment?}

A. The ninth\index{God's law:commandments:ninth ``f10!} commandment is, You shalt not bear false witness
against\index{Falsehood:false witness against neighbour ``f10!} thy neighbor\index{Love for others:neighbour as self
``f10!}.\footnote{\ Exodus 20:16\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 144 \textit{What are the duties required}\index{God's law:commandments:duties:required by God ``f10!}\textit{ in the
ninth}\index{God's law:commandments:ninth ``f10!}\textit{ commandment?}

A. The duties required\index{God's law:commandments:duties:required by God ``f10!} in the ninth\index{God's
law:commandments:ninth ``f10!} commandment are, the preserving\index{Truth:preservation of ``f10!} and

Zechariah:ch.   8, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}.} and the good name of our neighbor\index{Love for others:neighbour as self
``f10!}, as well as our own;\footnote{\ 3 John 1:12\index{64 3 John:v.   1, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}.} appearing and
standing\index{Truth:appear and stand for ``f10!} for the truth\index{Truth:defend ``f10!};\footnote{\ Proverbs
31:8-9\index{20 Proverbs:ch.  31, v.   8-9, pg. ``f30!}.} and from the heart\index{Love for others:from heart
``f10!},\footnote{\ Psalm 15:2\index{19 Psalms:ch.  15, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}.} sincerely,\footnote{\ 2 Chronicles
19:9\index{14 2 Chronicles:ch.  19, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}.} freely,\footnote{\ 1 Samuel 19:4-5\index{09 1 Samuel:ch.  19,
v.   4-5, pg. ``f30!}.} clearly,\index{Truth:speak freely and clearly ``f10!}\footnote{\ Joshua 7:19\index{06
Joshua:ch.   7, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}.} and fully,\footnote{\ 2 Samuel 14:18-20\index{10 2 Samuel:ch.  14, v.  18-20, pg.
``f30!}.} speaking the truth\index{Truth:speak, and only ``f10!}, and only the truth, in matters of
judgment\index{Truth:in matters of judgment and justice ``f10!} and justice,\footnote{\ Leviticus 19:15\index{03
Leviticus:ch.  19, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}; Proverbs 14:5, 25\index{20 Proverbs:ch.  14, v.   5, 25, pg. ``f30!}.} and in
all other things whatsoever;\footnote{\ 2 Corinthians 1:1\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   1, v.   1, pg.
``f30!}7-18\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   1, v.  17-18, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 4:25\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.  25,
pg. ``f30!}.} a charitable\index{Love for others:charitable thoughts ``f10!} esteem of our

covering of their infirmities;\index{Love for others:covering infirmities of others ``f10!}\footnote{\ Proverbs

acknowledging of their\index{Love for others:acknowledge gifts and graces of others ``f10!} gifts and
graces,\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 1:4\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   1, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}{}-5, 7\index{46 1
Corinthians:ch.   1, v.   4-5, 7, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Timothy 1:4-5\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   1, v.   4-5, pg. ``f30!}.}
defending their\index{Human life:defend ``f10!} innocency;\index{Love for others:defend innocence ``f10!}\footnote{\ 1
Samuel 22:14\index{09 1 Samuel:ch.  22, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}.} a ready receiving of a\index{Truth:receiving a good
report ``f10!} good report,\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 13:6-7\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  13, v.   6-7, pg. ``f30!}.} and
unwillingness\index{Truth:unwillingness to admit evil report ``f10!} to admit of an evil\index{Truth:not admit evil

Q. 145 \textit{What are the sins forbidden}\index{God's law:commandments:sins forbidden ``f10!}\textit{ in the
ninth}\index{God's law:commandments:ninth ``f10!}\textit{ commandment?}

A. The sins forbidden\index{God's law:commandments:sins forbidden ``f10!} in the ninth\index{God's
law:commandments:ninth ``f10!} commandment are, all prejudicing\index{Falsehood:prejudicing truth or justice ``f10!}
the truth, and the good name of our neighbor\index{Love for others:neighbour as self ``f10!}s, as well as our
own,\footnote{\ 1 Samuel 17:28\index{09 1 Samuel:ch.  17, v.  28, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Samuel 1:9-10, 15-16\index{10 2
Samuel:ch.   1, v.   9-10, 15-16, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Samuel 16:3\index{10 2 Samuel:ch.  16, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}.}

Leviticus:ch.  19, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}; Habakkuk 1:4\index{35 Habakkuk:ch.   1, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.} giving false
evidence,\footnote{\ Proverbs 6:16, 19\index{20 Proverbs:ch.   6, v.  16, 19, pg. ``f30!}; Proverbs 19:5\index{20
Proverbs:ch.  19, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.} suborning false witnesses\index{Falsehood:suborning false witnesses
``f10!},\footnote{\ Acts 6:1\index{44 Acts:ch.   6, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}3\index{44 Acts:ch.   6, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}.}

Q. 146 \textit{Which is the tenth}\index{God's law:commandments:tenth ``f10!}\textit{ commandment?}

A. The tenth\index{God's law:commandments:tenth ``f10!} commandment is, You shalt not
covet\index{Covetousness:covetousness ``f10!} thy neighbor\index{Love for others:neighbour as self ``f10!}{}'s house,
you\index{Covetousness:nothing of neighbour ``f10!} shalt not covet thy neighbor's wife, nor his manservant, nor his
maidservant\index{Sabbath:servants not to be made to work ``f10!}, nor his ox, nor his ass, nor any thing that is thy
neighbor's.\footnote{\ Exodus 20:17\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 147 \textit{What are the duties required}\index{God's law:commandments:duties:required by God ``f10!}\textit{ in the
tenth}\index{God's law:commandments:tenth ``f10!}\textit{ commandment?}

A. The duties required\index{God's law:commandments:duties:required by God ``f10!} in the tenth\index{God's
law:commandments:tenth ``f10!} commandment are, such a full contentment\index{contentment ``f10!} with our own
condition,\footnote{\ Hebrews 13:5\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  13, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Timothy 6:6\index{54 1 Timothy:ch. 
 6, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}.} and such a charitable\index{Love for others:charitable thoughts ``f10!} frame of the whole
soul\index{Love for others:with whole soul ``f10!} toward our neighbor\index{Love for others:neighbour as self ``f10!},
as that all our inward motions\index{Love for others:inward thoughts further others' good ``f10!} and affections
to\index{Covetousness:inordinate affections to others' goods ``f10!}uching\index{Love for others:advancement of others
``f10!} him, tend unto, and further all that good which is his.\footnote{\ Job 31:29\index{18 Job:ch.  31, v.  29, pg.
``f30!}; Psalm 122:7-9\index{19 Psalms:ch. 122, v.   7-9, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Timothy 1:5\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   1, v.  
5, pg. ``f30!}; Esther 10:3\index{17 Esther:ch.  10, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 13:4-7\index{46 1
Corinthians:ch.  13, v.   4-7, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 148 \textit{What are the sins forbidden}\index{God's law:commandments:sins forbidden ``f10!}\textit{ in the
tenth}\index{God's law:commandments:tenth ``f10!}\textit{ commandment?}

A. The sins forbidden\index{God's law:commandments:sins forbidden ``f10!} in the tenth\index{God's
law:commandments:tenth ``f10!} commandment are, discontentment\index{discontentment ``f10!} with our own
estate;\footnote{\ 1 Kings 21:4\index{11 1 Kings:ch.  21, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}; Esther 5:13\index{17 Esther:ch.   5, v. 
13, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 10:10\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  10, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}.} envying\index{Envy:envy
``f10!}\footnote{\ Galatians 5:2\index{48 Galatians:ch.   5, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}6\index{48 Galatians:ch.   5, v.  26,
pg. ``f30!}; James 3:1\index{59 James:ch.   3, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}4, 16\index{59 James:ch.   3, v.  14, 16, pg.
``f30!}.} and grieving at\index{Envy:grieving at success of others ``f10!} the good of our neighbor\index{Love for
others:neighbour as self ``f10!},\footnote{\ Psalm 112:9-10\index{19 Psalms:ch. 112, v.   9-10, pg. ``f30!}; Nehemiah
2:10\index{16 Nehemiah:ch.   2, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}.} together with all inordinate
motions\index{Covetousness:inordinate affections to others' goods ``f10!} and affections to anything that is
his.\footnote{\ Romans 7:7\index{45 Romans:ch.   7, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}{}-8\index{45 Romans:ch.   7, v.   7-8, pg.
``f30!}; Romans 13:9\index{45 Romans:ch.  13, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}; Colossians 3:5\index{51 Colossians:ch.   3, v.   5,
pg. ``f30!}; Deuteronomy 5:21\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.   5, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}.}

\bigskip


Q. 149 \textit{Is any man able perfectly to keep the commandment}\index{God's law:commandments:given to Adam
``f10!}\textit{s}\index{God's law:commandments:ten ``f10!}\textit{ of God?}

A. No man is able, either of himself,\footnote{\ James 3:2\index{59 James:ch.   3, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; John
15:5\index{43 John:ch.  15, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 8:3\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}.} or by any
grace\index{Grace:empowerment ``f10!} received in this life, perfectly to keep the commandment\index{God's
law:commandments:given to Adam ``f10!}s\index{God's law:commandments:ten ``f10!} of God;\footnote{\ Ecclesiastes
7:2\index{21 Ecclesiastes:ch.   7, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}0\index{21 Ecclesiastes:ch.   7, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 1:8,
10\index{62 1 John:ch.   1, v.   8, 10, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 5:1\index{48 Galatians:ch.   5, v.   1, pg.
``f30!}7\index{48 Galatians:ch.   5, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 7:18\index{45 Romans:ch.   7, v.  18, pg.
``f30!}{}-19\index{45 Romans:ch.   7, v.  18-19, pg. ``f30!}.} but does daily break the\index{Lord's Supper:bread
broken ``f10!}m\index{God's law:broken daily by all men (thought, word, deed) ``f10!} in thought,\footnote{\ Genesis
6:5\index{01 Genesis:ch.   6, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}; Genesis 8:21\index{01 Genesis:ch.   8, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}.} word,
and deed.\footnote{\ Romans 3:9\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}{}-19\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.   9-19,
pg. ``f30!}; James 3:2\index{59 James:ch.   3, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}{}-13\index{59 James:ch.   3, v.   2-13, pg.
``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 150 \textit{Are all transgressions}\index{God's law:commandments:transgressions ``f10!}\textit{ of the law of God
equally heinous}\index{God's law:commandments:all transgression equally heinous ``f10!}\textit{ in themselves, and in
the sight of God?}

A. All transgressions\index{God's law:commandments:transgressions ``f10!} of the law of God are not equally
heinous\index{God's law:commandments:all transgression equally heinous ``f10!}; but some sins in themselves, and by
reason of several aggravations\index{Sin:aggravations:which compound ``f10!}, are more
heinous\index{Sin:aggravations:make more heinous ``f10!} in the sight of God than others.\footnote{\ John
19:11\index{43 John:ch.  19, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}; Ezekiel 8:6, 13, 15\index{26 Ezekiel:ch.   8, v.   6, 13, 15, pg.
``f30!}; 1 John 5:16\index{62 1 John:ch.   5, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 78:17, 32, 56\index{19 Psalms:ch.  78, v.  17,
32, 56, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 151 \textit{What are those aggravations}\index{Sin:aggravations:which compound ``f10!}\textit{ that make some sins
more heinous}\index{Sin:aggravations:make more heinous ``f10!}\textit{ than others?}

A. Sins receive their aggravations\index{Sin:aggravations:which compound ``f10!}, 1. From the persons
offending:\index{Sin:aggravations:maturity of person ``f10!}\footnote{\ Jeremiah 2:8\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.   2, v.   8,
pg. ``f30!}.} if they be of riper\index{Sin:aggravations:performed by person of riper age ``f10!} age,\footnote{\ Job
32:7, 9\index{18 Job:ch.  32, v.   7, 9, pg. ``f30!}; Ecclesiastes 4:13\index{21 Ecclesiastes:ch.   4, v.  13, pg.
``f30!}.} greater experience\index{Sin:aggravations:performed by person with greater experience of grace ``f10!} or
grace\index{Sin:aggravations:those with greater experience or grace ``f10!},\footnote{\ 1 Kings 11:4, 9\index{11 1
Kings:ch.  11, v.   4, 9, pg. ``f30!}.} eminent\index{Sin:aggravations:person's place or office ``f10!} for
profession\index{Faith:profession of ``f10!},\footnote{\ 2 Samuel 12:14\index{10 2 Samuel:ch.  12, v.  14, pg. ``f30!};
1 Corinthians 5:1\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   5, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}.} gifts,\footnote{\ James 4:17\index{59 James:ch.
  4, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 12:47-48\index{42 Luke:ch.  12, v.  47-48, pg. ``f30!}.} place,\footnote{\ Jeremiah
5:4-5\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.   5, v.   4-5, pg. ``f30!}.} office,\footnote{\ 2 Samuel 12:7-9\index{10 2 Samuel:ch.  12,
v.   7-9, pg. ``f30!}; Ezekiel 8:11-12\index{26 Ezekiel:ch.   8, v.  11-12, pg. ``f30!}.} guides to
others,\footnote{\ Romans 2:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}7-24\index{45 Romans:ch.   2, v.  17-24, pg.
``f30!}.} and whose example is likely to be followed\index{Sin:aggravations:setting bad example ``f10!} by
others.\footnote{\ Galatians 2:11-14\index{48 Galatians:ch.   2, v.  11-14, pg. ``f30!}.} 2. From the parties
offended:\footnote{\ Matthew 21:38-39\index{40 Matthew:ch.  21, v.  38-39, pg. ``f30!}.} if immediately against
God,\footnote{\ 1 Samuel 2:25\index{09 1 Samuel:ch.   2, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 5:4\index{44 Acts:ch.   5, v.   4,
pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 51:4\index{19 Psalms:ch.  51, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.} his attributes\index{God's attributes:to
be:revered ``f10!},\footnote{\ Romans 2:4\index{45 Romans:ch.   2, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.} and
worship;\index{Worship:abuses ``f10!}\footnote{\ Malachi 1:8, 14\index{39 Malachi:ch.   1, v.   8, 14, pg. ``f30!}.}
against Christ, and his grace\index{Sin:aggravations:against God's grace ``f10!};\footnote{\ Hebrews 2:2-3\index{58
Hebrews:ch.   2, v.   2-3, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 12:2\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  12, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}5\index{58
Hebrews:ch.  12, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}.} the Holy Spirit\index{Holy Spirit:Holy Spirit ``f10!},\footnote{\ Hebrews
10:29\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  10, v.  29, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 12:31-32\index{40 Matthew:ch.  12, v.  31-32, pg.
``f30!}.} his witness,\footnote{\ Ephesians 4:3\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}0\index{49 Ephesians:ch.
  4, v.  30, pg. ``f30!}.} and workings\index{Sin:aggravations:against Holy Spirit's working
``f10!};\footnote{\ Hebrews 6:4-6\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   6, v.   4-6, pg. ``f30!}.} against
superiors\index{Inferiors:sins against superiors ``f10!}, men of eminency,\footnote{\ Jude 1:8\index{65 Jude:v.   1, v.
  8, pg. ``f30!}; Numbers 12:8-9\index{04 Numbers:ch.  12, v.   8-9, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 3:5\index{23 Isaiah:ch.   3,
v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.} and such as we stand especially related and engaged unto;\footnote{\ Proverbs 30:17\index{20
Proverbs:ch.  30, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Corinthians 12:15\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.  12, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm
