\bigskip

Q. 152 \textit{What does every sin deserve}\index{Sin:deserves damnation ``f10!}\textit{ at the hands of God?}

A. Every sin, even the least, being against the sovereignty\index{God's attributes:sovereign lordship
``f10!},\footnote{\ James 2:10\index{59 James:ch.   2, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}{}-11\index{59 James:ch.   2, v.  10-11, pg.
``f30!}.} goodness\index{God's attributes:goodness ``f10!},\footnote{\ Exodus 20:1-2\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.   1-2,
pg. ``f30!}.} and holiness of God\index{God's attributes:holy:nature ``f10!},\footnote{\ Habakkuk 1:13\index{35
Habakkuk:ch.   1, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; Leviticus 10:3\index{03 Leviticus:ch.  10, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}; Leviticus
11:44-45\index{03 Leviticus:ch.  11, v.  44-45, pg. ``f30!}.} and against his righteous law\index{God's law:righteous
requirements ``f10!},\footnote{\ 1 John 3:4\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 7:12\index{45
Romans:ch.   7, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}.} deserves\index{Sin:deserves damnation ``f10!} his wrath and\index{Wrath:of
God:for sin ``f10!} curse,\index{Curse:of God ``f10!}\footnote{\ Ephesians 5:6\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   5, v.   6, pg.
``f30!}; Galatians 3:10\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}.} both in this life,\footnote{\ Lamentations
3:39\index{25 Lamentations:ch.   3, v.  39, pg. ``f30!}; Deuteronomy 28:15-68\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.  28, v.  15-68,
pg. ``f30!}.} and that which is to come;\footnote{\ Matthew 25:41\index{40 Matthew:ch.  25, v.  41, pg. ``f30!}.} and
cannot be expiated\index{Sin:expiated only by blood of Christ ``f10!} but by the blood\index{Jesus:shed blood for
remission of sins ``f10!} of Christ.\footnote{\ Hebrews 9:22\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   9, v.  22, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Peter
1:18\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   1, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}{}-19\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   1, v.  18-19, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 153 \textit{What does God require of us}\index{God's law:commandments:duties:required by God ``f10!}\textit{, that we
may escape}\index{Wrath:of God:requirements to escape ``f10!}\textit{ his wrath and}\index{Wrath:of God:for sin
``f10!}\textit{ curse due}\index{Curse:deserved for sin ``f10!}\textit{ to us by reason of the transgression
of}\index{God's law:commandments:transgressions ``f10!}\textit{ the law?}

A. That we may escape\index{Wrath:of God:requirements to escape ``f10!} the wrath and\index{Wrath:of God:for sin ``f10!}
curse of God\index{Curse:of God ``f10!} due to us by reason of the transgression of\index{God's
law:commandments:transgressions ``f10!} the law, he requires of us\index{Repentance:required for pardon ``f10!}
repentance to\index{Repentance:to those offended ``f10!}ward God, and faith\index{Faith:in Jesus Christ ``f10!} toward
our Lord Jesus Christ,\footnote{\ Acts 16:30\index{44 Acts:ch.  16, v.  30, pg. ``f30!}{}-31\index{44 Acts:ch.  16, v. 
30-31, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 20:21\index{44 Acts:ch.  20, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 3:7-8\index{40 Matthew:ch.   3, v.  
7-8, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 13:3, 5\index{42 Luke:ch.  13, v.   3, 5, pg. ``f30!}; John 3:16\index{43 John:ch.   3, v.  16,
pg. ``f30!}, 18\index{43 John:ch.   3, v.  16, 18, pg. ``f30!}.} and the diligent use\index{Grace:diligent use of means
``f10!} of the outward means whereby Christ communicates to us the benefits of his\index{Believers:benefits:of Christ's
mediation ``f10!} mediation\index{Jesus:mediator:of covenant ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Proverbs 2:1\index{20 Proverbs:ch.  
2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}{}-5\index{20 Proverbs:ch.   2, v.   1-5, pg. ``f30!}; Proverbs 8:33-36\index{20 Proverbs:ch.  
8, v.  33-36, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 154 \textit{What are the outward means whereby Christ communicates to us the benefits of
his}\index{Believers:benefits:of Christ's mediation ``f10!}\textit{ mediation}\index{Jesus:mediator:of covenant
``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The outward and ordinary means whereby Christ communicates to his church\index{Church:Christ's ``f10!} the benefits
of his mediation\index{Jesus:mediator:of covenant ``f10!}, are all his ordinances;
especially\index{Worship:ordinances:means of Christ's mediation ``f10!} the word,
sacraments\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!}, and prayer; all\index{Prayer:act of worship ``f10!} which are made
effectual\index{Worship:ordinances:made effectual for salvation ``f10!} to the elect\index{Election:elect of God
``f10!} for their salvation\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Matthew 28:19\index{40
Matthew:ch.  28, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}{}-20\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  19-20, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 2:42\index{44 Acts:ch.
  2, v.  42, pg. ``f30!}, 46\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  42, 46, pg. ``f30!}{}-47\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  42, 46-47,
pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 155 \textit{How is the word made effectual}\index{Scripture:word of God:for salvation ``f10!}\textit{ to
salvation}\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The Spirit\index{Holy Spirit:Holy Spirit ``f10!} of God makes the reading\index{Scripture:to be:read and heard
``f10!}, but especially the preaching of the word, an effectual\index{Preaching:effectual means of convincing and
enlightening ``f10!} means of enlightening\index{Effectual call:enlightening minds spiritually
``f10!},\footnote{\ Nehemiah 8:8\index{16 Nehemiah:ch.   8, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 26:18\index{44 Acts:ch.  26, v. 
18, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 19:8\index{19 Psalms:ch.  19, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}.} convincing, and\index{Preaching:convincing
and converting sinners ``f10!} humbling\index{Humility:sinners humbled ``f10!} sinners;\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians
14:24-25\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  14, v.  24-25, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Chronicles 34:18-19, 26-28\index{14 2 Chronicles:ch.
 34, v.  18-19, 26-28, pg. ``f30!}.} of driving\index{Preaching:drive men to Christ ``f10!} them out of themselves, and
drawing them\index{Effectual call:drawing to Christ ``f10!} unto Christ;\footnote{\ Acts 2:37\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.
 37, pg. ``f30!}, 41\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  37, 41, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 8:27-39\index{44 Acts:ch.   8, v.  27-39, pg.
``f30!}.} of conforming\index{Sanctification:conforming to image of Christ ``f10!} them to his
image\index{Mankind:image of God ``f10!},\footnote{\ 2 Corinthians 3:18\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   3, v.  18, pg.
``f30!}.} and subduing them\index{Holy Spirit:subdues will of man ``f10!} to his will;\footnote{\ 2 Corinthians
10:4-6\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.  10, v.   4-6, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 6:17\index{45 Romans:ch.   6, v.  17, pg.
``f30!}.} of strength\index{Sanctification:supply of strength from Holy Spirit ``f10!}ening them\index{Holy
Spirit:strengthens believers against temptation ``f10!} against temptations\index{Temptation:temptation ``f10!} and
corruptions\index{Sanctification:Holy Spirit strengthens against corruptions ``f10!};\footnote{\ Matthew 4:4\index{40
Matthew:ch.   4, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}, 7, 10\index{40 Matthew:ch.   4, v.   4, 7, 10, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians
6:16\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   6, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}{}-17\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   6, v.  16-17, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm
19:11\index{19 Psalms:ch.  19, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 10:11\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  10, v.  11, pg.
``f30!}.} of building them\index{Holy Spirit:builds up the elect ``f10!} up in grace\index{Grace:in believers:by Holy
Spirit ``f10!},\footnote{\ Acts 20:32\index{44 Acts:ch.  20, v.  32, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Timothy 3:15\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.
  3, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}{}-17\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   3, v.  15-17, pg. ``f30!}.} and establishing their hearts in
holiness and\index{Believers:holy:being perfected ``f10!} comfort through\index{Faith:source of comfort ``f10!} faith
unto salvation\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Romans 1:16\index{45 Romans:ch.   1, v. 
16, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 10:1\index{45 Romans:ch.  10, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}3-17\index{45 Romans:ch.  10, v.  13-17, pg.
``f30!}; Romans 15:4\index{45 Romans:ch.  15, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 16:2\index{45 Romans:ch.  16, v.   2, pg.
``f30!}5\index{45 Romans:ch.  16, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Thessalonians 3:2, 10-11, 13\index{52 1 Thessalonians:ch.   3,
v.   2, 10-11, 13, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 156 \textit{Is the word of God to be read}\index{Scripture:to be:read and heard ``f10!}\textit{ by all?}

A. Although all are not to be permitted to read\index{Scripture:to be:read and heard ``f10!} the word publicly to the
congregation\index{Scripture:not all permitted to read to congregation ``f10!},\footnote{\ Deuteronomy 31:9,
11-13\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.  31, v.   9, 11-13, pg. ``f30!}; Nehemiah 8:2-3\index{16 Nehemiah:ch.   8, v.   2-3, pg.
``f30!}; Nehemiah 9:3-5\index{16 Nehemiah:ch.   9, v.   3-5, pg. ``f30!}.} yet all sorts of people are bound to read it
apart by themselves,\footnote{\ Deuteronomy 17:19\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.  17, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}; Revelation
1:3\index{66 Revelation:ch.   1, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}; John 5:39\index{43 John:ch.   5, v.  39, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah
34:16\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  34, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}.} and with their families\index{family, natural
``f10!}:\footnote{\ Deuteronomy 6:6\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.   6, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}{}-9\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.   6,
v.   6-9, pg. ``f30!}; Genesis 18:17, 19\index{01 Genesis:ch.  18, v.  17, 19, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 78:5\index{19
Psalms:ch.  78, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}{}-7\index{19 Psalms:ch.  78, v.   5-7, pg. ``f30!}.} to which end, the
holy\index{Scripture:holy ``f10!} scriptures are\index{Scripture:word of God:revelation ``f10!} to be
translated\index{Scripture:to be:translated into common (vulgar) languages ``f10!} out of the original into vulgar
languages.\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 14:6, 9, 11-12, 15-16, 24, 27-28\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  14, v.   6, 9, 11-12,
15-16, 24, 27-28, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 157 \textit{How is the word of God to be read}\index{Scripture:to be:read and heard ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The holy\index{Scripture:holy ``f10!} scriptures are\index{Scripture:word of God:revelation ``f10!} to be
read\index{Scripture:to be:read and heard ``f10!} with an high and reverent\index{Scripture:to be:treated with reverent
esteem ``f10!} esteem of them\index{Scripture:to be:esteemed ``f10!};\footnote{\ Psalm 19:10\index{19 Psalms:ch.  19,
v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; Nehemiah 8:3-10\index{16 Nehemiah:ch.   8, v.   3-10, pg. ``f30!}; Exodus 24:7\index{02 Exodus:ch.
 24, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Chronicles 34:27\index{14 2 Chronicles:ch.  34, v.  27, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 66:2\index{23
Isaiah:ch.  66, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}.} with a firm persuasion\index{Scripture:authored by God ``f10!} that they are the
very word of God,\footnote{\ 2 Peter 1:19\index{61 2 Peter:ch.   1, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}{}-21\index{61 2 Peter:ch.   1,
v.  19-21, pg. ``f30!}.} and that he only can enable\index{Scripture:understanding enabled by Holy Spirit ``f10!} us to
understand them;\footnote{\ Luke 24:45\index{42 Luke:ch.  24, v.  45, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Corinthians 3:13-16\index{47 2
Corinthians:ch.   3, v.  13-16, pg. ``f30!}.} with desire to know\index{God's law:desire to know and obey ``f10!},
believe, and obey the will\index{Scripture:to be:obeyed:will of God ``f10!} of God revealed in
them;\footnote{\ Deuteronomy 17:10, 20\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.  17, v.  10, 20, pg. ``f30!}.} with
diligence,\footnote{\ Acts 17:11\index{44 Acts:ch.  17, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}.} and attention
to\index{Scripture:diligence in application ``f10!} the matter and scope of them;\footnote{\ Acts 8:30, 34\index{44
Acts:ch.   8, v.  30, 34, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 10:26-28\index{42 Luke:ch.  10, v.  26-28, pg. ``f30!}.} with
meditation\index{meditation ``f10!},\footnote{\ Psalm 1:2\index{19 Psalms:ch.   1, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm
119:97\index{19 Psalms:ch. 119, v.  97, pg. ``f30!}.} application,\footnote{\ 2 Chronicles 24:21\index{14 2
Chronicles:ch.  24, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}.} self-denial\index{Prayer:with self-denial ``f10!},\footnote{\ Proverbs
3:5\index{20 Proverbs:ch.   3, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}; Deuteronomy 33:3\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.  33, v.   3, pg.
``f30!}.} and prayer.\footnote{\ Proverbs 2:1\index{20 Proverbs:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}{}-6\index{20 Proverbs:ch. 
 2, v.   1-6, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 119:18\index{19 Psalms:ch. 119, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}; Nehemiah 7:6, 8\index{16
Nehemiah:ch.   7, v.   6, 8, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 158 \textit{By whom is the word of God to be preached?}

A. The word of God is to be preached only by such as are sufficiently gifted\index{Preachers:to be:sufficiently gifted
``f10!},\footnote{\ 1 Timothy 3:2\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   3, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}, 6\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   3, v.  
2, 6, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 4:8\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}{}-11\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.  
8-11, pg. ``f30!}; Hosea 4:6\index{28 Hosea:ch.   4, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; Malachi 2:7\index{39 Malachi:ch.   2, v.   7,
pg. ``f30!}; 2 Corinthians 3:6\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   3, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}.} and also duly approved
and\index{Preachers:only gifted, approved, and called ``f10!} called to that office\index{Preachers:called to office
``f10!}.\footnote{\ Jeremiah 14:15\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  14, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 10:1\index{45 Romans:ch.  10,
v.   1, pg. ``f30!}5\index{45 Romans:ch.  10, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 5:4\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   5, v.   4, pg.
``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 12:28\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  12, v.  28, pg. ``f30!}{}-29\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  12,
v.  28-29, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Timothy 3:1\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   3, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}0\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   3, v. 
10, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Timothy 4:1\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   4, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}4\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   4, v.  14, pg.
``f30!}; 1 Timothy 5:22\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   5, v.  22, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 159 \textit{How is the word of God to be preached by those}\index{Preaching:sound doctrine ``f10!}\textit{ that are
called thereunto?}

A. They that are called to labor in the\index{Preachers:labor in ministry of the word ``f10!} ministry of the
word\index{Preaching:ministry of the Word ``f10!}, are to preach sound\index{Preaching:sound doctrine ``f10!}
doctrine,\footnote{\ Titus 2:1, 8\index{56 Titus:ch.   2, v.   1, 8, pg. ``f30!}.}
diligently,\index{Preaching:diligently ``f10!}\footnote{\ Acts 18:25\index{44 Acts:ch.  18, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}.} in
season and\index{Preaching:in all seasons ``f10!} out of season\index{Preaching:plainly ``f10!};\footnote{\ 2 Timothy
4:2\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   4, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}.} plainly,\index{Preaching:plain, not enticing words
``f10!}\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 14:19\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  14, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}.} not in the
enticing\index{Preaching:not enticing words of man's wisdom ``f10!} words of man's wisdom\index{wisdom, man's ``f10!},
but in demonstration\index{Preaching:demonstration of the Spirit ``f10!} of the Spirit, and of power\index{Preachers:to
demonstrate power ``f10!};\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 2:4\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   2, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.}
faithfully\index{Preaching:faithfully ``f10!},\footnote{\ Jeremiah 23:28\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  23, v.  28, pg.
``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 4:1\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   4, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}{}-2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   4, v.  
1-2, pg. ``f30!}.} making known the whole counsel of God\index{Causation:God's own will ``f10!};\footnote{\ Acts
20:27\index{44 Acts:ch.  20, v.  27, pg. ``f30!}.} wisely,\footnote{\ Colossians 1:28\index{51 Colossians:ch.   1, v. 
28, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Timothy 2:15\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   2, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}.} applying themselves to the
necessities and capacities\index{Preachers:wisely target capacities of hearers ``f10!} of the
hearers\index{Preaching:target capacities of hearers ``f10!};\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 3:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  
3, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 5:12-14\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   5, v.  12-14, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 12:42\index{42 Luke:ch. 
12, v.  42, pg. ``f30!}.} zealously\index{Preachers:to have zeal for souls of men ``f10!},\footnote{\ Acts
18:25\index{44 Acts:ch.  18, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}.} with fervent love to God\index{Love toward God:for God
``f10!}\footnote{\ 2 Corinthians 5:13-14\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   5, v.  13-14, pg. ``f30!}; Philippians
1:1\index{50 Philippians:ch.   1, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}5-17\index{50 Philippians:ch.   1, v.  15-17, pg. ``f30!}.} and
the souls of his people;\footnote{\ Colossians 4:12\index{51 Colossians:ch.   4, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Corinthians
12:15\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.  12, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}.} sincerely,\footnote{\ 2 Corinthians 2:17\index{47 2
Corinthians:ch.   2, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Corinthians 4:2\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   4, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}.}
aiming at his glory\index{Preaching:for God's glory ``f10!},\footnote{\ 1 Thessalonians 2:4\index{52 1
Thessalonians:ch.   2, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}{}-6\index{52 1 Thessalonians:ch.   2, v.   4-6, pg. ``f30!}; John
7:18\index{43 John:ch.   7, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}.} and their conversion\index{Conversion:conversion
``f10!},\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 9:19-22\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   9, v.  19-22, pg. ``f30!}.}
edification,\index{Holy Spirit:edification of believers ``f10!}\footnote{\ 2 Corinthians 12:19\index{47 2
Corinthians:ch.  12, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 4:12\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}.} and
salvation\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!}.\footnote{\ 1 Timothy 4:1\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   4, v.  
1, pg. ``f30!}6\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   4, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 26:16-18\index{44 Acts:ch.  26, v.  16-18, pg.
``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 160 \textit{What is required of those that hear the word preached}\index{Preaching:preparation for ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. It is required of those that hear the word preached\index{Preaching:preparation for ``f10!}, that they attend upon it
with diligence\index{Preaching:diligence in application ``f10!},\footnote{\ Proverbs 8:34\index{20 Proverbs:ch.   8, v.
 34, pg. ``f30!}.} preparation,\footnote{\ 1 Peter 2:1-2\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   2, v.   1-2, pg. ``f30!}; Luke
8:18\index{42 Luke:ch.   8, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}.} and prayer;\footnote{\ Psalm 119:18\index{19 Psalms:ch. 119, v.  18,
pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 6:18\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   6, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}{}-19\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   6, v.  18-19,
pg. ``f30!}.} examine: What\index{Scripture:to be:used to examine all doctrines ``f10!} they hear by the
scriptures\index{Scripture:to be:read and heard ``f10!};\footnote{\ Acts 17:11\index{44 Acts:ch.  17, v.  11, pg.
``f30!}.} receive the truth\index{Scripture:truth to be received with faith ``f10!} with faith,\footnote{\ Hebrews
4:2\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   4, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}.} love,\footnote{\ 2 Thessalonians 2:10\index{53 2 Thessalonians:ch. 
 2, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}.} meekness\index{Love for others:meekness ``f10!},\footnote{\ James 1:21\index{59 James:ch.  
1, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}.} and readiness of mind,\index{Preaching:hearing:readiness of mind ``f10!}\footnote{\ Acts
17:11\index{44 Acts:ch.  17, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}.} as the word of God;\footnote{\ 1 Thessalonians 2:13\index{52 1
Thessalonians:ch.   2, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}.} meditate\index{meditation ``f10!},\footnote{\ Luke 9:44\index{42 Luke:ch. 
 9, v.  44, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 2:1\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}.} and confer of it;\footnote{\ Luke
24:14\index{42 Luke:ch.  24, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}; Deuteronomy 6:6\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.   6, v.   6, pg.
``f30!}{}-7\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.   6, v.   6-7, pg. ``f30!}.} hide\index{Preaching:hearing:hiding in heart ``f10!}
it in their hearts\index{Heart:word preached hidden in ``f10!},\footnote{\ Proverbs 2:1\index{20 Proverbs:ch.   2, v.  
1, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 119:11\index{19 Psalms:ch. 119, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}.} and bring forth the fruit of it in their
lives.\footnote{\ Luke 8:15\index{42 Luke:ch.   8, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}; James 1:25\index{59 James:ch.   1, v.  25, pg.
``f30!}.}

Q. 161 \textit{How do the sacraments}\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!}\textit{ become
effectual}\index{Sacraments:effectual means of salvation ``f10!}\textit{ means of salvation}\index{Salvation:belief in
Jesus by faith ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The sacraments\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!} become effectual\index{Sacraments:effectual means of
salvation ``f10!} means of salvation\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!}, not by any
power\index{Sacraments:no power in themselves ``f10!} in themselves, or any virtue\index{Sacraments:grace:not conferred
by elements ``f10!} derived from the piety or\index{Lord's Supper:efficacy, not dependent on piety or intention of
person administering ``f10!} intention of him by whom they are administered, but only\index{Sacraments:no virtue from
person administering ``f10!} by the working of the\index{Sacraments:Holy Spirit working ``f10!} Holy Ghost\index{Holy
Spirit:Holy Ghost ``f10!}, and the blessing of Christ, by whom they are instituted\index{Sacraments:instituted
by:Christ ``f10!}.\footnote{\ 1 Peter 3:21\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   3, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 8:13, 23\index{44
Acts:ch.   8, v.  13, 23, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 3:6-7\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   3, v.   6-7, pg. ``f30!}; 1
Corinthians 12:13\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  12, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 162 \textit{What is a sacrament}\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. A sacrament\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!} is a holy ordinance instituted by
Christ\index{Sacraments:instituted by:Christ ``f10!} in his church\index{Church:Christ's ``f10!},\footnote{\ Genesis
17:7\index{01 Genesis:ch.  17, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}, 10\index{01 Genesis:ch.  17, v.   7, 10, pg. ``f30!}; Exodus 12;
Matthew 26:26\index{40 Matthew:ch.  26, v.  26, pg. ``f30!}{}-28\index{40 Matthew:ch.  26, v.  26-28, pg. ``f30!};
Matthew 28:19\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}.} to signify\index{Sacraments:holy:signs ``f10!}, seal,
and\index{Sacraments:seals of covenant of grace ``f10!} exhibit\footnote{\ Romans 4:11\index{45 Romans:ch.   4, v.  11,
pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 11:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}4\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.
 24, pg. ``f30!}{}-25\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  24-25, pg. ``f30!}.} unto those that are within the covenant
of grace\index{Covenant:grace:grace ``f10!},\footnote{\ Romans 15:8\index{45 Romans:ch.  15, v.   8, pg. ``f30!};
Exodus 12:48\index{02 Exodus:ch.  12, v.  48, pg. ``f30!}.} the benefits of his mediation\index{Jesus:mediator:of
covenant ``f10!};\footnote{\ Acts 2:38\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  38, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 10:16\index{46 1
Corinthians:ch.  10, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}.} to strengthen and\index{Believers:benefits:of Christ's mediation ``f10!}
increase their faith\index{Faith:increase of ``f10!}, and all other graces\index{Grace:exhibited in sacraments
``f10!};\footnote{\ Romans 4:11\index{45 Romans:ch.   4, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 3:27\index{48 Galatians:ch.  
3, v.  27, pg. ``f30!}.} to oblige them to obedience\index{God's law:commandments:obedience:required
``f10!};\footnote{\ Romans 6:3-4\index{45 Romans:ch.   6, v.   3-4, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 10:21\index{46 1
Corinthians:ch.  10, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}.} to testify\index{Sacraments:testimony through participation ``f10!} and
cherish their love\index{Love for others:for saints ``f10!} and communion one\index{Communion:of saints ``f10!} with
another;\footnote{\ Ephesians 4:2-5\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.   2-5, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 12:13\index{46 1
Corinthians:ch.  12, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}.} and to distinguish\index{Sacraments:distinguish from those who are outside
``f10!} them from those that are without.\footnote{\ Ephesians 2:1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   1, pg.
``f30!}1-12\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.  11-12, pg. ``f30!}; Genesis 34:14\index{01 Genesis:ch.  34, v.  14, pg.
``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 163 \textit{What are the parts of a sacrament}\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The parts of a sacrament\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!} are two; the one an outward and sensible sign,
used\index{Sacraments:sensible signs ``f10!} according to Christ's own appointment; the\index{Lord's Supper:proper
administration ``f10!} other an inward\index{Sacraments:outward sign, inward grace ``f10!} and spiritual
grace\index{Grace:exhibited in sacraments ``f10!} thereby signified.\footnote{\ Matthew 3:11\index{40 Matthew:ch.   3,
v.  11, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Peter 3:21\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   3, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 2:28-29\index{45 Romans:ch.  
2, v.  28-29, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 164 \textit{How many sacraments}\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!}\textit{ has Christ instituted
in}\index{Sacraments:instituted by:Christ ``f10!}\textit{ his church}\index{Church:Christ's ``f10!}\textit{ under the
New Testament}\index{Scripture:New Testament ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. Under the New Testament\index{Scripture:New Testament ``f10!} Christ has instituted in\index{Sacraments:instituted
by:Christ ``f10!} his church\index{Church:Christ's ``f10!} only two sacraments\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances
``f10!}, Baptism and\index{Baptism:sacrament ``f10!} the Lord's supper\index{Lord's Supper:sacrament
``f10!}.\footnote{\ Matthew 26:26\index{40 Matthew:ch.  26, v.  26, pg. ``f30!}{}-28\index{40 Matthew:ch.  26, v. 
26-28, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 28:19\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 11:2\index{46 1
Corinthians:ch.  11, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}0\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}, 23\index{46 1
Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  20, 23, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 165 \textit{What is Baptism}\index{Baptism:definition ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. Baptism is a\index{Baptism:sacrament ``f10!} sacrament\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!} of the New
Testament\index{Scripture:New Testament ``f10!}, wherein Christ has ordained the\index{Baptism:ordained by Jesus
``f10!} washing\index{Baptism:washing with water ``f10!} with water in\index{Baptism:to use water ``f10!} the name of
the Father\index{Father:God the ``f10!}, and of the Son\index{Jesus:Son of God ``f10!}, and of the Holy
Ghost\index{Holy Spirit:Holy Ghost ``f10!},\footnote{\ Matthew 28:19\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}.} to
be a sign\index{Baptism:sign of salvation ``f10!} and seal of\index{Baptism:seal of salvationof ``f10!}
ingrafting\index{Believers:ingrafted into Christ ``f10!} into himself,\footnote{\ Galatians 3:27\index{48 Galatians:ch.
  3, v.  27, pg. ``f30!}.} of remission\index{Redemption:remission of sins ``f10!} of sins by his
blood\index{Jesus:shed blood for remission of sins ``f10!},\footnote{\ Mark 1:4\index{41 Mark:ch.   1, v.   4, pg.
``f30!}; Revelation 1:5\index{66 Revelation:ch.   1, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.} and
regeneration\index{Regeneration:regeneration ``f10!} by his Spirit;\footnote{\ Titus 3:5\index{56 Titus:ch.   3, v.  
5, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 5:2\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   5, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}6\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   5, v.  26, pg.
``f30!}.} of adoption\index{Adoption:in salvation ``f10!},\footnote{\ Galatians 3:26-27\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v. 
26-27, pg. ``f30!}.} and resurrection unto\index{Resurrection:believers:to everlasting life ``f10!} everlasting
life\index{everlasting life ``f10!};\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 15:29\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  15, v.  29, pg.
``f30!}; Romans 6:5\index{45 Romans:ch.   6, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.} and whereby the parties baptized are solemnly
admitted into\index{Baptism:admission into visible Church ``f10!} the visible church\index{Church:visible
``f10!},\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 12:13\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  12, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}.} and enter into an open
and professed engagement to be\index{Oaths and Vows:engagements to God ``f10!} wholly and only the
Lord's.\footnote{\ Romans 6:4\index{45 Romans:ch.   6, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 166 \textit{Unto whom is}\index{Baptism:recipients ``f10!}\textit{ Baptism to be administered?}

A. Baptism is not to be administered to any\index{Baptism:not to be administered outside those in visible church ``f10!}
that are out of the visible church\index{Church:visible ``f10!}, and so strangers\index{Baptism:not for strangers from
covenant of promise ``f10!} from the covenant of promise\index{Covenant:promises ``f10!}, till they profess their
faith\index{Faith:profession of ``f10!} in Christ, and obedience\index{God's law:commandments:obedience:required
``f10!} to him,\footnote{\ Acts 2:38\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  38, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 8:36-37\index{44 Acts:ch.   8, v.
 36-37, pg. ``f30!}.} but infants\index{Infants:of believing parents, to be baptized ``f10!} descending from
parents\index{Baptism:infants of believing parents ``f10!}, either both, or but one of them, professing
faith\index{Faith:professed in baptism ``f10!} in Christ, and obedience to him, are in that respect within the
covenant\index{Covenant:new:ways dispensed ``f10!}, and to be baptized\index{Baptism:required as obedience
``f10!}.\footnote{\ Genesis 17:7\index{01 Genesis:ch.  17, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}, 9\index{01 Genesis:ch.  17, v.   7, 9,
pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 3:9, 14\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.   9, 14, pg. ``f30!}; Colossians 2:11-12\index{51
Colossians:ch.   2, v.  11-12, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 2:38\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  38, pg. ``f30!}{}-39\index{44 Acts:ch.
  2, v.  38-39, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 4:11\index{45 Romans:ch.   4, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}{}-12\index{45 Romans:ch.   4, v. 
11-12, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 11:16\index{45 Romans:ch.  11, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 7:14\index{46 1
Corinthians:ch.   7, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 28:19\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}; Luke
18:1\index{42 Luke:ch.  18, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}5\index{42 Luke:ch.  18, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}{}-16\index{42 Luke:ch.  18,
v.  15-16, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 167 \textit{How is our Baptism to be improved by us?}

A. The needful but much neglected\index{Baptism:improvement of ``f10!} duty of improving\index{Baptism:duty of improving
``f10!} our Baptism, is to be performed by us all our life long, especially in the time of
temptation\index{Temptation:temptation ``f10!}, and when we are present at the administration\index{Baptism:efficacy
not time dependent ``f10!} of it to others;\footnote{\ Colossians 2:11-12\index{51 Colossians:ch.   2, v.  11-12, pg.
``f30!}; Romans 6:4\index{45 Romans:ch.   6, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}, 6, 11\index{45 Romans:ch.   6, v.   4, 6, 11, pg.
``f30!}.}[1] by serious\index{Sacraments:improving by serious reflection ``f10!} and thankful\index{Prayer:thanking God
``f10!} consideration of the nature of it, and of the ends for which Christ instituted it\index{Baptism:instituted by
Christ ``f10!}, the privileges\index{Believers:privileges ``f10!} and benefits conferred\index{Baptism:benefits
conferred ``f10!} and sealed thereby\index{Baptism:benefits sealed ``f10!}, and our solemn vow
made\index{Baptism:solemn vow made ``f10!} therein;\footnote{\ Romans 6:3-5\index{45 Romans:ch.   6, v.   3-5, pg.
``f30!}.} by being humbled\index{Humility:before God ``f10!} for our sinful defilement\index{Sin:defilement ``f10!},
our falling\index{God's law:broken daily by believers ``f10!} short of, and walking contrary\index{Baptism:not to
walking contrary ``f10!} to, the grace\index{Grace:exhibited in sacraments ``f10!} of baptism, and\index{Baptism:means
of grace ``f10!} our engagements\index{Oaths and Vows:engagements to God ``f10!};\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians
1:11-13\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   1, v.  11-13, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 6:2-3\index{45 Romans:ch.   6, v.   2-3, pg.
``f30!}.} by growing up\index{Assurance:growing ``f10!} to assurance\index{Assurance:of pardon of sin ``f10!} of pardon
of sin, and of all other blessings\index{Baptism:blessings sealed ``f10!} sealed to us in that
sacrament\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!};\footnote{\ Romans 4:11\index{45 Romans:ch.   4, v.  11, pg.
``f30!}{}-12\index{45 Romans:ch.   4, v.  11-12, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Peter 3:21\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   3, v.  21, pg.
``f30!}.} by drawing strength\index{Baptism:drawing strength from ``f10!} from the death\index{Jesus:resurrection:from
the dead ``f10!} and resurrection of Christ, into whom we are baptized\index{Baptism:into Christ ``f10!}, for the
mortifying\index{Sin:mortified ``f10!} of sin, and quickening of grace;\index{Grace:in believers:by Holy Spirit
``f10!}\footnote{\ Romans 6:3-5\index{45 Romans:ch.   6, v.   3-5, pg. ``f30!}.} and by endeavoring to live by
faith\index{Faith:living by ``f10!},\footnote{\ Galatians 3:26-27\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.  26-27, pg. ``f30!}.}
to have our conversation\index{Believers:to walk faithfully in obedience (conversation) ``f10!} in holiness
and\index{Believers:holy:being perfected ``f10!} righteousness,\footnote{\ Romans 6:22\index{45 Romans:ch.   6, v.  22,
pg. ``f30!}.} as those that have therein given up their names to Christ;\footnote{\ Acts 2:38\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.
 38, pg. ``f30!}.} and to walk in brotherly\index{Love for others:for saints ``f10!} love, as being
baptized\index{Baptism:by Spirit ``f10!} by the same Spirit\index{Holy Spirit:believers baptized by, into one body
``f10!} into one body.\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 12:13\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  12, v.  13, pg. ``f30!},
25-27\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  12, v.  13, 25-27, pg. ``f30!}.}
