\bigskip


Q. 168 \textit{What is the Lord's supper}\index{Lord's Supper:sacrament ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The Lord's supper\index{Lord's Supper:sacrament ``f10!} is a sacrament\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!} of
the New Testament\index{Scripture:New Testament ``f10!},\footnote{\ Luke 22:20\index{42 Luke:ch.  22, v.  20, pg.
``f30!}.} wherein, by giving and receiving\index{Lord's Supper:defined ``f10!} bread and\index{Lord's Supper:bread
``f10!} wine\index{Lord's Supper:wine ``f10!} according to the appointment of\index{Lord's Supper:proper administration
``f10!} Jesus Christ, his death\index{Jesus:death:death ``f10!} is showed forth; and they that worthily\index{Lord's
Supper:spiritual feeding:worthy receivers ``f10!} communicate feed\index{Lord's Supper:spiritual feeding:in faith
``f10!} upon his body and blood\index{Lord's Supper:body and blood of Jesus ``f10!}, to their spiritual
nourishment\index{Lord's Supper:spiritual feeding:nourishment ``f10!} and growth in
grace\index{Sanctification:spiritual growth:in grace ``f10!};\footnote{\ Matthew 26:26\index{40 Matthew:ch.  26, v. 
26, pg. ``f30!}{}-28\index{40 Matthew:ch.  26, v.  26-28, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 11:13-26\index{46 1
Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  13-26, pg. ``f30!}.} have their union and\index{Believers:union with Christ:mystical ``f10!}
communion with him\index{Communion:with Christ ``f10!} confirmed\index{Sacraments:confirm union with Christ
``f10!};\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 10:16\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  10, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}.}
testify\index{Sacraments:testimony through participation ``f10!} and renew their thankfulness\index{Prayer:thanking God
``f10!},\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 11:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}4\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch. 
11, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}.} and engagement to God\index{Oaths and Vows:engagements to God ``f10!},\footnote{\ 1
Corinthians 10:14-16, 21\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  10, v.  14-16, 21, pg. ``f30!}.} and their mutual love\index{Love
for others:mutual:love ``f10!} and fellowship each\index{Fellowship:with fellow believers ``f10!} with other, as
members of the\index{Church members ``f10!} same mystical body.\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 10:17\index{46 1
Corinthians:ch.  10, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 169 \textit{How has Christ appointed bread and}\index{Lord's Supper:bread ``f10!}\textit{ wine}\index{Lord's
Supper:wine ``f10!}\textit{ to be given and received in the sacrament}\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!}\textit{
of the Lord's supper}\index{Lord's Supper:sacrament ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. Christ has appointed the ministers\index{Church officers:minsters ``f10!} of his word, in the administration of
this\index{Lord's Supper:ministers to administer ``f10!} sacrament\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!} of the
Lord's Supper\index{Lord's Supper:sacrament ``f10!}, to set apart the bread and\index{Lord's Supper:bread ``f10!}
wine\index{Lord's Supper:wine ``f10!} from common use, by the word of institution\index{Sacraments:instituted by:Christ
``f10!}, thanksgiving\index{Prayer:thanking God ``f10!}, and prayer; to\index{Prayer:Jesus institution of Lord's Supper
``f10!} take and break the\index{Lord's Supper:bread broken ``f10!} bread, and to give both the bread and the wine to
the communicants\index{Lord's Supper:both bread and wine to communicants ``f10!}: who are, by the same appointment, to
take\index{Lord's Supper:proper administration ``f10!} and eat the bread, and to drink the wine, in thankful
remembrance that\index{Lord's Supper:remembrance of Christ's sacrifice ``f10!} the body of Christ was broken and given,
and his blood\index{Jesus:shed blood for remission of sins ``f10!} shed, for them.\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians
11:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}3\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  23, pg.
``f30!}{}-24\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  23-24, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 26:26\index{40 Matthew:ch.  26, v.  26,
pg. ``f30!}{}-28\index{40 Matthew:ch.  26, v.  26-28, pg. ``f30!}; Mark 14:22-24\index{41 Mark:ch.  14, v.  22-24, pg.
``f30!}; Luke 22:19\index{42 Luke:ch.  22, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}{}-20\index{42 Luke:ch.  22, v.  19-20, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 170 \textit{How do they that worthily}\index{Lord's Supper:spiritual feeding:worthy receivers ``f10!}\textit{
communicate in}\index{Lord's Supper:communion ``f10!}\textit{ the Lord's supper}\index{Lord's Supper:sacrament
``f10!}\textit{ feed}\index{Lord's Supper:spiritual feeding:in faith ``f10!}\textit{ upon the body and
blood}\index{Lord's Supper:body and blood of Jesus ``f10!}\textit{ of Christ therein?}

A. As the body and blood\index{Lord's Supper:body and blood of Jesus ``f10!} of Christ are not corporally\index{Lord's
Supper:spiritual feeding:not corporal ``f10!} or carnally\index{Lord's Supper:spiritual feeding:not carnal ``f10!}
present in, with, or under the bread and\index{Lord's Supper:bread ``f10!} wine\index{Lord's Supper:wine ``f10!} in the
Lord's supper\index{Lord's Supper:sacrament ``f10!},\footnote{\ Acts 3:21\index{44 Acts:ch.   3, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}.}
and yet are spiritually\index{Lord's Supper:spiritual feeding:worthy receivers ``f10!} present to the
faith\index{Faith:profession of ``f10!} of the receiver, no less truly and really than the elements\index{Lord's
Supper:elements:bread and wine ``f10!} themselves are to their outward\index{Lord's Supper:elements:outward senses
``f10!} senses;\footnote{\ Matthew 26:26\index{40 Matthew:ch.  26, v.  26, pg. ``f30!}, 28\index{40 Matthew:ch.  26, v.
 26, 28, pg. ``f30!}.} so they that worthily communicate in\index{Lord's Supper:communion ``f10!} the
sacrament\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!} of the Lord's supper, do therein feed\index{Lord's Supper:spiritual
feeding:in faith ``f10!} upon the body and blood of Christ, not after a corporal and carnal, but in a spiritual manner;
yet truly and really,\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 11:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}4\index{46 1
Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}{}-29\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  24-29, pg. ``f30!}.} while by
faith\index{Faith:in Jesus Christ ``f10!} they receive and apply unto themselves Christ crucified\index{Jesus:crucified
``f10!}, and all the benefits of his death\index{Jesus:death:death ``f10!}.\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 10:16\index{46 1
Corinthians:ch.  10, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 171 \textit{How are they that receive the sacrament}\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!}\textit{ of the Lord's
supper}\index{Lord's Supper:sacrament ``f10!}\textit{ to prepare themselves}\index{Lord's Supper:preparation:actions
``f10!}\textit{ before they come unto it?}

A. They that receive the sacrament\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!} of the Lord's supper\index{Lord's
Supper:sacrament ``f10!} are, before they come, to prepare themselves\index{Lord's Supper:preparation:actions ``f10!}
thereunto, by examining\index{Lord's Supper:preparation:self-examination ``f10!} themselves\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians
11:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}8\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  28, pg. ``f30!}.} of
their being in Christ,\footnote{\ 2 Corinthians 13:5\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.  13, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.} of their
sins and wants;\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 5:7\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   5, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}; Exodus 12:15\index{02
Exodus:ch.  12, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}.} of the truth and\index{Lord's Supper:evidence of true faith required ``f10!}
measure of their knowledge,\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 11:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}9\index{46
1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  29, pg. ``f30!}.} faith,\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 13:5\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  13, v.  
5, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 26:28\index{40 Matthew:ch.  26, v.  28, pg. ``f30!}.} repentance;\index{Repentance:for all sins
``f10!}\footnote{\ Zechariah 12:10\index{38 Zechariah:ch.  12, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 11:31\index{46 1
Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  31, pg. ``f30!}.} love to God\index{Love toward God:for God ``f10!} and the
brethren\index{Believers:to build up fellow believers ``f10!},\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 10:16\index{46 1
Corinthians:ch.  10, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}{}-17\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  10, v.  16-17, pg. ``f30!}; Acts
2:46-47\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  46-47, pg. ``f30!}.} charity\index{Good works:charity ``f10!} to all
men,\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 5:8\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   5, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 11:18, 20\index{46
1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  18, 20, pg. ``f30!}.} forgiving those\index{Forgiveness:forgiving ``f10!} that have done
them wrong;\footnote{\ Matthew 5:23-24\index{40 Matthew:ch.   5, v.  23-24, pg. ``f30!}.} of their desires
after\index{Lord's Supper:desire to be in Christ ``f10!} Christ,\footnote{\ Isaiah 55:1\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  55, v.  
1, pg. ``f30!}; John 7:37\index{43 John:ch.   7, v.  37, pg. ``f30!}.} and of their new
obedience\index{Believers:obedience:strive for new ``f10!};\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 5:7\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  
5, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}{}-8\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   5, v.   7-8, pg. ``f30!}.} and by renewing
the\index{Sanctification:renewed in image of God ``f10!} exercise of these graces\index{Grace:exhibited in sacraments
``f10!},\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 11:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}5\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch. 
11, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}{}-26\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  25-26, pg. ``f30!}, 28\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11,
v.  25-26, 28, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 10:21-22, 24\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  10, v.  21-22, 24, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm
26:6\index{19 Psalms:ch.  26, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}.} by serious\index{Sacraments:improving by serious reflection ``f10!}
meditation\index{meditation ``f10!},\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 11:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.   2, pg.
``f30!}4\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}{}-25\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  24-25, pg.
``f30!}.} and fervent\index{Prayer:with fervency ``f10!} prayer.\footnote{\ 2 Chronicles 30:18-19\index{14 2
Chronicles:ch.  30, v.  18-19, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 26:26\index{40 Matthew:ch.  26, v.  26, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 172 \textit{May one who doubts}\index{Assurance:doubts ``f10!}\textit{ of his being in Christ, or of his due
preparation, come}\index{Lord's Supper:preparation:actions ``f10!}\textit{ to the Lord's supper}\index{Lord's
Supper:sacrament ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. One who doubts\index{Assurance:doubts ``f10!} of his being in Christ, or of his due preparation to the\index{Lord's
Supper:preparation:actions ``f10!} sacrament\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!} of the Lord's supper\index{Lord's
Supper:sacrament ``f10!}, may have true interest in Christ\index{Believers:interest (share) in Christ ``f10!}, though
he be not yet assured thereof\index{Assurance:believer may await ``f10!};\footnote{\ Isaiah 1:10\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  
1, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 5:13\index{62 1 John:ch.   5, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 77:1-12\index{19 Psalms:ch. 
77, v.   1-12, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 88:1-18\index{19 Psalms:ch.  88, v.   1-18, pg. ``f30!}; Jonah 2:4, 7\index{32
Jonah:ch.   2, v.   4, 7, pg. ``f30!}.} and in God's account has it, if he be duly affected with the
apprehension\index{Lord's Supper:apprehension of interest in Christ ``f10!} of the want of it,\footnote{\ Isaiah
54:7-10\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  54, v.   7-10, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 5:3-4\index{40 Matthew:ch.   5, v.   3-4, pg. ``f30!};
Psalm 31:22\index{19 Psalms:ch.  31, v.  22, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 73:13, 22-23\index{19 Psalms:ch.  73, v.  13, 22-23,
pg. ``f30!}.} and unfeignedly desires to\index{Lord's Supper:desire to be in Christ ``f10!} be found in
Christ,\footnote{\ Philippians 3:8-9\index{50 Philippians:ch.   3, v.   8-9, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 10:17\index{19
Psalms:ch.  10, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 42:1-2, 5, 11\index{19 Psalms:ch.  42, v.   1-2, 5, 11, pg. ``f30!}.} and to
depart\index{Lord's Supper:preparation:depart from sin ``f10!} from iniquity:\footnote{\ 2 Timothy 2:19\index{55 2
Timothy:ch.   2, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 1:10\index{23 Isaiah:ch.   1, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 66:18-20\index{19
Psalms:ch.  66, v.  18-20, pg. ``f30!}.} in which case (because promises\index{Lord's Supper:promises of ``f10!} are
made, and this sacrament is appointed, for the relief\index{Lord's Supper:relief for weak and doubting faith ``f10!}
even of weak and doubting\index{doubting Christians ``f10!} Christians)\footnote{\ Isaiah 40:11, 29, 31\index{23
Isaiah:ch.  40, v.  11, 29, 31, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 11:28\index{40 Matthew:ch.  11, v.  28, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew
12:20\index{40 Matthew:ch.  12, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 26:28\index{40 Matthew:ch.  26, v.  28, pg. ``f30!}.} he
is to bewail\index{Lord's Supper:preparation:bewail sin ``f10!} his unbelief\index{unbelief (misbelief)
``f10!},\footnote{\ Mark 9:24\index{41 Mark:ch.   9, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}.} and labor to have his doubts
resolved;\index{Lord's Supper:preparation:resolve doubts ``f10!}\footnote{\ Acts 2:37\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  37,
pg. ``f30!}; Acts 16:30\index{44 Acts:ch.  16, v.  30, pg. ``f30!}.} and, so doing, he may and ought to come to the
Lord's supper, that he may be further strengthened\index{Sacraments:strengthening ordinances ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Romans
4:11\index{45 Romans:ch.   4, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 11:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.   2, pg.
``f30!}8\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  28, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 173 \textit{May any who profess the faith}\index{Faith:profession of ``f10!}\textit{, and desire to
come}\index{Lord's Supper:desire to attend ``f10!}\textit{ to the Lord's supper}\index{Lord's Supper:sacrament
``f10!}\textit{, be kept from it?}

A. Such as are found to be ignorant\index{ignorance ``f10!} or scandalous\index{Scandalous behaviour:behaviour ``f10!},
notwithstanding their profession\index{Faith:profession of ``f10!} of the faith, and desire to come\index{Lord's
Supper:desire to attend ``f10!} to the Lord's supper\index{Lord's Supper:sacrament ``f10!}, may and ought to be kept
from that sacrament\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!}, by the power which\index{Church:power delegated by Christ
``f10!} Christ has left in his church\index{Church:Christ's ``f10!},\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 5; 1 Corinthians
11:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}7\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  27, pg.
``f30!}{}-31\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  27-31, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 7:6\index{40 Matthew:ch.   7, v.   6, pg.
``f30!}; Jude 1:23\index{65 Jude:v.   1, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Timothy 5:22\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   5, v.  22, pg.
``f30!}.} until they receive instruction\index{Lord's Supper:unworthy participation ``f10!}, and manifest
their\index{Lord's Supper:ungodly not to be admitted ``f10!} reformation\index{Church discipline:suspension from Lord's
Supper ``f10!}.\footnote{\ 2 Corinthians 2:7\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   2, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 174 \textit{What is required of them that receive the sacrament}\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!}\textit{ of
the Lord's supper}\index{Lord's Supper:sacrament ``f10!}\textit{ in the time of the administration}\index{Lord's
Supper:proper administration ``f10!}\textit{ of it?}

A. It is required of them that receive the sacrament\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!} of the Lord's
supper\index{Lord's Supper:sacrament ``f10!}, that, during the time of the administration\index{Lord's Supper:proper
administration ``f10!} of it, with all holy\index{Lord's Supper:elements:holy use ``f10!} reverence and attention they
wait upon\index{Lord's Supper:waiting on God ``f10!} God in that ordinance,\footnote{\ Leviticus 10:3\index{03
Leviticus:ch.  10, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 12:1\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  12, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}8\index{58
Hebrews:ch.  12, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 5:7\index{19 Psalms:ch.   5, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 11:17,
26-27\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  17, 26-27, pg. ``f30!}.} diligently observe the\index{Lord's
Supper:elements:diligently observe ``f10!} sacramental\index{Lord's Supper:elements:union between sign and signified
``f10!} elements\index{Lord's Supper:elements:bread and wine ``f10!} and actions,\footnote{\ Exodus 24:8\index{02
Exodus:ch.  24, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 26:28\index{40 Matthew:ch.  26, v.  28, pg. ``f30!}.} heedfully discern
the\index{Lord's Supper:discern Lord's body ``f10!} Lord's body,\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 11:2\index{46 1
Corinthians:ch.  11, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}9\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  29, pg. ``f30!}.} and affectionately
meditate\index{meditation ``f10!} on his death\index{Jesus:death:death ``f10!} and sufferings,\footnote{\ Luke
22:19\index{42 Luke:ch.  22, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}.} and thereby stir\index{Grace:in believers:to be stirred up ``f10!}
up themselves to a vigorous exercise of their graces;\index{Grace:exhibited in sacraments ``f10!}\footnote{\ 1
Corinthians 10:3-5, 11, 14\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  10, v.   3-5, 11, 14, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 11:2\index{46 1
Corinthians:ch.  11, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}6\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  26, pg. ``f30!}.} in judging
themselves\index{Judgement:personal ``f10!},\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 11:31\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  31, pg.
``f30!}.} and sorrowing for sin\index{Confession:sorrow for sin ``f10!};\footnote{\ Zechariah 12:10\index{38
Zechariah:ch.  12, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}.} in earnest hungering\index{Believers:to hunger after Christ in Lord's Supper
``f10!} and thirsting\index{Lord's Supper:desire to be in Christ ``f10!} after Christ,\footnote{\ Revelation
22:17\index{66 Revelation:ch.  22, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}.} feeding\index{Lord's Supper:spiritual feeding:in faith ``f10!}
on him by faith,\footnote{\ John 6:35\index{43 John:ch.   6, v.  35, pg. ``f30!}.} receiving of
his\index{Faith:instrument:for receiving Christ ``f10!} fulness,\footnote{\ John 1:1\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.   1, pg.
``f30!}6\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}.} trusting in his\index{Lord's Supper:trusting in Christ's merits
``f10!} merits\index{Faith:trusts in the merits of Christ ``f10!},\footnote{\ Philippians 1:1\index{50 Philippians:ch. 
 1, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}6\index{50 Philippians:ch.   1, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}.} rejoicing in his\index{Lord's
Supper:rejoice in Christ ``f10!} love,\footnote{\ Psalm 63:4-5\index{19 Psalms:ch.  63, v.   4-5, pg. ``f30!}; 2
Chronicles 30:21\index{14 2 Chronicles:ch.  30, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}.} giving thanks\index{Prayer:thanking God ``f10!}
for his grace\index{Grace:thanks for ``f10!};\footnote{\ Psalm 22:26\index{19 Psalms:ch.  22, v.  26, pg. ``f30!}.} in
renewing of their covenant with\index{Covenant:renewal with God ``f10!} God, and love to all\index{Love for others:for
saints ``f10!} the saints\index{Believers:saints ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Jeremiah 1:5\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.   1, v.   5,
pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 1:5\index{19 Psalms:ch.   1, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 2:42\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  42, pg.
``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 175 \textit{What is the duty of Christians, after}\index{Lord's Supper:after participation:duty ``f10!}\textit{ they
have received the sacrament}\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!}\textit{ of the Lord's supper}\index{Lord's
Supper:sacrament ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The duty of Christians, after\index{Lord's Supper:after participation:duty ``f10!} they have received the
sacrament\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!} of the Lord's supper\index{Lord's Supper:sacrament ``f10!}, is
seriously\index{Lord's Supper:after participation:seriously consider behaviour ``f10!} to consider how they have
behaved\index{Lord's Supper:post assessment of behaviour during ``f10!} themselves therein, and with what
success;\footnote{\ Psalm 28:7\index{19 Psalms:ch.  28, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 85:8\index{19 Psalms:ch.  85, v.  
8, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 11:17, 30-31\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  17, 30-31, pg. ``f30!}.} if they find
quickening and comfort, to\index{Lord's Supper:benefits believers receive ``f10!} bless God\index{Lord's Supper:bless
God for it ``f10!} for it,\footnote{\ 2 Chronicles 30:21\index{14 2 Chronicles:ch.  30, v.  21, pg.
``f30!}{}-16\index{14 2 Chronicles:ch.  30, v.  21-16, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 2:42\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  42, pg.
``f30!}, 46\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  42, 46, pg. ``f30!}.} beg the continuance of it,\footnote{\ Psalm 36:10\index{19
Psalms:ch.  36, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; Song of Solomon 3:4\index{22 Song of Solomon:ch.   3, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}; 1
Chronicles 29:18\index{13 1 Chronicles:ch.  29, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}.} watch against\index{Temptation:watchfulness
required to avoid ``f10!} relapses\index{Lord's Supper:after participation:watch against relapses ``f10!},\footnote{\ 1
Corinthians 10:3-5, 12\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  10, v.   3-5, 12, pg. ``f30!}.} fulfil their\index{Oaths and
Vows:duty to fulfill ``f10!} vows,\footnote{\ Psalm 50:14\index{19 Psalms:ch.  50, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}.} and encourage
themselves to a frequent attendance\index{Lord's Supper:attendance to be frequent ``f10!} on that
ordinance:\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 11:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}5\index{46 1
Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}{}-26\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  25-26, pg. ``f30!}; Acts
2:42\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  42, pg. ``f30!}, 46\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  42, 46, pg. ``f30!}.} but if they find
no present benefit, more exactly to review their preparation to, and\index{Lord's Supper:preparation:actions ``f10!}
carriage at, the sacrament;\footnote{\ Song of Solomon 5:1-6\index{22 Song of Solomon:ch.   5, v.   1-6, pg. ``f30!};
Ecclesiastes 5:1\index{21 Ecclesiastes:ch.   5, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}{}-6\index{21 Ecclesiastes:ch.   5, v.   1-6, pg.
``f30!}.} in both which, if they can approve\index{Lord's Supper:after participation:application ``f10!} themselves to
God and their own consciences, they\index{Conscience:approved ``f10!} are to wait for\index{Lord's Supper:waiting on
God ``f10!} the fruit of it in due time:\footnote{\ Psalm 42:5, 8\index{19 Psalms:ch.  42, v.   5, 8, pg. ``f30!};
Psalm 43:3-5\index{19 Psalms:ch.  43, v.   3-5, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 123:1\index{19 Psalms:ch. 123, v.   1, pg.
``f30!}{}-2\index{19 Psalms:ch. 123, v.   1-2, pg. ``f30!}.} but, if they see they have failed\index{God's law:broken
daily by believers ``f10!} in either, they are to be humbled\index{Humility:before God ``f10!},\footnote{\ 2 Chronicles
30:18-19\index{14 2 Chronicles:ch.  30, v.  18-19, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 1:16, 18\index{23 Isaiah:ch.   1, v.  16, 18,
pg. ``f30!}.} and to attend upon it afterwards with more care and diligence\index{Lord's Supper:diligence in
application ``f10!}.\footnote{\ 2 Corinthians 7:1\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   7, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}1\index{47 2
Corinthians:ch.   7, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Chronicles 15:12-14\index{13 1 Chronicles:ch.  15, v.  12-14, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 176 \textit{Wherein do the sacraments}\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!}\textit{ of baptism
and}\index{Baptism:sacrament ``f10!}\textit{ the Lord's supper}\index{Lord's Supper:sacrament ``f10!}\textit{ agree?}

A. The sacraments\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!} of baptism and\index{Baptism:sacrament ``f10!} the Lord's
supper\index{Lord's Supper:sacrament ``f10!} agree, in that the author of both\index{Sacraments:God is author ``f10!}
is God;\footnote{\ Matthew 28:19\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 11:2\index{46 1
Corinthians:ch.  11, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}3\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}.} the spiritual
part\index{Sacraments:spiritual part is Christ ``f10!} of both is Christ and his
benefits\index{Sacraments:benefits:worthy believers receive ``f10!};\footnote{\ Romans 6:3-4\index{45 Romans:ch.   6,
v.   3-4, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 10:16\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  10, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}.} both are
seals\index{Sacraments:covenant seals ``f10!} of the same covenant,\index{Covenant:new:seals ``f10!}\footnote{\ Romans
4:11\index{45 Romans:ch.   4, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}; Colossians 2:12\index{51 Colossians:ch.   2, v.  12, pg. ``f30!};
Matthew 26:27-28\index{40 Matthew:ch.  26, v.  27-28, pg. ``f30!}.} are to be dispensed\index{Sacraments:dispensed by
minister of the Word ``f10!} by ministers\index{Church officers:minsters ``f10!} of the gospel\index{Gospel:gospel
``f10!}, and by none other;\footnote{\ John 1:3\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}3\index{43 John:ch.   1, v. 
33, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 28:19\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 4:1\index{46 1
Corinthians:ch.   4, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 11:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.   2, pg.
``f30!}3\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 5:4\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   5, v.   4, pg.
``f30!}.} and to be continued in the church of Christ\index{Church:Christ's ``f10!} until his second
coming\index{Jesus:second coming ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Matthew 28:19\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  19, pg.
``f30!}{}-20\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  19-20, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 11:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  
2, pg. ``f30!}6\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  26, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 177 \textit{Wherein do the sacraments}\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!}\textit{ of baptism
and}\index{Baptism:sacrament ``f10!}\textit{ the Lord's supper}\index{Lord's Supper:sacrament ``f10!}\textit{ differ?}

A. The sacraments\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!} of baptism and\index{Baptism:sacrament ``f10!} the Lord's
supper\index{Lord's Supper:sacrament ``f10!} differ, in that baptism is to be administered but once\index{Baptism:to be
administered once ``f10!}, with water, to\index{Baptism:to use water ``f10!} be a sign\index{Baptism:sign of salvation
``f10!} and seal of\index{Baptism:seal of salvationof ``f10!} our regeneration\index{Regeneration:regeneration ``f10!}
and ingrafting\index{Believers:ingrafted into Christ ``f10!} into Christ,\footnote{\ Matthew 3:11\index{40 Matthew:ch. 
 3, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}; Titus 3:5\index{56 Titus:ch.   3, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 3:27\index{48 Galatians:ch.  
3, v.  27, pg. ``f30!}.} and that even to infants\index{Infants:of believing parents, to be baptized
``f10!};\footnote{\ Genesis 17:7\index{01 Genesis:ch.  17, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}, 9\index{01 Genesis:ch.  17, v.   7, 9,
pg. ``f30!}; Acts 2:38\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  38, pg. ``f30!}{}-39\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  38-39, pg. ``f30!}; 1
Corinthians 7:14\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   7, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}.} whereas the Lord's supper is to be administered
often\index{Lord's Supper:administer often ``f10!}, in the elements\index{Lord's Supper:elements:bread and wine ``f10!}
of bread and\index{Lord's Supper:bread ``f10!} wine\index{Lord's Supper:wine ``f10!}, to represent and\index{Lord's
Supper:elements:represent Christ ``f10!} exhibit Christ as spiritual nourishment\index{Lord's Supper:spiritual
feeding:nourishment ``f10!} to the soul,\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 11:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.   2, pg.
``f30!}3\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}{}-26\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  23-26, pg.
``f30!}.} and to confirm\index{Sacraments:confirm union with Christ ``f10!} our continuance and growth in
him\index{Sanctification:spiritual growth:in Christ ``f10!},\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 10:16\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch. 
10, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}.} and that only to such as are of years and ability to examine themselves\index{Lord's
Supper:preparation:self-examination ``f10!}.\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 11:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.   2, pg.
``f30!}8\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  28, pg. ``f30!}{}-29\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  28-29, pg.
``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 178 \textit{What is prayer}\index{Prayer:defined ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. Prayer is an\index{Prayer:defined ``f10!} offering up of our\index{Prayer:offering desires to God ``f10!} desires
unto God,\footnote{\ Psalm 62:8\index{19 Psalms:ch.  62, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}.} in the name of Christ,\footnote{\ John
16:2\index{43 John:ch.  16, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}3\index{43 John:ch.  16, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}.} by the help of
his\index{Prayer:helped by Holy Spirit ``f10!} Spirit;\footnote{\ Romans 8:2\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   2, pg.
``f30!}6\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.  26, pg. ``f30!}.} with confession\index{Confession:of sin ``f10!} of our
sins,\footnote{\ Psalm 32:5\index{19 Psalms:ch.  32, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}{}-6\index{19 Psalms:ch.  32, v.   5-6, pg.
``f30!}; Daniel 9:4\index{27 Daniel:ch.   9, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.} and thankful\index{Prayer:thanking God ``f10!}
acknowledgment\index{Prayer:acknowledgment of:God's mercies ``f10!} of his mercies\index{God's attributes:merciful
``f10!}.\footnote{\ Philippians 4:6\index{50 Philippians:ch.   4, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip


Q. 179 \textit{Are we to pray unto}\index{Prayer:to God alone ``f10!}\textit{ God only?}

A. God only being able to search the\index{Heart:God alone able to search ``f10!} hearts,\footnote{\ 1 Kings
8:39\index{11 1 Kings:ch.   8, v.  39, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 1:24\index{44 Acts:ch.   1, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}; Romans
8:2\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}7\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.  27, pg. ``f30!}.} hear the
requests\index{Prayer:assurance of being heard ``f10!},\footnote{\ Psalm 65:2\index{19 Psalms:ch.  65, v.   2, pg.
``f30!}.} pardon the\index{Forgiveness:God alone pardons ``f10!} sins,\footnote{\ Micah 7:18\index{33 Micah:ch.   7, v.
 18, pg. ``f30!}.} and fulfil the desires of\index{Prayer:offering desires to God ``f10!} all;\footnote{\ Psalm
145:18\index{19 Psalms:ch. 145, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}{}-19\index{19 Psalms:ch. 145, v.  18-19, pg. ``f30!}.} and only to
be believed in\index{Faith:belief to be in God alone ``f10!},\footnote{\ Romans 10:1\index{45 Romans:ch.  10, v.   1,
pg. ``f30!}4\index{45 Romans:ch.  10, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}.} and worshiped\index{Worship:adoration of God ``f10!} with
religious worship\index{Worship:of God, required of all men ``f10!};\footnote{\ Matthew 4:10\index{40 Matthew:ch.   4,
v.  10, pg. ``f30!}.} prayer, which is a\index{Prayer:act of worship ``f10!} special part thereof,\footnote{\ 1
Corinthians 1:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   1, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}.} is to be made by all to him
alone,\footnote{\ Psalm 50:15\index{19 Psalms:ch.  50, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}.} and to none other.\footnote{\ Romans
10:1\index{45 Romans:ch.  10, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}4\index{45 Romans:ch.  10, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 180 \textit{What is it to pray in the}\index{Prayer:in the name of Christ ``f10!}\textit{ name of Christ?}

A. To pray in the\index{Prayer:in the name of Christ ``f10!} name of Christ is, in obedience\index{God's
law:commandments:obedience:required ``f10!} to his command, and\index{Prayer:commanded ``f10!} in
confidence\index{Prayer:with confidence ``f10!} on his promises\index{Prayer:confidence on God's promises ``f10!}, to
ask mercy for\index{Mercy:prayer for ``f10!} his sake;\footnote{\ John 14:13-14\index{43 John:ch.  14, v.  13-14, pg.
``f30!}; John 16:2\index{43 John:ch.  16, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}4\index{43 John:ch.  16, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}; Daniel
9:17\index{27 Daniel:ch.   9, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}.} not by bare mentioning of his name,\footnote{\ Matthew
7:21\index{40 Matthew:ch.   7, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}.} but by drawing our\index{Prayer:drawing encouragement ``f10!}
encouragement to pray, and our boldness\index{Prayer:with boldness ``f10!}, strength, and hope\index{Prayer:with
strength and hope ``f10!} of acceptance in\index{Prayer:accepted in Christ ``f10!} prayer, from Christ and his
mediation\index{Jesus:mediator:of covenant ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Hebrews 4:14-16\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   4, v.  14-16, pg.
``f30!}; 1 John 5:13\index{62 1 John:ch.   5, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}{}-15\index{62 1 John:ch.   5, v.  13-15, pg.
``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 181 \textit{Why are we to pray in the}\index{Prayer:in the name of Christ ``f10!}\textit{ name of Christ?}

A. The sinfulness of man, and his distance\index{Mankind:great distance between him and God ``f10!} from God by reason
thereof, being so great, as that we can have no access into\index{Believers:access to God only through Christ ``f10!}
his presence without a mediator\index{Jesus:mediator:of covenant ``f10!};\footnote{\ John 14:6\index{43 John:ch.  14,
v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 59:2\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  59, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 3:12\index{49 Ephesians:ch.  
3, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}.} and there being none in heaven\index{Jesus:mediator:only one ``f10!} or earth appointed to, or
fit for, that glorious work\index{Jesus:glorious work ``f10!} but Christ alone,\footnote{\ John 6:27\index{43 John:ch. 
 6, v.  27, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 7:25\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   7, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}{}-27\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   7, v. 
25-27, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Timothy 2:5\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   2, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.} we are to pray in
no\index{Prayer:in the name of Christ ``f10!} other name but his only.\footnote{\ Colossians 3:17\index{51
Colossians:ch.   3, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 13:15\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  13, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 182 \textit{How does the Spirit help us to}\index{Prayer:helped by Holy Spirit ``f10!}\textit{ pray?}

A. We not knowing\index{Prayer:not know what we ought to pray ``f10!}: What to pray for as\index{Prayer:helped by Holy
Spirit ``f10!} we ought, the Spirit helps our infirmities, by\index{Believers:helped in infirmities by the Holy Spirit
``f10!} enabling us\index{Prayer:enabled by Holy Spirit ``f10!} to understand both for whom, and: What, and: How
prayer\index{Prayer:direction for ``f10!} is to be made; and by working and quickening in
our\index{Conversion:quickened to new life ``f10!} hearts (although not in all persons, nor at all times, in the same
measure) those apprehensions, affections, and graces\index{Prayer:right affections ``f10!} which are requisite
for\index{God's law:commandments:duties:required by God ``f10!} the right performance of that duty\index{Prayer:grace
required to perform ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Romans 8:2\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}6\index{45 Romans:ch.  
8, v.  26, pg. ``f30!}{}-27\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.  26-27, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 10:17\index{19 Psalms:ch.  10, v. 
17, pg. ``f30!}; Zechariah 12:10\index{38 Zechariah:ch.  12, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip


\bigskip


Q. 183 \textit{For whom are we to pray}\index{Prayer:for others ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. We are to pray for the\index{Prayer:for whole Church ``f10!} whole church\index{Church:universal ``f10!} of Christ
upon earth;\footnote{\ Ephesians 6:18\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   6, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 28:9\index{19 Psalms:ch. 
28, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}.} for magistrates\index{Civil magistrate:pray for ``f10!},\footnote{\ 1 Timothy 2:1\index{54 1
Timothy:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}{}-2\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   2, v.   1-2, pg. ``f30!}.} and ministers\index{Church
officers:minsters ``f10!};\footnote{\ Colossians 4:3\index{51 Colossians:ch.   4, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}.} for
ourselves,\footnote{\ Genesis 32:11\index{01 Genesis:ch.  32, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}.} our brethren\index{Prayer:for
brothers in Christ ``f10!},\footnote{\ James 5:16\index{59 James:ch.   5, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}.} yea, our
enemies\index{Enemies:believers delivered from ``f10!};\footnote{\ Matthew 5:44\index{40 Matthew:ch.   5, v.  44, pg.
``f30!}.} and for all sorts of men living,\footnote{\ 1 Timothy 2:1\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   2, v.   1, pg.
``f30!}{}-2\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   2, v.   1-2, pg. ``f30!}.} or that shall live hereafter;\footnote{\ John
17:2\index{43 John:ch.  17, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}0\index{43 John:ch.  17, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Samuel 7:29\index{10 2
Samuel:ch.   7, v.  29, pg. ``f30!}.} but not for the dead\index{Prayer:not to be offered for the dead
``f10!},\footnote{\ 2 Samuel 12:21-23\index{10 2 Samuel:ch.  12, v.  21-23, pg. ``f30!}.} nor for those that are known
to have sinned the sin\index{Sin:sinned the sin unto death ``f10!} unto death\index{Death:committed sin unto
``f10!}.\footnote{\ 1 John 5:16\index{62 1 John:ch.   5, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 184 \textit{For what things are we to pray}\index{Prayer:for lawful things ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. We are to pray for all\index{Prayer:for glory of God ``f10!} things tending to the glory of God,\index{Mankind:to
glorify God in thought, word, deed ``f10!}\footnote{\ Matthew 6:9\index{40 Matthew:ch.   6, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}.} the
welfare\index{Prayer:for welfare of the Church ``f10!} of the church,\footnote{\ Psalm 51:1\index{19 Psalms:ch.  51, v.
  1, pg. ``f30!}8\index{19 Psalms:ch.  51, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 122:6\index{19 Psalms:ch. 122, v.   6, pg.
``f30!}.} our own\footnote{\ Matthew 7:1\index{40 Matthew:ch.   7, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}1\index{40 Matthew:ch.   7, v. 
11, pg. ``f30!}.} or others good;\footnote{\ Psalm 125:4\index{19 Psalms:ch. 125, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.} but not for
anything that is unlawful\index{Prayer:not for unlawful ``f10!}.\footnote{\ 1 John 5:14\index{62 1 John:ch.   5, v. 
14, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip


\bigskip


Q. 185 \textit{How are we to pray}\index{Prayer:direction for ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. We are to pray with an\index{Prayer:praising God ``f10!} awful apprehension\index{Prayer:apprehension of God's
majesty ``f10!} of the majesty of God,\footnote{\ Ecclesiastes 5:1\index{21 Ecclesiastes:ch.   5, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}.}
and deep sense of our own unworthiness\index{Prayer:acknowledgment of:deep sense of unworthiness
``f10!},\footnote{\ Genesis 18:27\index{01 Genesis:ch.  18, v.  27, pg. ``f30!}; Genesis 32:10\index{01 Genesis:ch. 
32, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}.} necessities,\index{Prayer:for necessities ``f10!}\footnote{\ Luke 15:17-19\index{42 Luke:ch. 
15, v.  17-19, pg. ``f30!}.} and sins;\footnote{\ Luke 18:1\index{42 Luke:ch.  18, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}3-14\index{42
Luke:ch.  18, v.  13-14, pg. ``f30!}.} with penitent\index{Repentance:penitence ``f10!},\footnote{\ Psalm 51:1\index{19
Psalms:ch.  51, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}7\index{19 Psalms:ch.  51, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}.} thankful\index{Prayer:thanking God
``f10!},\footnote{\ Philippians 4:6\index{50 Philippians:ch.   4, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}.} and enlarged
hearts\index{Prayer:with understanding and faith ``f10!};\footnote{\ 1 Samuel 1:15\index{09 1 Samuel:ch.   1, v.  15,
pg. ``f30!}; 1 Samuel 2:1\index{09 1 Samuel:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}.} with understanding,\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians
14:15\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  14, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}.} faith,\footnote{\ Mark 11:24\index{41 Mark:ch.  11, v.  24,
pg. ``f30!}; James 1:6\index{59 James:ch.   1, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}.} sincerity,\footnote{\ Psalm 17:1\index{19
Psalms:ch.  17, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 145:18\index{19 Psalms:ch. 145, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}.}
fervency\index{Prayer:with fervency ``f10!},\footnote{\ James 5:16\index{59 James:ch.   5, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}.}
love,\footnote{\ 1 Timothy 2:8\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   2, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}.} and perseverance,\index{Prayer:with
perseverance ``f10!}\footnote{\ Ephesians 6:18\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   6, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}.} waiting upon
him,\index{Patience:waiting on God ``f10!}\footnote{\ Micah 7:7\index{33 Micah:ch.   7, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}.} with
humble submission\index{Humility:submission before God ``f10!} to his will.\footnote{\ Matthew 26:39\index{40
Matthew:ch.  26, v.  39, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 186 \textit{What rule has God given for}\index{Prayer:direction for ``f10!}\textit{ our direction in the duty of
prayer}\index{Prayer:duty of ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The whole word of God is of use to direct us in the duty of prayer\index{Prayer:duty of ``f10!};\footnote{\ 1 John
5:14\index{62 1 John:ch.   5, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}.} but the special rule of direction\index{Prayer:direction for
``f10!} is that form of prayer\index{Prayer:Lord's:pattern for our prayers ``f10!} which our Savior\index{Jesus:saviour
of the Church ``f10!} Christ taught his\index{Prayer:Lord's:Jesus taught his disciples ``f10!}
disciples\index{disciples of Jesus ``f10!}, commonly called The Lord's prayer.\footnote{\ Matthew 6:2-13\index{40
Matthew:ch.   6, v.   2-13, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 11:2\index{42 Luke:ch.  11, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}{}-4\index{42 Luke:ch. 
11, v.   2-4, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 187 \textit{How is the Lord's prayer}\index{Prayer:Lord's:pattern for our prayers ``f10!}\textit{ to be used?}

A. The Lord's prayer\index{Prayer:Lord's:pattern for our prayers ``f10!} is not only for
direction\index{Prayer:direction for ``f10!}, as a pattern, according to which we are to make other prayers; but may
also be used as a prayer, so that it be done with understanding\index{Prayer:with understanding and faith ``f10!},
faith, reverence, and other graces\index{Prayer:accompanied by graces ``f10!} necessary to the right performance of the
duty of prayer\index{Prayer:duty of ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Matthew 6:9\index{40 Matthew:ch.   6, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}; Luke
11:2\index{42 Luke:ch.  11, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 188 \textit{Of how many parts does the Lord's prayer}\index{Prayer:Lord's:pattern for our prayers ``f10!}\textit{
consist?}

A. The Lord's prayer\index{Prayer:Lord's:pattern for our prayers ``f10!} consists of three parts; a
preface\index{Prayer:Lord's:preface ``f10!}, petitions\index{Prayer:Lord's:petitions:petitions ``f10!}, and a
conclusion\index{Prayer:Lord's:conclusion ``f10!}.


\bigskip

Q. 189 \textit{What does the preface of}\index{Prayer:Lord's:preface ``f10!}\textit{ the Lord's
prayer}\index{Prayer:Lord's:pattern for our prayers ``f10!}\textit{ teach us?}

A. The preface of\index{Prayer:Lord's:preface ``f10!} the Lord's prayer\index{Prayer:Lord's:pattern for our prayers
``f10!} (contained in these words, Our Father\index{Father:God the ``f10!} which art in heaven\index{Heaven:God's abode
``f10!},)\footnote{\ Matthew 6:9\index{40 Matthew:ch.   6, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}.} teaches us, when we pray, to draw
near\index{Prayer:draw near to God ``f10!} to God with confidence\index{Prayer:with confidence ``f10!} of his fatherly
goodness\index{God's attributes:goodness ``f10!}, and our interest therein\index{Prayer:acknowledgment of:interest
(share) in God as Father ``f10!};\footnote{\ Luke 11:13\index{42 Luke:ch.  11, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 8:1\index{45
Romans:ch.   8, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}5\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}.} with reverence, and
all\index{Prayer:with reverence ``f10!} other childlike\index{Love toward God:childlike ``f10!}
dispositions,\footnote{\ Isaiah 64:9\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  64, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}.} heavenly
affections,\footnote{\ Psalm 123:1\index{19 Psalms:ch. 123, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}; Lamentations 3:41\index{25
Lamentations:ch.   3, v.  41, pg. ``f30!}.} and due\index{Worship:affections directed to God ``f10!} apprehensions of
his sovereign\index{God's attributes:sovereign lordship ``f10!} power, majesty, and\index{Prayer:apprehension of God's
majesty ``f10!} gracious\index{Grace:God's free ``f10!} condescension\index{God's attributes:condescension, voluntary
``f10!}:\footnote{\ Isaiah 63:15-16\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  63, v.  15-16, pg. ``f30!}; Nehemiah 1:4\index{16 Nehemiah:ch.
  1, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}{}-6\index{16 Nehemiah:ch.   1, v.   4-6, pg. ``f30!}.} as also, to pray with
an\index{Prayer:praising God ``f10!}d\index{Prayer:for others ``f10!} for others.\footnote{\ Acts 12:5\index{44
Acts:ch.  12, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 190 \textit{What do we pray for in}\index{Prayer:Lord's:petitions:items to pray for ``f10!}\textit{ the first
petition}\index{Prayer:Lord's:petitions:first ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. In the first petition\index{Prayer:Lord's:petitions:first ``f10!} (which is, Hallowed\index{God's name:hallowed
``f10!} be thy name,)\footnote{\ Matthew 6:9\index{40 Matthew:ch.   6, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}.} acknowledging the
utter\index{Prayer:acknowledgment of:inability to honour God rightly ``f10!} inability\index{Prayer:acknowledgment
of:reliance on God ``f10!} and indisposition\index{Prayer:acknowledgment of:indisposition ``f10!} that is in ourselves
and all men to honor God\index{Mankind:to honor God ``f10!} aright\index{Sin:original:inability to:honour God rightly
``f10!},\footnote{\ 2 Corinthians 3:5\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   3, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 51:1\index{19
Psalms:ch.  51, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}5\index{19 Psalms:ch.  51, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}.} pray,
that\index{Prayer:Lord's:petitions:items to pray for ``f10!} God would by his grace\index{Grace:God's free ``f10!}
enable and\index{Worship:correct:enabled by Holy Spirit ``f10!} incline us and others to know, to acknowledge,
and\index{Worship:acknowledge God ``f10!} highly to esteem him\index{Worship:esteem God ``f10!},\footnote{\ Psalm
67:2-3\index{19 Psalms:ch.  67, v.   2-3, pg. ``f30!}.} his titles\index{God's name:titles to be honoured
``f10!},\footnote{\ Psalm 83:18\index{19 Psalms:ch.  83, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}.} attributes\index{God's attributes:to
be:revered ``f10!},\footnote{\ Psalm 86:10-13, 15\index{19 Psalms:ch.  86, v.  10-13, 15, pg. ``f30!}.} ordinances,
word\index{Worship:ordinances:to be:esteemed ``f10!},\footnote{\ 2 Thessalonians 3:1\index{53 2 Thessalonians:ch.   3,
v.   1, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 138:1-3\index{19 Psalms:ch. 138, v.   1-3, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 147:19-20\index{19 Psalms:ch.
147, v.  19-20, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Corinthians 2:14-15\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   2, v.  14-15, pg. ``f30!}.} works, and
whatsoever\index{Providence:God's works ``f10!} he is pleased\index{Providence:at God's pleasure ``f10!} to make
himself known by;\footnote{\ Psalm 8; Psalm 145.} and to glorify\index{Worship:glorifying God ``f10!} him in
thought\index{God's name:to be used:reverently in thoughts and words ``f10!}, word,\footnote{\ Psalm 19:14\index{19
Psalms:ch.  19, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 103:1\index{19 Psalms:ch. 103, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}.} and
deed:\index{Mankind:to glorify God in thought, word, deed ``f10!}\footnote{\ Philippians 1:9, 11\index{50
Philippians:ch.   1, v.   9, 11, pg. ``f30!}.} that he would prevent and\index{Prayer:that God would prevent and remove
atheism ``f10!} remove atheism\index{atheism ``f10!},\footnote{\ Psalm 67:1-4\index{19 Psalms:ch.  67, v.   1-4, pg.
``f30!}.} ignorance\index{ignorance ``f10!},\footnote{\ Ephesians 1:1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   1, pg.
``f30!}7-18\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.  17-18, pg. ``f30!}.} idolatry\index{Idolatry:idolatry
``f10!},\footnote{\ Psalm 97:7\index{19 Psalms:ch.  97, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}.} profaneness\index{God's name:not to
be:profaned ``f10!},\footnote{\ Psalm 74:18, 22-23\index{19 Psalms:ch.  74, v.  18, 22-23, pg. ``f30!}.} and:
whatsoever is dishonorable\index{Prayer:for removal of all that is dishonorable to God ``f10!} to him;\footnote{\ 2
Kings 19:15-16\index{12 2 Kings:ch.  19, v.  15-16, pg. ``f30!}.} and, by his overruling\index{Providence:overruling
``f10!} providence\index{Providence:providence ``f10!}, direct and dispose of\index{Providence:God disposes all things
for his glory ``f10!} all things to his own glory\index{God's attributes:glory:his own ``f10!}.\footnote{\ 2 Chronicles
20:6, 10-12\index{14 2 Chronicles:ch.  20, v.   6, 10-12, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 83; Psalm 140:4, 8\index{19 Psalms:ch.
140, v.   4, 8, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 191 \textit{What do we pray for in}\index{Prayer:Lord's:petitions:items to pray for ``f10!}\textit{ the second
petition}\index{Prayer:Lord's:petitions:second ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. In the second petition\index{Prayer:Lord's:petitions:second ``f10!} (which is, Thy kingdom come\index{Kingdom of
God:prayer for advancement ``f10!},)\footnote{\ Matthew 6:1\index{40 Matthew:ch.   6, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}0\index{40

mankind to be\index{Sin:original:all mankind descending from Adam ``f10!} by nature under the dominion of

``f10!},\footnote{\ Ephesians 2:2\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}{}-3\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.  
2-3, pg. ``f30!}.} we pray, that\index{Prayer:Lord's:petitions:items to pray for ``f10!} the kingdom of

``f10!},\footnote{\ Psalm 68:1, 18\index{19 Psalms:ch.  68, v.   1, 18, pg. ``f30!}; Revelation 12:10-11\index{66
Revelation:ch.  12, v.  10-11, pg. ``f30!}.} the gospel\index{Gospel:gospel ``f10!} propagated\index{Gospel:to all

``f30!}.} the Jews called\index{Jews:called ``f10!},\footnote{\ Romans 10:1\index{45 Romans:ch.  10, v.   1, pg.
``f30!}.} the fulness of the\index{Gentiles:fulness of ``f10!} Gentiles\index{Gentiles:called ``f10!} brought
in;\footnote{\ John 17:9\index{43 John:ch.  17, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}, 20\index{43 John:ch.  17, v.   9, 20, pg. ``f30!};
Romans 11:25-26\index{45 Romans:ch.  11, v.  25-26, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 67.} the church
furnished\index{Church:institution ``f10!} with all gospel officers\index{Church officers:officers ``f10!} and
ordinances,\footnote{\ Matthew 9:38\index{40 Matthew:ch.   9, v.  38, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Thessalonians 3:1\index{53 2
Thessalonians:ch.   3, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}.} purged from corruption\index{Prayer:for Church ``f10!},\footnote{\ Malachi
1:11\index{39 Malachi:ch.   1, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}; Zephaniah 3:9\index{36 Zephaniah:ch.   3, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}.}
countenanced\index{Civil magistrate:to support Church ``f10!} and maintained by the civil magistrate:\index{Civil

1, pg. ``f30!}{}-2\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   2, v.   1-2, pg. ``f30!}.} that the ordinances of Christ may be purely
dispensed, and\index{Prayer:for ordinances to be dispensed purely ``f10!} made effectual to the
converting\index{Conversion:conversion ``f10!} of those that are yet in their sins, and the confirming\index{Love for
others:confirming ``f10!}, comforting\index{Love for others:comforting others ``f10!}, and building up\index{Holy
Spirit:builds up the elect ``f10!} of those that are already converted:\footnote{\ Acts 4:29-30\index{44 Acts:ch.   4,
v.  29-30, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 6:18\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   6, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}{}-20\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   6,
v.  18-20, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 15:29-30, 32\index{45 Romans:ch.  15, v.  29-30, 32, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Thessalonians
1:11\index{53 2 Thessalonians:ch.   1, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Thessalonians 2:16-17\index{53 2 Thessalonians:ch.   2,
v.  16-17, pg. ``f30!}.} that Christ would rule in our hearts here\index{Heart:new:ruled by Jesus
``f10!},\footnote{\ Ephesians 3:14-20\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   3, v.  14-20, pg. ``f30!}.} and
hasten\index{Jesus:return:desire to see hastened ``f10!} the time of his second coming\index{Jesus:second coming
``f10!}, and our reigning\index{Resurrection:believers:reigning with Christ ``f10!} with him
forever:\footnote{\ Revelation 22:20\index{66 Revelation:ch.  22, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}.} and that he would be
pleased\index{Providence:at God's pleasure ``f10!} so to exercise the kingdom of his\index{Kingdom:of Christ ``f10!}
power in all\index{Jesus:almighty power ``f10!} the world, as may best conduce to these ends.\footnote{\ Isaiah
64:1-2\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  64, v.   1-2, pg. ``f30!}; Revelation 4:8\index{66 Revelation:ch.   4, v.   8, pg.
``f30!}{}-11\index{66 Revelation:ch.   4, v.   8-11, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 192 \textit{What do we pray for in}\index{Prayer:Lord's:petitions:items to pray for ``f10!}\textit{ the third
petition}\index{Prayer:Lord's:petitions:third ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. In the third petition\index{Prayer:Lord's:petitions:third ``f10!} (which is, Thy will be done in earth, as it is in
heaven\index{Heaven:God's will done ``f10!},)\footnote{\ Matthew 6:1\index{40 Matthew:ch.   6, v.   1, pg.
``f30!}0\index{40 Matthew:ch.   6, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}.} acknowledging, that by\index{Prayer:acknowledgment of:sin
``f10!} nature we and all men are not only utterly unable\index{Sin:original:utterly unable and unwilling to do will of
God ``f10!} and unwilling to know and do the will of God,\footnote{\ Romans 7:18\index{45 Romans:ch.   7, v.  18, pg.
``f30!}; Job 21:14\index{18 Job:ch.  21, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 2:14\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   2, v. 
14, pg. ``f30!}.} but prone to rebel\index{Scripture:people prone to rebel against ``f10!} against his
word,\footnote{\ Romans 8:7\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}.} to repine\index{Providence:repine and murmur
against ``f10!} and murmur\index{murmuring ``f10!} against his providence\index{Providence:providence
``f10!},\footnote{\ Exodus 17:7\index{02 Exodus:ch.  17, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}; Numbers 14:2\index{04 Numbers:ch.  14, v.
  2, pg. ``f30!}.} and wholly inclined\index{Sin:original:inclined to do evil ``f10!} to do the will of the flesh, and
of the devil\index{Devil:devil ``f10!}:\footnote{\ Ephesians 2:2\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}.} we
pray, that\index{Prayer:Lord's:petitions:items to pray for ``f10!} God would by his Spirit take away from ourselves and
others all blindness\index{blindness, spiritual ``f10!},\footnote{\ Ephesians 1:1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   1,
pg. ``f30!}7-18\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.  17-18, pg. ``f30!}.} weakness,\footnote{\ Ephesians 3:16\index{49
Ephesians:ch.   3, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}.} indisposedness\index{Sin:original:utterly indisposed
``f10!},\footnote{\ Matthew 26:40-41\index{40 Matthew:ch.  26, v.  40-41, pg. ``f30!}.} and perverseness of
heart;\index{Heart:perverse ``f10!}\footnote{\ Jeremiah 31:18\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  31, v.  18, pg.
``f30!}{}-19\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  31, v.  18-19, pg. ``f30!}.} and by his grace\index{Grace:God's free ``f10!} make
us able and willing to know\index{Conversion:renewal of the will ``f10!}, do, and submit\index{Holy Spirit:subdues will
of man ``f10!} to his will in all things,\footnote{\ Psalm 119:1, 8, 35-36\index{19 Psalms:ch. 119, v.   1, 8, 35-36,
pg. ``f30!}; Acts 21:14\index{44 Acts:ch.  21, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}.} with the like humility\index{Humility:before God
``f10!},\footnote{\ Micah 6:8\index{33 Micah:ch.   6, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}.} cheerfulness\index{cheerfulness
``f10!},\footnote{\ Psalm 100:2\index{19 Psalms:ch. 100, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; Job 1:21\index{18 Job:ch.   1, v.  21,
pg. ``f30!}; 2 Samuel 15:25-26\index{10 2 Samuel:ch.  15, v.  25-26, pg. ``f30!}.} faithfulness\index{faithfulness
``f10!},\footnote{\ Isaiah 38:3\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  38, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}.} diligence,\footnote{\ Psalm
119:4-5\index{19 Psalms:ch. 119, v.   4-5, pg. ``f30!}.} zeal,\footnote{\ Romans 12:11\index{45 Romans:ch.  12, v.  11,
pg. ``f30!}.} sincerity,\footnote{\ Psalm 119:80\index{19 Psalms:ch. 119, v.  80, pg. ``f30!}.} and
constancy\index{Believers:desire to obey God ``f10!},\footnote{\ Psalm 119:11\index{19 Psalms:ch. 119, v.  11, pg.
``f30!}2\index{19 Psalms:ch. 119, v. 112, pg. ``f30!}.} as the angels\index{Angels:angels ``f10!} do in
heaven\index{Angels:works in heaven ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Isaiah 6:2-3\index{23 Isaiah:ch.   6, v.   2-3, pg. ``f30!};
Psalm 103:20-21\index{19 Psalms:ch. 103, v.  20-21, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 18:10\index{40 Matthew:ch.  18, v.  10, pg.
``f30!}.}

Q. 193 \textit{What do we pray for in}\index{Prayer:Lord's:petitions:items to pray for ``f10!}\textit{ the fourth
petition}\index{Prayer:Lord's:petitions:fourth ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. In the fourth petition\index{Prayer:Lord's:petitions:fourth ``f10!} (which is, Give us this day our daily
bread\index{Prayer:for daily needs ``f10!},)\footnote{\ Matthew 6:1\index{40 Matthew:ch.   6, v.   1, pg.
``f30!}1\index{40 Matthew:ch.   6, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}.} acknowledging, that in\index{Prayer:acknowledgment of:sin
``f10!} Adam, and by our own sin, we have forfeited\index{Sin:forfeited right to outward blessings in life ``f10!} our
right to all the outward blessings of\index{Material things:temporal blessings ``f10!} this life, and
deserve\index{Sin:deserves damnation ``f10!} to be wholly deprived of them by God, and to have them
cursed\index{Curse:deserved for sin ``f10!} to us in the use of them;\footnote{\ Genesis 2:17\index{01 Genesis:ch.   2,
v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; Genesis 3:17\index{01 Genesis:ch.   3, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 8:2\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.
  2, pg. ``f30!}0\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}{}-22\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.  20-22, pg. ``f30!};
Jeremiah 5:25\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.   5, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}; Deuteronomy 28:15-68\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.  28, v. 
15-68, pg. ``f30!}.} and that neither they of themselves are able to sustain us\index{Worldly:goods cannot sustain us
``f10!},\footnote{\ Deuteronomy 8:3\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.   8, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}.} nor we to
merit,\index{Salvation:not by:merit ``f10!}\footnote{\ Genesis 32:10\index{01 Genesis:ch.  32, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}.} or
by our own industry\index{Salvation:not by:industry ``f10!} to procure them;\footnote{\ Deuteronomy 8:17\index{05
Deuteronomy:ch.   8, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}{}-18\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.   8, v.  17-18, pg. ``f30!}.} but prone to
desire\index{Worldly:desires ``f10!},\footnote{\ Jeremiah 6:13\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.   6, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; Mark
7:21-22\index{41 Mark:ch.   7, v.  21-22, pg. ``f30!}.} get,\footnote{\ Hosea 12:7\index{28 Hosea:ch.  12, v.   7, pg.
``f30!}.} and use them unlawfully\index{Material things:unlawful use ``f10!}:\footnote{\ James 4:3\index{59 James:ch.  
4, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}.} we pray for ourselves\index{Prayer:for ourselves ``f10!} and others, that both they and we,
waiting upon the\index{Patience:waiting on God ``f10!} providence\index{Providence:providence ``f10!} of God from day
to day in the use of lawful means\index{Material things:to be lawfully procured ``f10!}, may, of his free gift,
and\index{Providence:provides good gifts ``f10!} as to his fatherly\index{Father:God the ``f10!} wisdom
shall\index{God's attributes:wisdom ``f10!} seem best, enjoy a competent portion\index{Prayer:for necessities ``f10!}
of them;\footnote{\ Genesis 28:20\index{01 Genesis:ch.  28, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}; Genesis 43:12-14\index{01 Genesis:ch. 
43, v.  12-14, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 4:28\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.  28, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Thessalonians
3:1\index{53 2 Thessalonians:ch.   3, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}1\index{53 2 Thessalonians:ch.   3, v.  11, pg.
``f30!}{}-12\index{53 2 Thessalonians:ch.   3, v.  11-12, pg. ``f30!}; Philippians 4:6\index{50 Philippians:ch.   4, v.
  6, pg. ``f30!}.} and have the same continued and blessed unto us in our holy\index{Believers:holy:being perfected
``f10!} and comfortable use of them,\footnote{\ 2 Timothy 4:3\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   4, v.   3, pg.
``f30!}{}-5\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   4, v.   3-5, pg. ``f30!}.} and contentment\index{contentment ``f10!} in
them;\footnote{\ 1 Timothy 6:6\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   6, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}{}-8\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   6, v.  
6-8, pg. ``f30!}.} and be kept from all things that are contrary to our temporal support\index{Prayer:for temporal
support ``f10!} and comfort.\footnote{\ Proverbs 30:8-9\index{20 Proverbs:ch.  30, v.   8-9, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 194 \textit{What do we pray for in}\index{Prayer:Lord's:petitions:items to pray for ``f10!}\textit{ the fifth
petition}\index{Prayer:Lord's:petitions:fifth ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. In the fifth petition\index{Prayer:Lord's:petitions:fifth ``f10!} (which is, Forgive\index{Forgiveness:beg pardon for
``f10!} us our debts\index{Forgiveness:of debtors ``f10!}, as we forgive our debtors,)\footnote{\ Matthew 6:1\index{40
Matthew:ch.   6, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}2\index{40 Matthew:ch.   6, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}.} acknowledging, that
we\index{Prayer:acknowledgment of:sin ``f10!} and all others are guilty\index{guilt ``f10!} both of original and actual
sin, and thereby become debtors to the justice of God\index{God's attributes:administers justice ``f10!}; and that
neither we, nor any other creature\index{creatures ``f10!}, can make the least satisfaction for
that\index{Jesus:satisfied divine justice ``f10!} debt:\footnote{\ Romans 3:9\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.   9, pg.
``f30!}{}-22\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.   9-22, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 18:24-25\index{40 Matthew:ch.  18, v.  24-25, pg.
``f30!}; Psalm 130:3\index{19 Psalms:ch. 130, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}{}-4\index{19 Psalms:ch. 130, v.   3-4, pg. ``f30!}.}
we pray for ourselves\index{Prayer:for ourselves ``f10!} and others, that God of his free grace\index{Grace:God's free
``f10!} would, through the obedience and\index{Jesus:obedience:imputed to believers ``f10!} satisfaction of Christ,
apprehended\index{Faith:instrument:which applies Christ to believers ``f10!} and applied by faith\index{Faith:in Jesus
Christ ``f10!}, acquit\index{Judgement day:believers:acquitted by God ``f10!} us both from the guilt and
punishment\index{Punishment:of sin ``f10!} of sin,\footnote{\ Romans 3:2\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.   2, pg.
``f30!}4\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}{}-26\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.  24-26, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews
9:22\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   9, v.  22, pg. ``f30!}.} accept us in his Beloved\index{Jesus:beloved of the Father
``f10!};\footnote{\ Ephesians 1:6\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}{}-7\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.  
6-7, pg. ``f30!}.} continue his favor and grace to us,\footnote{\ 2 Peter 1:2\index{61 2 Peter:ch.   1, v.   2, pg.
``f30!}.} pardon our daily failings\index{God's law:broken daily by all men (thought, word, deed)
``f10!},\footnote{\ Hosea 14:2\index{28 Hosea:ch.  14, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; Jeremiah 14:7\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  14, v.
  7, pg. ``f30!}.} and fill us with peace\index{Prayer:for peace and joy ``f10!} and joy, in\index{Joy:in Holy Spirit
``f10!} giving us daily more and more assurance\index{Assurance:of forgiveness ``f10!} of
forgiveness;\footnote{\ Romans 15:13\index{45 Romans:ch.  15, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 51:7-10, 12\index{19
Psalms:ch.  51, v.   7-10, 12, pg. ``f30!}.} which we are the rather emboldened\index{Prayer:with boldness ``f10!} to
ask, and encouraged\index{Prayer:assurance of being heard ``f10!} to expect, when we have this testimony in ourselves,
that we from the heart\index{Forgiveness:from the heart ``f10!} forgive others their offenses\index{Forgiveness:of
offenses ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Luke 11:4\index{42 Luke:ch.  11, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 6:1\index{40 Matthew:ch.  
6, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}4-15\index{40 Matthew:ch.   6, v.  14-15, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 18:35\index{40 Matthew:ch.  18, v.
 35, pg. ``f30!}.}

Q. 195 \textit{What do we pray for in}\index{Prayer:Lord's:petitions:items to pray for ``f10!}\textit{ the sixth
petition}\index{Prayer:Lord's:petitions:sixth ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. In the sixth petition\index{Prayer:Lord's:petitions:sixth ``f10!} (which is, And lead us not into
temptation\index{Temptation:temptation ``f10!}, but deliver us from\index{Salvation:delivered from thraldom to sin
``f10!} evil,)\footnote{\ Matthew 6:1\index{40 Matthew:ch.   6, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}3\index{40 Matthew:ch.   6, v.  13,
pg. ``f30!}.} acknowledging, that the\index{Prayer:acknowledgment of:God's mercies ``f10!} most wise\index{God's
attributes:wisdom ``f10!}, righteous, and gracious\index{Grace:God's free ``f10!} God, for divers holy\index{God's
attributes:holy:ends ``f10!} and just ends, may so order things, that we may be assaulted\index{Temptation:assaults
believers ``f10!}, foiled, and for a time led captive\index{Temptation:captive to ``f10!} by temptations;\footnote{\ 2
Chronicles 32:31\index{14 2 Chronicles:ch.  32, v.  31, pg. ``f30!}.} that Satan,\index{Satan:tempter
``f10!}\footnote{\ 1 Chronicles 21:1\index{13 1 Chronicles:ch.  21, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}.} the world,\footnote{\ Luke
21:34\index{42 Luke:ch.  21, v.  34, pg. ``f30!}; Mark 4:19\index{41 Mark:ch.   4, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}.} and the flesh,
are ready powerfully to draw us\index{Temptation:draws us aside ``f10!} aside, and ensnare\index{Prayer:for freedom
from temptation ``f10!} us;\footnote{\ James 1:14\index{59 James:ch.   1, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}.} and that we, even after
the pardon of our\index{Forgiveness:God alone pardons ``f10!} sins, by reason of our
corruption\index{Sanctification:remnants of corruption remain ``f10!},\footnote{\ Galatians 5:1\index{48 Galatians:ch. 
 5, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}7\index{48 Galatians:ch.   5, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}.} weakness,
and\index{Sanctification:weaknesses and imperfections remain ``f10!} want of watchfulness\index{Temptation:watchfulness
required to avoid ``f10!},\footnote{\ Matthew 26:41\index{40 Matthew:ch.  26, v.  41, pg. ``f30!}.} are not only
subject to be tempted, and forward to expose\index{Temptation:tendency to expose self to ``f10!} ourselves unto
temptations,\footnote{\ Matthew 26:69-72\index{40 Matthew:ch.  26, v.  69-72, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 2:11-14\index{48
Galatians:ch.   2, v.  11-14, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Chronicles 18:3\index{14 2 Chronicles:ch.  18, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}; 2
Chronicles 19:2\index{14 2 Chronicles:ch.  19, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}.} but also of ourselves
unable\index{Temptation:unable and unwilling to resist ``f10!} and unwilling to resist them\index{Temptation:unwilling
to resist ``f10!}, to recover out\index{Temptation:recovery from ``f10!} of them, and to improve
them;\footnote{\ Romans 7:23\index{45 Romans:ch.   7, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}{}-24\index{45 Romans:ch.   7, v.  23-24, pg.
``f30!}; 1 Chronicles 21:1\index{13 1 Chronicles:ch.  21, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}{}-4\index{13 1 Chronicles:ch.  21, v.  
1-4, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Chronicles 16:7-10\index{14 2 Chronicles:ch.  16, v.   7-10, pg. ``f30!}.} and worthy to be left
under the power of them\index{Temptation:under the power of ``f10!}:\footnote{\ Psalm 81:11\index{19 Psalms:ch.  81, v.
 11, pg. ``f30!}{}-12\index{19 Psalms:ch.  81, v.  11-12, pg. ``f30!}.} we pray,
that\index{Prayer:Lord's:petitions:items to pray for ``f10!} God would so overrule\index{Providence:overruling ``f10!}
the world and all in it,\footnote{\ John 17:15\index{43 John:ch.  17, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}.} subdue the\index{Prayer:for
God to subdue the flesh (sin in the world) ``f10!} flesh,\footnote{\ Psalm 51:1\index{19 Psalms:ch.  51, v.   1, pg.
``f30!}0\index{19 Psalms:ch.  51, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 119:133\index{19 Psalms:ch. 119, v. 133, pg. ``f30!}.} and
restrain\index{Prayer:for restraining Satan ``f10!} Satan,\footnote{\ 2 Corinthians 12:7-8\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch. 
12, v.   7-8, pg. ``f30!}.} order all things,\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 10:12-13\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  10, v. 
12-13, pg. ``f30!}.} bestow and bless all\index{Believers:blessed in/by God ``f10!} means of grace\index{Grace:means of
``f10!},\footnote{\ Hebrews 13:20-21\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  13, v.  20-21, pg. ``f30!}.} and quicken us to watchfulness
in the use of them, that we and all his people may by his providence\index{Providence:providence ``f10!} be kept from
being tempted to sin;\footnote{\ Matthew 26:41\index{40 Matthew:ch.  26, v.  41, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 19:13\index{19
Psalms:ch.  19, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}.} or, if tempted, that by his Spirit we may be powerfully supported and\index{Holy
Spirit:strengthens believers against temptation ``f10!} enabled to stand\index{Temptation:enabled to stand by Holy
Spirit ``f10!} in the hour of\index{Temptation:delivery from ``f10!} temptation;\footnote{\ Ephesians 3:14-17\index{49
Ephesians:ch.   3, v.  14-17, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Thessalonians 3:13\index{52 1 Thessalonians:ch.   3, v.  13, pg. ``f30!};
Jude 1:24\index{65 Jude:v.   1, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}.} or when fallen\index{Prayer:when fallen ``f10!}, raised again and
recovered out of it,\footnote{\ Psalm 51:1\index{19 Psalms:ch.  51, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}2\index{19 Psalms:ch.  51, v. 
12, pg. ``f30!}.} and have a sanctified\index{Sanctification:sanctification ``f10!} use and improvement
thereof:\footnote{\ 1 Peter 5:8-10\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   5, v.   8-10, pg. ``f30!}.} that our sanctification and
salvation\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!} may be perfected\index{Sanctification:perfected
``f10!},\footnote{\ 2 Corinthians 13:7, 9\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.  13, v.   7, 9, pg. ``f30!}.} Satan
trodden\index{Satan:trodden under our feet ``f10!} under our feet,\footnote{\ Romans 16:2\index{45 Romans:ch.  16, v.  
2, pg. ``f30!}0\index{45 Romans:ch.  16, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}; Zechariah 3:2\index{38 Zechariah:ch.   3, v.   2, pg.
``f30!}; Luke 22:31-32\index{42 Luke:ch.  22, v.  31-32, pg. ``f30!}.} and we fully freed from sin\index{Prayer:for
freedom from sin ``f10!}, temptation, and all evil\index{Prayer:for deliverance from evil ``f10!},
forever.\footnote{\ John 17:15\index{43 John:ch.  17, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Thessalonians 5:23\index{52 1
Thessalonians:ch.   5, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip


\bigskip

Q. 196 \textit{What does the conclusion}\index{Prayer:Lord's:conclusion ``f10!}\textit{ of the Lord's
prayer}\index{Prayer:Lord's:pattern for our prayers ``f10!}\textit{ teach us?}\footnote{\ Although this
conclusion\index{Prayer:Lord's:conclusion ``f10!} is not found in the oldest yet discovered manuscripts, it is found in
the majority of Byzantine texts, and its content perfectly harmonizes with what is said about the kingdom in Daniel
7:14\index{27 Daniel:ch.   7, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}.}

A. The conclusion\index{Prayer:Lord's:conclusion ``f10!} of the Lord's prayer\index{Prayer:Lord's:pattern for our
prayers ``f10!} (which is, For thine is the kingdom, and the\index{Kingdom of God:prayer ascribing power and glory
``f10!} power, and the glory, forever\index{Prayer:for glory of God ``f10!}. Amen\index{Amen, testimony of our true
desire for God's glory ``f10!}.),\footnote{\ Matthew 6:1\index{40 Matthew:ch.   6, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}3\index{40
Matthew:ch.   6, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}.} teaches us to enforce our\index{Prayer:enforce petitions with arguments ``f10!}
petitions\index{Prayer:Lord's:petitions:petitions ``f10!} with arguments,\footnote{\ Romans 15:30\index{45 Romans:ch. 
15, v.  30, pg. ``f30!}.} which are to be taken, not from any worthiness\index{Prayer:accepted not by worthiness on our
part ``f10!} in ourselves, or in any other creature\index{creatures ``f10!}, but from God;\footnote{\ Daniel
9:4\index{27 Daniel:ch.   9, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}, 7-9, 16-19\index{27 Daniel:ch.   9, v.   4, 7-9, 16-19, pg. ``f30!}.}
and with our prayers\index{Prayer:praising God ``f10!} to join praises,\footnote{\ Philippians 4:6\index{50
Philippians:ch.   4, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}.} ascribing to\index{Worship:praising God ``f10!} God alone eternal
sovereignty\index{God's attributes:sovereign lordship ``f10!}, omnipotency\index{God's attributes:omnipotency ``f10!},
and glorious excellency\index{God's attributes:glory:excellency ``f10!};\footnote{\ 1 Chronicles 29:10-13\index{13 1
Chronicles:ch.  29, v.  10-13, pg. ``f30!}.} in regard whereof, as he is able and willing to help\index{Prayer:helped
by Holy Spirit ``f10!} us,\footnote{\ Ephesians 3:20\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   3, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}{}-21\index{49
Ephesians:ch.   3, v.  20-21, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 11:13\index{42 Luke:ch.  11, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}.} so we by
faith\index{Faith:in prayer ``f10!} are emboldened\index{Prayer:with boldness ``f10!} to plead with him that he
would,\footnote{\ 2 Chronicles 20:6, 11\index{14 2 Chronicles:ch.  20, v.   6, 11, pg. ``f30!}.} and
quietly\index{Prayer:quiet reliance on God ``f10!} to rely upon him, that he will fulfil our\index{Prayer:assurance of
being heard ``f10!} requests.\footnote{\ 2 Chronicles 14:11\index{14 2 Chronicles:ch.  14, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}.} And,
to testify\index{Sacraments:testimony through participation ``f10!} this our desire and\index{Prayer:offering desires
to God ``f10!} assurance, we\index{Assurance:of faith ``f10!} say, Amen.\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 14:16\index{46 1
Corinthians:ch.  14, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; Revelation 22:20\index{66 Revelation:ch.  22, v.  20, pg.
``f30!}{}-21\index{66 Revelation:ch.  22, v.  20-21, pg. ``f30!}.}



\subsubsection[The Westminster Shorter Catechism of 1648]{{The Westminster Shorter Catechism of
1648}}
Q 1. \textit{What is the chief}\index{Mankind:chief end/purpose ``f10!}\textit{ end of man?}

A. Man's chief\index{Mankind:chief end/purpose ``f10!} end is to glorify\index{Worship:glorifying God ``f10!}
God,\footnote{\ Psalm 86:9\index{19 Psalms:ch.  86, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 60:21\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  60, v.  21,
pg. ``f30!}; Romans 11:36\index{45 Romans:ch.  11, v.  36, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 6:20\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  
6, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 10:31\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  10, v.  31, pg. ``f30!}; Revelation
4:11\index{66 Revelation:ch.   4, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}.} and to enjoy him for ever.\footnote{\ Psalm 16:5-11\index{19
Psalms:ch.  16, v.   5-11, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 144:15\index{19 Psalms:ch. 144, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 12:2\index{23
Isaiah:ch.  12, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 2:10\index{42 Luke:ch.   2, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; Philippians 4:4\index{50
Philippians:ch.   4, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}; Revelation 21:3-4\index{66 Revelation:ch.  21, v.   3-4, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 2 \textit{What rule }has \textit{God given to}\index{Scripture:direction for how to glorify God ``f10!}\textit{
direct us how we may glorify}\index{Worship:glorifying God ``f10!}\textit{ and enjoy him?}

A. The Word of God\index{Scripture:word of God:word of God ``f10!}, which is contained in the
Scripture\index{Scripture:word of God:Holy Spirit speaking ``f10!}s of the Old and New Testament\index{Scripture:New
Testament ``f10!}s,\footnote{\ Matthew 19:4\index{40 Matthew:ch.  19, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}{}-5\index{40 Matthew:ch.  19,
v.   4-5, pg. ``f30!} with Genesis 2:24\index{01 Genesis:ch.   2, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 24:27, 44\index{42 Luke:ch.
 24, v.  27, 44, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 2:13\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   2, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians
14:37\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  14, v.  37, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Peter 1:2\index{61 2 Peter:ch.   1, v.   2, pg.
``f30!}0-21\index{61 2 Peter:ch.   1, v.  20-21, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Peter 3:2, 15-16\index{61 2 Peter:ch.   3, v.   2,
15-16, pg. ``f30!}.} is the only rule to direct\index{Scripture:direction for how to glorify God ``f10!} us how we may
glorify\index{Worship:glorifying God ``f10!} and enjoy him.\footnote{\ Deuteronomy 4:2\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.   4, v.
  2, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 19:7\index{19 Psalms:ch.  19, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}{}-11\index{19 Psalms:ch.  19, v.   7-11, pg.
``f30!}; Isaiah 8:20\index{23 Isaiah:ch.   8, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}; John 15:11\index{43 John:ch.  15, v.  11, pg.
``f30!}; John 20:30-31\index{43 John:ch.  20, v.  30-31, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 17:11\index{44 Acts:ch.  17, v.  11, pg.
``f30!}; 2 Timothy 3:15\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   3, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}{}-17\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   3, v.  15-17, pg.
``f30!}; 1 John 1:4\index{62 1 John:ch.   1, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 3 \textit{What do the Scriptures principally}\index{Scripture:principal teaching ``f10!}\textit{ teach?}

A. The Scriptures principally\index{Scripture:principal teaching ``f10!} teach what man is to believe concerning
God,\footnote{\ Genesis 1:1\index{01 Genesis:ch.   1, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}; John 5:39\index{43 John:ch.   5, v.  39, pg.
``f30!}; John 20:31\index{43 John:ch.  20, v.  31, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 10:1\index{45 Romans:ch.  10, v.   1, pg.
``f30!}7\index{45 Romans:ch.  10, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Timothy 3:15\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   3, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}.}
and what duty God\index{God's law:commandments:duties:required by God ``f10!} requires of man.\footnote{\ Deuteronomy
10:12-13\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.  10, v.  12-13, pg. ``f30!}; Joshua 1:8\index{06 Joshua:ch.   1, v.   8, pg. ``f30!};
Psalm 119:105\index{19 Psalms:ch. 119, v. 105, pg. ``f30!}; Micah 6:8\index{33 Micah:ch.   6, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}; 2
Timothy 3:16\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   3, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}{}-17\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   3, v.  16-17, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 4 \textit{What is God?}

A. God is a\index{God's attributes:listed (definition of God) ``f10!} Spirit,\footnote{\ Deuteronomy 4:15-19\index{05
Deuteronomy:ch.   4, v.  15-19, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 24:39\index{42 Luke:ch.  24, v.  39, pg. ``f30!}; John 1:1\index{43
John:ch.   1, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}8\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}; John 4:24\index{43 John:ch.   4, v.  24,
pg. ``f30!}; Acts 17:29\index{44 Acts:ch.  17, v.  29, pg. ``f30!}.} infinite,\footnote{\ 1 Kings 8:27\index{11 1
Kings:ch.   8, v.  27, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 139:7-10\index{19 Psalms:ch. 139, v.   7-10, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm
145:3\index{19 Psalms:ch. 145, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 147:5\index{19 Psalms:ch. 147, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}; Jeremiah
23:24\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  23, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 11:33\index{45 Romans:ch.  11, v.  33, pg.
``f30!}{}-36\index{45 Romans:ch.  11, v.  33-36, pg. ``f30!}.} eternal,\index{God's attributes:eternal
``f10!}\footnote{\ Deuteronomy 33:27\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.  33, v.  27, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 90:2\index{19 Psalms:ch. 
90, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 102:12, 24-27\index{19 Psalms:ch. 102, v.  12, 24-27, pg. ``f30!}; Revelation 1:4,
8\index{66 Revelation:ch.   1, v.   4, 8, pg. ``f30!}.} and unchangeable\index{God's attributes:unchangeable
``f10!},\footnote{\ Psalm 33:11\index{19 Psalms:ch.  33, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}; Malachi 3:6\index{39 Malachi:ch.   3, v. 
 6, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 1:1\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   1, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}2\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   1, v.  12, pg.
``f30!}; Hebrews 6:17\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   6, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}{}-18\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   6, v.  17-18, pg.
``f30!}; Hebrews 13:8\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  13, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}; James 1:17\index{59 James:ch.   1, v.  17, pg.
``f30!}.} in his being,\footnote{\ Exodus 3:14\index{02 Exodus:ch.   3, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 115:2-3\index{19
Psalms:ch. 115, v.   2-3, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Timothy 1:17\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   1, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Timothy
6:1\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   6, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}5\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   6, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}{}-16\index{54 1
Timothy:ch.   6, v.  15-16, pg. ``f30!}.} wisdom,\footnote{\ Psalm 104:24\index{19 Psalms:ch. 104, v.  24, pg. ``f30!};
Romans 11:33\index{45 Romans:ch.  11, v.  33, pg. ``f30!}{}-34\index{45 Romans:ch.  11, v.  33-34, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews
4:13\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   4, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 3:2\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}0\index{62 1
