\bigskip

Q. 5 \textit{Are }there\textit{ }more\textit{ Gods than one?}

A. There is but one only,\footnote{\ Deuteronomy 6:4\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.   6, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah
44:6\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  44, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 45:21-22\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  45, v.  21-22, pg. ``f30!}; 1
Corinthians 8:4-6\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   8, v.   4-6, pg. ``f30!}.} the living and true God .\footnote{\ Jeremiah
10:10\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  10, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; John 17:3\index{43 John:ch.  17, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}; 1
Thessalonians 1:9\index{52 1 Thessalonians:ch.   1, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 5:20\index{62 1 John:ch.   5, v.  20,
pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip


\bigskip

Q. 6 \textit{How many persons}\index{God's attributes:trinity:three persons ``f10!}\textit{ are there in the
Godhead}\index{God's attributes:Godhead ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. There are three persons\index{God's attributes:trinity:three persons ``f10!} in the Godhead\index{God's
attributes:Godhead ``f10!}; the Father\index{Father:God the ``f10!}, the Son\index{Jesus:Son of God ``f10!}, and the
Holy Ghost\index{Holy Spirit:Holy Ghost ``f10!};\footnote{\ Matthew 3:16-17\index{40 Matthew:ch.   3, v.  16-17, pg.
``f30!}; Matthew 28:19\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Corinthians 13:1\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch. 
13, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}4\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.  13, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Peter 1:2\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   1, v. 
 2, pg. ``f30!}.} and these three are one God, the same in substance\index{God's attributes:trinity:one substance
``f10!}, equal in power and glory\index{God's attributes:trinity:persons equal ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Psalm 45:6\index{19
Psalms:ch.  45, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; John 1:1\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}; John 17:5\index{43 John:ch. 
17, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 5:3\index{44 Acts:ch.   5, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}{}-4\index{44 Acts:ch.   5, v.   3-4, pg.
``f30!}; Romans 9:5\index{45 Romans:ch.   9, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}; Colossians 2:9\index{51 Colossians:ch.   2, v.   9,
pg. ``f30!}; \textrm{sundry judicial laws} \par Jude 24\index{65 Jude:v.  24, pg. ``f30!}{}-25\index{65 Jude:v. 24-25,
pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 7 \textit{What }are\textit{ the decrees}\index{Predestination:eternal decrees ``f10!}\textit{ of God?}

A. The decrees\index{Predestination:eternal decrees ``f10!} of God are, his eternal purpose\index{Predestination:eternal
purpose ``f10!}, according to the counsel of his\index{Causation:God's own will ``f10!} will, whereby, for his own
glory\index{God's attributes:glory:his own ``f10!}, he has foreordained\index{Predestination:fore-ordination ``f10!}
whatsoever comes to pass.\footnote{\ Psalm 33:11\index{19 Psalms:ch.  33, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 14:24\index{23
Isaiah:ch.  14, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 2:23\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 1:1\index{49
Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}{}-12\index{49 Ephesians:ch.  
1, v.  11-12, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 8 \textit{How does God execute his decrees}\index{Predestination:eternal decrees ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. God executes his decrees\index{Predestination:eternal decrees ``f10!} in the works of creation\index{God's
attributes:creator:works of ``f10!} and providence\index{Providence:providence ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Psalm 148:8\index{19
Psalms:ch. 148, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 40:26\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  40, v.  26, pg. ``f30!}; Daniel 4:35\index{27
Daniel:ch.   4, v.  35, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 4:24-28\index{44 Acts:ch.   4, v.  24-28, pg. ``f30!}; Revelation
4:11\index{66 Revelation:ch.   4, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 9 What\textit{ is the work of creation}\index{God's attributes:creator:works of ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The work of creation\index{God's attributes:creator:works of ``f10!} is, God's making all things of nothing, by the
word of his power\index{Creation:by word of God's power ``f10!},\footnote{\ Genesis 1:1\index{01 Genesis:ch.   1, v.  
1, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 33:6, 9\index{19 Psalms:ch.  33, v.   6, 9, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 11:3\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  11,
v.   3, pg. ``f30!}.} in the space of six\index{Creation:in six days ``f10!} days, and all very
good.\footnote{\ Genesis 1:31\index{01 Genesis:ch.   1, v.  31, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 10 \textit{How did God create man}\index{Mankind:created:by God ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. God created man\index{Mankind:created:by God ``f10!} male\index{Mankind:male and female ``f10!} and
female\index{Mankind:created:male and female ``f10!}, after his own image\index{Mankind:image of God ``f10!}
[a],\footnote{\ Genesis 1:2\index{01 Genesis:ch.   1, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}7\index{01 Genesis:ch.   1, v.  27, pg.
``f30!}.} in knowledge,\footnote{\ Colossians 3:10\index{51 Colossians:ch.   3, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}.} righteousness,
and holiness,\index{Mankind:created:holy ``f10!}\footnote{\ Ephesians 4:24\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.  24, pg.
``f30!}.} with dominion over the\index{Mankind:dominion over creation ``f10!} creatures\index{creatures
``f10!}.\footnote{\ Genesis 1:2\index{01 Genesis:ch.   1, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}8\index{01 Genesis:ch.   1, v.  28, pg.
``f30!}; Psalm 8.}


\bigskip

Q. 11 \textit{What }are\textit{ God's works}\index{Providence:God's works ``f10!}\textit{ of
providence}\index{Providence:providence ``f10!}\textit{?} 

A. God's works of providence\index{Providence:providence ``f10!} are, his most holy\index{God's attributes:holy:most
``f10!},\footnote{\ Psalm 145:17\index{19 Psalms:ch. 145, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}.} wise,\footnote{\ Psalm 104:24\index{19

``f30!}.} preserving\footnote{\ Nehemiah 9:6\index{16 Nehemiah:ch.   9, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}.} and

``f30!}9\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}{}-22\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.  19-22, pg. ``f30!}.} all

30, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 12 \textit{What special act of providence}\index{Providence:providence ``f10!}\textit{ did God exercise toward man in
the estate wherein}\index{Mankind:created:state of innocence ``f10!}\textit{ he was
created}\index{Mankind:created:state ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. When God had created man\index{Mankind:created:by God ``f10!}, he entered into a covenant of life\index{Covenant:life
``f10!} with him, upon condition\index{Covenant:works:conditional on perfect obedience ``f10!} of perfect
obedience\index{Jesus:obedience:to God's law ``f10!}; forbidding\index{God's law:commandments:given to Adam ``f10!} him
to eat of the tree of the\index{Tree:of the knowledge of good and evil ``f10!} knowledge of good and evil, upon pain of
death\index{Death:punishment for sin ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Genesis 2:16-17\index{01 Genesis:ch.   2, v.  16-17, pg.
``f30!}; James 2:10\index{59 James:ch.   2, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 13 \textit{Did our first parents}\index{Parents:first, sinned against God ``f10!}\textit{ continue in the estate
wherein}\index{Mankind:created:state of innocence ``f10!}\textit{ they were created}\index{Mankind:created:state
``f10!}\textit{?}

of creatures:free ``f10!} their own will, fell\index{Sin:original:all mankind descending from Adam ``f10!} from the

\bigskip

Q. 14 \textit{What is sin?}

A. Sin is\index{Sin:defined ``f10!} any want of conformity unto, or transgression of\index{God's
law:commandments:transgressions ``f10!}, the law of God.\footnote{\ Leviticus 5:1\index{03 Leviticus:ch.   5, v.   1,
pg. ``f30!}7\index{03 Leviticus:ch.   5, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; James 4:17\index{59 James:ch.   4, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; 1
John 3:4\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 15 \textit{What was the sin whereby our first parents}\index{Parents:first, sinned against God ``f10!}\textit{
fell}\index{Sin:original:all mankind descending from Adam ``f10!}\textit{ from the estate wherein they were

descending from Adam ``f10!} from the estate wherein thy were created\index{Mankind:created:state ``f10!}, was their

Genesis:ch.   3, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}.}

``f30!}{}-21\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.  12-21, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 15:22\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  15, v.

Q. 18 \textit{Wherein consists the sinfulness of that estate whereinto}\index{Sin:original:an estate of sin and misery
``f10!}\textit{ man fell}\index{Sin:original:all mankind descending from Adam ``f10!}\textit{?}

``f30!}, 19\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.  12, 19, pg. ``f30!}.} the want of original

3, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; Colossians 3:10\index{51 Colossians:ch.   3, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 4:24\index{49
Ephesians:ch.   4, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}.} and the corruption of his\index{Sin:original:corrupt nature:whole ``f10!}
whole nature,\footnote{\ Psalm 51:5\index{19 Psalms:ch.  51, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}; John 3:6\index{43 John:ch.   3, v.  
6, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 3:18\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 8:7\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   7,

``f30!}.} which is commonly called original sin; together with all actual transgressions\index{God's
law:commandments:transgressions ``f10!} which proceed from it\index{Sin:original:proceeds all transgressions
``f10!}.\footnote{\ Genesis 6:5\index{01 Genesis:ch.   6, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 53:1-3\index{19 Psalms:ch.  53, v.
  1-3, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 15:19\index{40 Matthew:ch.  15, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 3:10\index{45 Romans:ch.   3,
v.  10, pg. ``f30!}{}-18, 23\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.  10-18, 23, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 5:1\index{48 Galatians:ch. 
 5, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}9\index{48 Galatians:ch.   5, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}{}-21\index{48 Galatians:ch.   5, v.  19-21,
pg. ``f30!}; James 1:14\index{59 James:ch.   1, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}{}-15\index{59 James:ch.   1, v.  14-15, pg.
``f30!}.}

Q. 19 \textit{What is the misery}\index{Punishment:misery ``f10!}\textit{ of that estate

``f30!}.} are under his wrath\footnote{\ John 3:3\index{43 John:ch.   3, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}6\index{43 John:ch.   3, v.
 36, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 1:18\index{45 Romans:ch.   1, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 2:3\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2,
v.   3, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 5:6\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   5, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}.} and curse,\index{Curse:of God
``f10!}\footnote{\ Galatians 3:10\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; Revelation 22:3\index{66
Revelation:ch.  22, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}.} and so made liable\index{Sin:original:liable to all miseries ``f10!} to all
miseries\index{Punishment:misery ``f10!} in this life,\footnote{\ Genesis 3:16-19\index{01 Genesis:ch.   3, v.  16-19,

``f10!}\footnote{\ Ezekiel 18:4\index{26 Ezekiel:ch.  18, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 5:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.

\bigskip

Q. 20 \textit{Did God leave all mankind}\index{Mankind:not all left to perish in sin and misery ``f10!}\textit{ to
perish}\index{Redemption:not all perish ``f10!}\textit{ in the estate of sin}\index{Sin:original:an estate of sin and
misery ``f10!}\textit{ and misery}\index{Punishment:misery ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. God having, out of his mere good pleasure\index{Providence:at God's pleasure ``f10!}, from all eternity\index{God's
attributes:eternal ``f10!}, elected some to\index{Election:chosen by God ``f10!} everlasting life\index{everlasting
life ``f10!},\footnote{\ Acts 13:48\index{44 Acts:ch.  13, v.  48, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 1:4\index{49 Ephesians:ch.  
1, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}{}-5\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   4-5, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Thessalonians 2:13\index{53 2
Thessalonians:ch.   2, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}{}-14\index{53 2 Thessalonians:ch.   2, v.  13-14, pg. ``f30!}.} did enter
into a covenant of grace\index{Covenant:grace:grace ``f10!}, to deliver them\index{Salvation:delivered from thraldom to
sin ``f10!} out of the estate\index{Sin:original:an estate of sin and misery ``f10!} of sin and
misery\index{Punishment:misery ``f10!}, and to bring them into an estate of salvation\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus
by faith ``f10!} by a Redeemer\index{Jesus:redeemer of God's elect ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Genesis 3:15\index{01
Genesis:ch.   3, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}; Genesis 17:7\index{01 Genesis:ch.  17, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}; Exodus 19:5\index{02
Exodus:ch.  19, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}{}-6\index{02 Exodus:ch.  19, v.   5-6, pg. ``f30!}; Jeremiah 31:3\index{24
Jeremiah:ch.  31, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}1-34\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  31, v.  31-34, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 20:28\index{40
Matthew:ch.  20, v.  28, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 11:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}5\index{46
1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 9:15\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   9, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}.}

the Lord Jesus Christ,\footnote{\ John 14:6\index{43 John:ch.  14, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 4:12\index{44 Acts:ch.

``f30!}8\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}.} became man,\footnote{\ Isaiah 9:6\index{23 Isaiah:ch.   9, v.

Q. 22 \textit{How did Christ, being the Son}\index{Jesus:Son of God ``f10!}\textit{ of God, become man?}

A. Christ, the Son\index{Jesus:Son of God ``f10!} of God, became man, by taking to himself a true body, and a
reasonable\index{Jesus:human nature:reasonable soul ``f10!} soul,\footnote{\ Philippians 2:7\index{50 Philippians:ch.  
2, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 2:1\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}4\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   2, v.  14,
pg. ``f30!}, 17\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   2, v.  14, 17, pg. ``f30!}.} being conceived by\index{Jesus:conceived:by the
power of the Holy Spirit ``f10!} the power of the Holy Ghost\index{Holy Spirit:Holy Ghost ``f10!}, in the
womb\index{Jesus:conceived:in womb of virgin Mary ``f10!} of the virgin\index{Jesus:born of virgin Mary ``f10!}
Mary\index{Mary, mother of Jesus ``f10!}, and born of her,\footnote{\ Luke 1:27, 31, 35\index{42 Luke:ch.   1, v.  27,
31, 35, pg. ``f30!}.} yet without sin.\footnote{\ 2 Corinthians 5:21\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   5, v.  21, pg.
``f30!}; Hebrews 4:15\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   4, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 7:26\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   7, v.  26, pg.
``f30!}; 1 John 3:5\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.}

``f10!} us to God;\footnote{\ Romans 5:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}0-11\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.

``f30!}; Hebrews 1:3\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   1, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}.} of God the Father\index{Father:God the ``f10!},
and in coming to judge the\index{Jesus:judge:world ``f10!} world at the last day\index{Last day:last day
``f10!}.\footnote{\ Matthew 16:27\index{40 Matthew:ch.  16, v.  27, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 17:31\index{44 Acts:ch.  17, v.

``f10!} to us the redemption purchased\index{Redemption:purchased by Christ ``f10!} by Christ, by

``f30!}.} and thereby uniting\index{Believers:union with Christ:mystical ``f10!} us to Christ in our effectual
calling\index{Effectual call:calling ``f10!}.\footnote{\ John 15:5\index{43 John:ch.  15, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}; 1
Corinthians 1:9\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   1, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 3:17\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   3, v.  17,
pg. ``f30!}.}

Q. 31 \textit{What is effectual calling}\index{Effectual call:calling ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. Effectual\index{Effectual call:calling ``f10!} calling is the work of God's Spirit\index{Holy Spirit:God's Spirit
``f10!}, whereby, convincing us\index{Effectual call:convincing of sin and misery ``f10!} of our sin and
misery\index{Punishment:misery ``f10!}, enlightening\index{Effectual call:enlightening minds spiritually ``f10!} our
minds in the knowledge of Christ\index{Effectual call:knowledge of Christ given ``f10!},\footnote{\ Acts 26:18\index{44
Acts:ch.  26, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 2:10, 12\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   2, v.  10, 12, pg. ``f30!}; 2
Corinthians 4:6\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   4, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 1:1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   1,
pg. ``f30!}7-18\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.  17-18, pg. ``f30!}.} and renewing our\index{Conversion:renewed by Holy
Spirit ``f10!} wills,\footnote{\ Deuteronomy 30:6\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.  30, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; Ezekiel
36:26\index{26 Ezekiel:ch.  36, v.  26, pg. ``f30!}{}-27\index{26 Ezekiel:ch.  36, v.  26-27, pg. ``f30!}; John
3:5\index{43 John:ch.   3, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}; Titus 3:5\index{56 Titus:ch.   3, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.} he does

v.  44, pg. ``f30!}{}-45\index{43 John:ch.   6, v.  44-45, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 16:14\index{44 Acts:ch.  16, v.  14, pg.
``f30!}.} freely offered\index{Salvation:freely offered ``f10!} to us in the gospel\index{Gospel:gospel
``f10!}.\footnote{\ Isaiah 45:22\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  45, v.  22, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 11:28\index{40 Matthew:ch.  11,
v.  28, pg. ``f30!}{}-30\index{40 Matthew:ch.  11, v.  28-30, pg. ``f30!}; Revelation 22:17\index{66 Revelation:ch. 
22, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 32 \textit{What }benefits\textit{ do the}\index{Believers:benefits:as members of the Church
``f10!}\textit{y}\index{Believers:benefits:in this life ``f10!}\textit{ that are effectually called}\index{Effectual
call:calling ``f10!}\textit{ partake of in}\index{Effectual call:benefits in this life ``f10!}\textit{ this life?}

A. They that are effectually called\index{Effectual call:calling ``f10!} do in this life partake\index{Effectual
call:benefits in this life ``f10!} of justification\index{Justification:justification ``f10!},
